## 旧(舊)梦(夢)
---
## old dream; past experience
### jiùmèng
---
- **traditional:** 舊夢
- **definition:** old dream; past experience
- **pinyin:** jiùmèng
- **components:**
  - 旧(舊)
    - jiù
    - old; past; former
  - 梦(夢)
    - mèng
    - dream; vision; illusion; aspiration
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** compound word
  - **description:** 舊 (jiù, "old; past") represents something that belongs to a previous time or period. 夢 (mèng, "dream") refers to visions or experiences during sleep, and by extension, can refer to aspirations or past endeavors.
  - **interpretation:** 舊 (jiù, "old; past") conveys the sense of something that is no longer current, tying to the previous experiences or times. 夢 (mèng, "dream") connects to the experiences or aspirations that one may recall or reflect upon. Together, 舊夢 (jiùmèng) signifies a nostalgic recollection of past dreams or experiences, the old dreams that linger in memory, embodying both literal dreams and metaphorical longings or past aspirations.
- **examples:**
  - 有时(時)听(聽)到老歌，我会(會)想起某些旧(舊)梦(夢)。
    - Yǒushí tīngdào lǎo gē, wǒ huì xiǎngqǐ mǒuxiē jiùmèng.
    - Sometimes when I hear old songs, I think of certain past experiences.
  - 他的小说(說)常常写(寫)到旧(舊)梦(夢)。
    - Tā de xiǎoshuō chángcháng xiě dào jiùmèng.
    - His novels often describe old dreams.
  - 在那个(個)地方，他重温(溫)了一段旧(舊)梦(夢)。
    - Zài nàgè dìfāng, tā chóngwēnle yī duàn jiùmèng.
    - In that place, he relived a part of his past experiences.
### 旧(舊)梦(夢) → 旧(舊)
- **traditional:** 舊
- **definition:** old; past; former
- **pinyin:** jiù
- **components:**
  - 雈
    - huán
    - owl
  - 臼
    - jiù
    - mortar
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic 雈 (huán, 'owl') + phonetic 臼 (jiù) ->
    - originally 'a type of owl', borrowed for phonetic similarity to 'old'
  - **interpretation:** The character 舊 (jiù, 'old') combines the semantic component 雈 (huán, 'owl') with the phonetic component 臼 (jiù, 'mortar'). It was initially used to represent a type of owl, which was later borrowed for its sound to denote 'old', associating the unchanging nature of the owl with the concept of 'oldness' or the passage of time.
  - **simplification:** 旧 is the simplified form, reducing complexity from 舊 by removing the semantic component 雈 (huán, 'owl') while preserving the sound with 臼 (jiù).
- **examples:**
  - 这(這)本书(書)很旧(舊)。
    - Zhè běn shū hěn jiù.
    - This book is very old.
  - 他穿着(著)旧(舊)衬(襯)衫，看起来(來)有些疲倦。
    - Tā chuānzhe jiù chènshān, kàn qǐlái yǒu xiē píjuàn.
    - He is wearing a worn shirt and looks a bit tired.
  - 她时(時)常怀(懷)念过(過)去的旧(舊)时(時)光。
    - Tā shícháng huáiniàn guòqù de jiù shíguāng.
    - She often reminisces about the old times.
### 旧(舊)梦(夢) → 旧(舊) → 雈
- **definition:** owl
- **pinyin:** huán
- **components:**
  - 雚
    - guàn
    - type of bird
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts an owl, similar to 雚 (guàn, "type of bird")
  - **interpretation:** The character 雈 (huán, "owl") is a pictogram depicting the silhouette or characteristics of an owl. Historically, it is visually similar to 雚 (guàn, "type of bird"), emphasizing its avian nature. This is a direct representation of the creature it denotes.
### 旧(舊)梦(夢) → 旧(舊) → 雈 → 雚
- **definition:** type of bird
- **pinyin:** guàn
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Originally depicted a stork ->
    - additional component 吅 (xūn) suggests vocalization ->
    - final form 雚 (guān, "cry of waterfowl")
  - **interpretation:** The character 雚 (guān) originally depicted a stork and was a pictogram. Over time, it evolved with the addition of 吅 (xūn) to indicate the vocalization of the bird, becoming associated with the cry of waterfowl.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 雚](@media/glyph96da.png)
### 旧(舊)梦(夢) → 旧(舊) → 臼
- **definition:** mortar
- **pinyin:** jiù
- **components:**
  - 舂
    - chōng
    - pound grain
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a mortar, often used with a pestle in the ancient form of 舂 (chōng, "pound grain")
  - **interpretation:** The character 臼 (jiù, "mortar") is an ancient pictogram representing a mortar used for grinding, commonly seen in traditional processes such as grain pounding, as depicted in the related character 舂 (chōng, "pound grain"). Its form visually represents the receptacle used to process grains.
- **examples:**
  - 他用一臼轻(輕)轻(輕)拂去脸(臉)上的尘(塵)土。
    - Tā yòng yī jiù qīngqīng fú qù liǎn shàng de chéntǔ.
    - He used his pair of hands to gently brush away the dust on his face.
  - 运(運)动(動)员(員)凭(憑)借一臼快速接过(過)球。
    - Yùndòngyuán píngjiè yī jiù kuàisù jiē guò qiú.
    - The athlete quickly caught the ball with his pair of hands.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 臼](@media/glyph81fc.png)
### 旧(舊)梦(夢) → 旧(舊) → 臼 → 舂
- **definition:** pound grain
- **pinyin:** chōng
- **components:**
  - 廾
    - gǒng
    - both hands
  - 午
    - wǔ
    - pestle
  - 臼
    - jiù
    - mortar
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogrammic compound
  - **description:**
    - 廾 (both hands) + 午 (pestle) + 臼 (mortar) =
    - using both hands to pound with a mortar and pestle
  - **interpretation:** The character 舂(chōng, 'pound grain') represents the action of using both hands to pound grain with a pestle in a mortar. The combination of these components reflects the traditional method of processing grains. 廾 (gǒng, 'both hands') suggests the manual aspect, 午 (wǔ, 'pestle') indicates the tool used, and 臼 (jiù, 'mortar') represents the container. This imagery directly ties to its meaning of pounding grain.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 舂](@media/glyph8202.png)
### 旧(舊)梦(夢) → 旧(舊) → 臼 → 舂 → 廾
- **definition:** both hands
- **pinyin:** gǒng
- **components:**
  - 𠂇
    - shǒu
    - left hand
  - 又
    - yòu
    - right hand
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogrammic compound
  - **description:**
    - 𠂇 (left hand) + 又 (right hand) =
    - two hands
  - **interpretation:** The character combines depictions of the left hand 𠂇 and the right hand 又, representing the concept of using both hands together. This combination naturally conveys the meaning of 'two hands.'
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 廾](@media/glyph5efe.png)
### 旧(舊)梦(夢) → 旧(舊) → 臼 → 舂 → 廾 → 𠂇
- **definition:** left hand
- **pinyin:** shǒu
- **components:**
  - 又
    - yòu
    - again
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts 又 (yòu, "again") flipped, representing a left hand.
  - **interpretation:** 𠂇 is a pictogram representing a left hand, visually derived from the character 又 (yòu, "again") by flipping it.
### 旧(舊)梦(夢) → 旧(舊) → 臼 → 舂 → 廾 → 又
- **definition:** right hand
- **pinyin:** yòu
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a right hand
  - **interpretation:** The character 又 (yòu, "hand") is a pictogram representing a right hand, showing the fingers and palm, which highlights its original meaning related to manual actions.
- **examples:**
  - 「又」这(這)个(個)字最早来(來)源于(於)手。
    - 「Yòu」 zhè gè zì zuì zǎo láiyuán yú shǒu。
    - The character '又' originally comes from the hand.
  - 很多汉(漢)字含有又部首，表示与(與)手有关(關)的动(動)作。
    - Hěn duō hànzì hányǒu Yòu bùshǒu, biǎoshì yǔ shǒu yǒuguān de dòngzuò。
    - Many Chinese characters include the '又' radical, indicating actions related to the hand.
  - 古人用又描绘(繪)手的形态(態)，体(體)现(現)了古汉(漢)字的独(獨)特魅力。
    - Gǔrén yòng Yòu miáohuì shǒu de xíngtài, tǐxiàn le gǔ hànzì de dútè mèilì。
    - Ancient people used '又' to depict the shape of the hand, showcasing the unique charm of ancient Chinese characters.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 又](@media/glyph53c8.png)
### 旧(舊)梦(夢) → 旧(舊) → 臼 → 舂 → 午
- **definition:** pestle
- **pinyin:** wǔ
- **components:**
  - 杵
    - chǔ
    - pestle
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Pictogram: Depicts a pestle (modern 杵 (chǔ, "pestle")) ->
    - original meaning unrelated to time concepts
  - **interpretation:** 午 (wǔ, "noon") originally depicted a pestle, but over time it was borrowed for usage in the context of time. Despite its current association with noon, its visual origin is agricultural, related to pounding or grinding.
- **examples:**
  - 中午时(時)分，阳(陽)光灿(燦)烂(爛)。
    - Zhōngwǔ shífēn, yángguāng cànlàn.
    - At noon, the sunlight is brilliant.
  - 我在午休中，享受宁(寧)静(靜)。
    - Wǒ zài wǔxiū zhōng, xiǎngshòu níngjìng.
    - I enjoy tranquility during my noon break.
  - 午餐后(後)，公园(園)里(裡)热(熱)闹(鬧)非凡。
    - Wǔcān hòu, gōngyuán lǐ rènào fēifán.
    - After lunch, the park is bustling.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 午](@media/glyph5348.png)
### 旧(舊)梦(夢) → 旧(舊) → 臼 → 舂 → 午 → 杵
- **definition:** pestle
- **pinyin:** chǔ
- **components:**
  - 木
    - mù
    - wood
  - 午
    - wǔ
    - pestle
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic 木 (mù, "wood") + phonetic 午 (wǔ, "pestle") ->
    - a wooden pestle
  - **interpretation:** Combines 木 (mù, "wood"), which signifies that the object is made of wood, with 午 (wǔ, "pestle") serving as the phonetic component to suggest the word's pronunciation. The character effectively depicts a pestle made from wood, as was traditionally used.
- **examples:**
  - 他用杵捣(搗)碎坚(堅)果。
    - Tā yòng chǔ dǎosuì jiānguǒ.
    - He used a pestle to crush the nuts.
  - 这(這)根杵是用来(來)捣(搗)蒜的。
    - Zhè gēn chǔ shì yòng lái dǎo suàn de.
    - This pestle is used for crushing garlic.
  - 传(傳)统(統)上，杵和臼一起使用来(來)制(製)作药(藥)物。
    - Chuántǒng shàng, chǔ hé jiù yìqǐ shǐyòng lái zhìzuò yàowù.
    - Traditionally, a pestle is used with a mortar to make medicine.
### 旧(舊)梦(夢) → 梦(夢)
- **traditional:** 夢
- **definition:** dream; vision; illusion; aspiration
- **pinyin:** mèng
- **components:**
  - 爿
    - pán
    - bed
  - 人
    - rén
    - person
  - 目
    - mù
    - eye
  - 夕
    - xī
    - night
  - 瞢
    - méng
    - bewildered
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - Oracle bone script: person 人 (rén, 'person') lying on bed 爿 (pán, 'bed') + eye 目 (mù, 'eye') with emphasis ->
    - Bronze inscriptions: 目 with eyebrows 眉 + person as dots + moon 夕 (xī, 'night') added ->
    - 夢: eyebrows 卝 + eyes 罒 + person's body 冖 + 夕 ->
    - phono-semantic compound: phonetic 瞢 + semantic 夕
  - **interpretation:** In the oracle bone script, 夢 evokes a person on a bed with an emphasized eye, suggesting a state of being where one's vision is active despite resting, which aligns with dreaming. By the Bronze inscriptions, with the addition of 夕, it highlights the nocturnal and unconscious nature of dreams. Modern 夢 combines phonetic 瞢 with semantic 夕, reflecting dreaming as something occurring at night.
  - **simplification:** 梦 is a simplified form of 夢 where 目 + 冖 is simplified to a simpler eye component and 冖.
- **examples:**
  - 我昨晚做了一个(個)美好的梦(夢)。
    - Wǒ zuó wǎn zuò le yī gè měihǎo de mèng.
    - I had a wonderful dream last night.
  - 她希望有一天能实(實)现(現)自己的梦(夢)想。
    - Tā xīwàng yǒu yī tiān néng shíxiàn zìjǐ de mèngxiǎng.
    - She hopes to fulfill her dreams one day.
  - 每个(個)人都应(應)该(該)追寻(尋)自己的梦(夢)。
    - Měi gè rén dōu yīnggāi zhuīxún zìjǐ de mèng.
    - Everyone should pursue their own dreams.
### 旧(舊)梦(夢) → 梦(夢) → 爿
- **definition:** bed
- **pinyin:** pán
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a bed ->
    - original form of 牀 (chuáng, "bed") ->
    - contracted form in 臧 (zāng, "possess")
  - **interpretation:** The character 爿 (pán, "bed") visually represents a bed, emphasizing its usage in denoting places for resting or sleeping. It served as the original form for the character 牀 (chuáng, "bed"), reinforcing its meaning. Additionally, in the character 臧 (zāng, "possess"), it appears as a contracted form, reflecting its historical usage in composite forms.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 爿](@media/glyph723f.png)
### 旧(舊)梦(夢) → 梦(夢) → 人
- **definition:** person
- **pinyin:** rén
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts side view of a standing man, highlighting an arm and a leg ->
    - visual representation of a person
  - **interpretation:** The character 人 (rén, 'person') effectively uses simple lines to depict the essential form of a human, making it immediately recognizable and intuitive as meaning 'person.'
- **examples:**
  - 他是个(個)好人。
    - Tā shì gè hǎo rén.
    - He is a good person.
  - 每个(個)人都有责(責)任，为(為)社会(會)作出贡(貢)献(獻)。
    - Měi gè rén dōu yǒu zérèn, wèi shèhuì zuòchū gòngxiàn.
    - Every person has a responsibility to contribute to society.
  - 人在旅途中，心灵(靈)获(獲)得了成长(長)。
    - Rén zài lǚtú zhōng, xīnlíng huòdé le chéngzhǎng.
    - People gain growth along their journey.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 人](@media/glyph4eba.png)
### 旧(舊)梦(夢) → 梦(夢) → 目
- **definition:** eye
- **pinyin:** mù
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a human eye, now represented and rotated 90 degrees ->
    - eye
  - **interpretation:** The character 目(mù, 'eye') is a pictogram representing a human eye. Its original orientation has changed over time, resembling an eye seen from a sideways view.
- **examples:**
  - 他的目光炯炯有神。
    - Tā de mùguāng jiǒngjiǒng yǒu shén.
    - His gaze is bright and full of spirit.
  - 她目不转(轉)睛，注视(視)前方。
    - Tā mù bù zhuǎn jīng, zhùshì qiánfāng.
    - She stared intently, gazing ahead.
  - 雄鹰(鷹)展翅，双(雙)目炯炯看天际(際)。
    - Xióng yīng zhǎn chì, shuāng mù jiǒngjiǒng kàn tiānjì.
    - The eagle spreads its wings, its eyes piercingly gaze at the horizon.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 目](@media/glyph76ee.png)
### 旧(舊)梦(夢) → 梦(夢) → 夕
- **definition:** night
- **pinyin:** xī
- **components:**
  - 月
    - yuè
    - moon
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a moon crescent
  - **interpretation:** The character 夕 (xī, 'evening') is a pictogram that represents a crescent moon, capturing the image of the moon in the evening sky. The comparison to 月 (yuè, 'moon') underscores its depiction of the moon phase commonly associated with evening.
- **examples:**
  - 夕阳(陽)西下。
    - xī yáng xīxià.
    - The setting sun descends.
  - 夕阳(陽)西下，晚风(風)徐徐。
    - xī yáng xīxià, wǎn fēng xúxú.
    - The sun sets as the gentle evening breeze blows.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 夕](@media/glyph5915.png)
### 旧(舊)梦(夢) → 梦(夢) → 夕 → 月
- **definition:** moon
- **pinyin:** yuè
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a crescent moon
  - **interpretation:** The character 月(yuè, "moon") is a pictographic representation of a crescent moon, straightforwardly capturing the curved shape often associated with the moon's appearance. Though interchangeable with 夕 (xī, "evening") in the past, it distinctly represents the moon in this usage.
- **examples:**
  - 夜空挂(掛)着(著)明月。
    - Yè kōng guà zhe míng yuè.
    - The bright moon hangs in the night sky.
  - 人们(們)赏(賞)月，寄托(託)相思。
    - Rén men shǎng yuè, jì tuō xiāng sī.
    - People enjoy the moon, expressing their longing.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 月](@media/glyph6708.png)
### 旧(舊)梦(夢) → 梦(夢) → 瞢
- **definition:** bewildered
- **pinyin:** méng
- **components:**
  - 目
    - mù
    - eye
  - 亡
    - wáng
    - departed; gone; lost
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic 目 (mù, "eye") + phonetic 亡 (wáng) ->
    - sense of being lost or disoriented, particularly in vision ->
    - bewildered
  - **interpretation:** The character combines 目 (mù, "eye") as the semantic component with 亡 (wáng) as the phonetic component, suggesting a state where one's vision is metaphorically lost or confused, reflecting the meaning of being bewildered.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 瞢](@media/glyph77a2.png)
### 旧(舊)梦(夢) → 梦(夢) → 瞢 → 亡
- **definition:** departed; gone; lost
- **pinyin:** wáng
- **components:**
  - 刀
    - dāo
    - knife
  - 芒
    - máng
    - edge of a knife
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogram
  - **description:**
    - A line on 刀 (dāo, 'knife') ->
    - cutting edge of a knife ->
    - original form of 芒 (máng, 'edge of a knife')
  - **interpretation:** The character depicts a line on a knife, representing the sharp edge. This connection to sharpness and cutting leads to the concept of 'perish,' as an edge can cut or end something, symbolically indicating destruction or the end of life.
- **examples:**
  - 战(戰)士们(們)在战(戰)场(場)上英勇战(戰)斗(鬥)，许(許)多人不幸亡。
    - Zhànshìmen zài zhànchǎng shàng yīngyǒng zhàndòu, xǔduō rén bùxìng wáng.
    - The soldiers fought bravely on the battlefield, and many unfortunately perished.
  - 如果不努力经(經)营(營)，这(這)家公司可能会(會)亡。
    - Rúguǒ bù nǔlì jīngyíng, zhè jiā gōngsī kěnéng huì wáng.
    - If the company does not operate diligently, it may perish.
  - 古代帝国(國)由于(於)内(內)外问(問)题(題)而一朝亡。
    - Gǔdài dìguó yóuyú nèiwài wèntí ér yī zhāo wáng.
    - The ancient empire perished overnight due to internal and external issues.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 亡](@media/glyph4ea1.png)
### 旧(舊)梦(夢) → 梦(夢) → 瞢 → 亡 → 刀
- **definition:** knife
- **pinyin:** dāo
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a knife
  - **interpretation:** 刀 (dāo, "knife") is a pictographic representation of a knife or blade, with a sharp edge and a handle, resembling the form of a basic cutting tool.
- **examples:**
  - 他用锋(鋒)利的刀，切开(開)蔬菜。
    - tā yòng fēnglì de dāo, qiē kāi shūcài.
    - He uses a sharp knife to cut vegetables.
  - 这(這)把刀非常锋(鋒)利。
    - zhè bǎ dāo fēicháng fēnglì.
    - This knife is very sharp.
  - 厨(廚)师(師)小心地持刀，为(為)客人切肉。
    - chúshī xiǎoxīn de chí dāo, wèi kèrén qiē ròu.
    - The chef holds the knife carefully and slices meat for the guest.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 刀](@media/glyph5200.png)
### 旧(舊)梦(夢) → 梦(夢) → 瞢 → 亡 → 芒
- **definition:** edge of a knife
- **pinyin:** máng
- **components:**
  - 艹
    - cǎo
    - grass
  - 亡
    - wáng
    - to flee
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic 艹 (cǎo, "grass") + phonetic 亡 (wáng) ->
    - edge of a knife
  - **interpretation:** The character 芒(máng, "edge of a knife") uses the 艹 (cǎo, "grass") component to highlight its relation to plant life or natural elements, while 亡 (wáng) provides the phonetic indication. Originally it may have depicted something like 方 but evolved to illustrate the thinness or sharpness of grass edges, metaphorically linking to the sharp edge of a knife.
- **examples:**
  - 刀的芒在阳(陽)光下闪(閃)闪(閃)发(發)光。
    - Dāo de máng zài yángguāng xià shǎnshǎn fāguāng.
    - The edge of the knife glistens in the sunlight.
  - 我们(們)要小心刀的芒，因为(為)它非常锋(鋒)利。
    - Wǒmen yào xiǎoxīn dāo de máng, yīnwèi tā fēicháng fēnglì.
    - We must be careful of the knife's edge because it is very sharp.
  - 他用手指轻(輕)轻(輕)触(觸)摸刀的芒，感受到它的锋(鋒)利。
    - Tā yòng shǒuzhǐ qīngqīng chùmō dāo de máng, gǎnshòudào tā de fēnglì.
    - He gently touched the blade's edge with his finger and felt its sharpness.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 芒](@media/glyph8292.png)
### 旧(舊)梦(夢) → 梦(夢) → 瞢 → 亡 → 芒 → 艹
- **definition:** grass
- **pinyin:** cǎo
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts blades of grass
  - **interpretation:** 艹 is a pictogram representing grass or plants, resembling blades of grass. It is commonly used as a radical in other characters related to grass or vegetation.
- **examples:**
  - 他写(寫)字时(時)用艹作草字的偏旁。
    - Tā xiězì shí yòng cǎo zuò cǎozì de piānpáng.
    - He uses '艹' as the radical for grass in his characters.
  - 春天到来(來)时(時)，艹生长(長)得很快。
    - Chūntiān dàolái shí, cǎo shēngzhǎng de hěn kuài.
    - When spring arrives, grass grows rapidly.

## 忘记(記)
---
## forget
### wàngjì
---
- **traditional:** 忘記
- **definition:** forget
- **pinyin:** wàngjì
- **components:**
  - 忘
    - wàng
    - forget; lose
  - 记(記)
    - jì
    - remember; record
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** compound word
  - **description:** 忘 (wàng, "forget") suggests the act of losing memory or failing to remember something. 記 (jì, "remember") contrasts with 忘 (wàng, "forget") by indicating the act of keeping information in mind.
  - **interpretation:** In Chinese, 忘記 (wàngjì, "forget") combines 忘 (wàng, "forget") and 記 (jì, "remember") to denote the act of failing to retain or recall information. The pairing emphasizes the idea of letting go of what is or should be remembered.
- **examples:**
  - 我总(總)是忘记(記)带(帶)钥(鑰)匙。
    - Wǒ zǒng shì wàngjì dài yàoshi.
    - I always forget to bring keys.
  - 他常常忘记(記)吃药(藥)。
    - Tā chángcháng wàngjì chī yào.
    - He often forgets to take his medicine.
  - 请(請)不要忘记(記)这(這)次会(會)议(議)。
    - Qǐng bùyào wàngjì zhè cì huìyì.
    - Please don't forget this meeting.
### 忘记(記) → 忘
- **definition:** forget; lose
- **pinyin:** wàng
- **components:**
  - 亡
    - wáng
    - lose
  - 心
    - xīn
    - heart
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - 亡 (wáng, "lose") as phonetic + 心 (xīn, "heart") as semantic =
    - to lose something in the heart ->
    - forget
  - **interpretation:** The character 忘(wàng, "forget") combines the phonetic element 亡 (wáng, "lose") with 心 (xīn, "heart"), indicating the concept of losing something from the heart, hence the idea of forgetting.
- **examples:**
  - 他总(總)是忘记(記)带(帶)钥(鑰)匙。
    - Tā zǒng shì wàngjì dài yàoshi.
    - He always forgets to bring the keys.
  - 请(請)不要忘记(記)你的承诺(諾)。
    - Qǐng bùyào wàngjì nǐ de chéngnuò.
    - Please don't forget your promise.
  - 有时(時)我会(會)忘记(記)时(時)间(間)，错(錯)过(過)重要的事情。
    - Yǒushí wǒ huì wàngjì shíjiān, cuòguò zhòngyào de shìqíng.
    - Sometimes I forget the time and miss important things.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 忘](@media/glyph5fd8.png)
### 忘记(記) → 忘 → 亡
- **definition:** lose
- **pinyin:** wáng
- **components:**
  - 刀
    - dāo
    - knife
  - 芒
    - máng
    - edge of a knife
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogram
  - **description:**
    - A line on 刀 (dāo, 'knife') ->
    - cutting edge of a knife ->
    - original form of 芒 (máng, 'edge of a knife')
  - **interpretation:** The character depicts a line on a knife, representing the sharp edge. This connection to sharpness and cutting leads to the concept of 'perish,' as an edge can cut or end something, symbolically indicating destruction or the end of life.
- **examples:**
  - 战(戰)士们(們)在战(戰)场(場)上英勇战(戰)斗(鬥)，许(許)多人不幸亡。
    - Zhànshìmen zài zhànchǎng shàng yīngyǒng zhàndòu, xǔduō rén bùxìng wáng.
    - The soldiers fought bravely on the battlefield, and many unfortunately perished.
  - 如果不努力经(經)营(營)，这(這)家公司可能会(會)亡。
    - Rúguǒ bù nǔlì jīngyíng, zhè jiā gōngsī kěnéng huì wáng.
    - If the company does not operate diligently, it may perish.
  - 古代帝国(國)由于(於)内(內)外问(問)题(題)而一朝亡。
    - Gǔdài dìguó yóuyú nèiwài wèntí ér yī zhāo wáng.
    - The ancient empire perished overnight due to internal and external issues.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 亡](@media/glyph4ea1.png)
### 忘记(記) → 忘 → 亡 → 刀
- **definition:** knife
- **pinyin:** dāo
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a knife
  - **interpretation:** 刀 (dāo, "knife") is a pictographic representation of a knife or blade, with a sharp edge and a handle, resembling the form of a basic cutting tool.
- **examples:**
  - 他用锋(鋒)利的刀，切开(開)蔬菜。
    - tā yòng fēnglì de dāo, qiē kāi shūcài.
    - He uses a sharp knife to cut vegetables.
  - 这(這)把刀非常锋(鋒)利。
    - zhè bǎ dāo fēicháng fēnglì.
    - This knife is very sharp.
  - 厨(廚)师(師)小心地持刀，为(為)客人切肉。
    - chúshī xiǎoxīn de chí dāo, wèi kèrén qiē ròu.
    - The chef holds the knife carefully and slices meat for the guest.

### 忘记(記) → 忘 → 心
- **definition:** heart
- **pinyin:** xīn
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a heart
  - **interpretation:** The character 心(xīn, "heart") originally depicted the shape of an actual heart, representing thoughts, emotions, and the core of a person. Over time, it has become highly stylized, but it continues to convey the notion of the heart as the center of emotions and consciousness.
- **examples:**
  - 她的心一直都在帮(幫)助别(別)人。
    - Tā de xīn yīzhí dōu zài bāngzhù biérén.
    - Her heart is always in helping others.
  - 在城市的中心，有一个(個)美丽(麗)的公园(園)。
    - Zài chéngshì de zhōngxīn, yǒu yí gè měilì de gōngyuán.
    - At the center of the city, there is a beautiful park.
  - 对(對)于(於)许(許)多人来(來)说(說)，家庭是生活的核心。
    - Duìyú xǔduō rén lái shuō, jiātíng shì shēnghuó de héxīn.
    - For many people, family is the core of life.

### 忘记(記) → 记(記)
- **traditional:** 記
- **definition:** remember; record
- **pinyin:** jì
- **components:**
  - 言
    - yán
    - speech
  - 己
    - jǐ
    - self
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - 言 (yán, "speech; words") + 己 (jǐ, "self") =
    - speech related to oneself ->
    - final form 記
  - **interpretation:** The character 記 (jì, "record") combines speech 言, indicating communication or words, with the phonetic 己, referring to oneself. This combination suggests the idea of recording or remembering words related to oneself or one's experiences.
  - **simplification:** The traditional character 記 was simplified to 记 by replacing 言(言, "speech") with the simpler 讠, reducing stroke count while maintaining the semantic component.
- **examples:**
  - 我每天写(寫)日记(記)。
    - Wǒ měitiān xiě rìjì.
    - I write a diary every day.
  - 请(請)记(記)住这(這)条(條)重要的规(規)则(則)。
    - Qǐng jì zhù zhè tiáo zhòngyào de guīzé.
    - Please remember this important rule.
  - 他把电(電)话(話)号(號)码(碼)记(記)在本子上。
    - Tā bǎ diànhuà hàomǎ jì zài běnzi shàng.
    - He recorded the phone number in the notebook.
### 忘记(記) → 记(記) → 言
- **definition:** speech
- **pinyin:** yán
- **components:**
  - 舌
    - shé
    - tongue
  - 口
    - kǒu
    - mouth
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogram
  - **description:**
    - 舌 (mouth with a forked tongue) with added stroke at top to suggest tongue movement ->
    - speech
  - **interpretation:** The character 言(yán, "speech") depicts the addition of a horizontal stroke to the ancient form of 舌(shé, "tongue") to indicate the motion of the tongue as it moves to articulate speech. This directly connects the organ involved in speaking to the concept of speech itself.
- **examples:**
  - 他的言语(語)充满(滿)智慧。
    - Tā de yányǔ chōngmǎn zhìhuì.
    - His speech is full of wisdom.
  - 我们(們)应(應)该(該)以行动(動)证(證)明我们(們)的言词(詞)。
    - Wǒmen yīnggāi yǐ xíngdòng zhèngmíng wǒmen de yáncí.
    - We should prove our words with actions.
  - 他说(說)话(話)的方式显(顯)示了他的修养(養)。
    - Tā shuōhuà de fāngshì xiǎnshìle tā de xiūyǎng.
    - The way he speaks shows his refinement.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 言](@media/glyph8a00.png)
### 忘记(記) → 记(記) → 言 → 舌
- **definition:** tongue
- **pinyin:** shé
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a forked tongue emerging upwards from a mouth
  - **interpretation:** The character 舌(shé, 'tongue') visually represents a tongue extending out from a mouth, which aligns with its meaning. This direct depiction makes it easy to remember its association with speech and taste in its semantic family, also relating to words like 言(yán, 'word').
- **examples:**
  - 他的舌非常灵(靈)敏。
    - Tā de shé fēicháng língmǐn.
    - His tongue is very sensitive.
  - 品尝(嚐)美食时(時)，他的舌细(細)品滋味。
    - Pǐncháng měishí shí, tā de shé xì pǐn zīwèi.
    - While tasting delicious food, his tongue savors every flavor.
  - 他长(長)舌无(無)忌，经(經)常泄露秘密。
    - Tā chángshé wújì, jīngcháng xièlòu mìmì.
    - He is talkative and often spills secrets.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 舌](@media/glyph820c.png)
### 忘记(記) → 记(記) → 言 → 口
- **definition:** mouth
- **pinyin:** kǒu
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts an open mouth.
  - **interpretation:** The character 口(kǒu, 'mouth') is a straightforward pictogram that visually represents an open mouth. It is a fundamental character in the Chinese language, often used both as an independent word and as a component in more complex characters, lending a semantic association to ideas relating to speech, openings, or enclosures.
- **examples:**
  - 他张(張)开(開)口，大声(聲)喊叫。
    - Tā zhāngkāi kǒu, dàshēng hǎnjiào.
    - He opened his mouth and shouted loudly.
  - 这(這)口饭(飯)入口即化。
    - Zhè kǒu fàn rùkǒu jíhuà.
    - This mouthful of food melts in your mouth.
  - 小女孩咬了一口苹(蘋)果，露出甜美的笑容。
    - Xiǎo nǚhái yǎole yī kǒu píngguǒ, lùchū tiánměi de xiàoróng.
    - The little girl took a bite of the apple and smiled sweetly.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 口](@media/glyph53e3.png)
### 忘记(記) → 记(記) → 己
- **definition:** self
- **pinyin:** jǐ
- **components:**
  - 紀
    - jì
    - record
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts silk rope for binding objects; original form of 紀 (紀) (jì, "record")
  - **interpretation:** 己 (jǐ, "self") depicts a silk rope for binding, symbolizing the concept of self-containment or self-restriction, leading to the abstract sense of 'self'.
- **examples:**
  - 知己知彼，百战(戰)不殆。
    - Zhī jǐ zhī bǐ, bǎi zhàn bù dài.
    - Know yourself and know your enemy, and you will never be defeated.
  - 每个(個)人都应(應)该(該)反省自己。
    - Měi gè rén dōu yīng gāi fǎn xǐng zì jǐ.
    - Everyone should reflect on themselves.
  - 你要为(為)自己负(負)责(責)。
    - Nǐ yào wèi zì jǐ fù zé.
    - You need to be responsible for yourself.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 己](@media/glyph5df1.png)
### 忘记(記) → 记(記) → 己 → 紀
- **definition:** record
- **pinyin:** jì
- **components:**
  - 糸
    - mì
    - silk; thread
  - 己
    - jǐ
    - self
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic 糸 (mì, 'silk; thread') + phonetic 己 (jǐ) ->
    - record
  - **interpretation:** The character combines 糸 (mì, 'silk; thread') indicating threads or lines, with 己 (jǐ) as the phonetic component. In this context, 'thread' aligns with 'record' in the sense of a sequence or line of events documented over time.
  - **simplification:** The traditional form 紀 with 糸 (mì, 'silk; thread') replaced by the simpler 纟 in the simplified form 纪.
- **examples:**
  - 这(這)本书(書)详(詳)细(細)记(記)录(錄)了历(歷)史事件。
    - Zhè běn shū xiángxì jìlù le lìshǐ shìjiàn.
    - This book records historical events in detail.
  - 古代人通过(過)文字来(來)纪(紀)念重要事情。
    - Gǔdài rén tōngguò wénzì lái jìniàn zhòngyào shìqíng.
    - Ancient people recorded important events through writing.
  - 公司在年底会(會)发(發)布(佈)年度报(報)告来(來)记(記)录(錄)发(發)展情况(況)。
    - Gōngsī zài niándǐ huì fābù niándù bàogào lái jìlù fāzhǎn qíngkuàng.
    - The company will release an annual report at the end of the year to record development status.
### 忘记(記) → 记(記) → 己 → 紀 → 糸
- **definition:** silk; thread
- **pinyin:** mì
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a skein of silk
  - **interpretation:** The character 糸(mì, "silk; thread") represents a pictorial representation of a skein of silk, visually capturing the concept of thread or fiber.
- **examples:**
  - 她手工制(製)作了一条(條)漂亮的丝(絲)巾。
    - Tā shǒugōng zhìzuòle yī tiáo piàoliang de sī jīn.
    - She handcrafted a beautiful silk scarf.
  - 这(這)个(個)设(設)计(計)图(圖)必须(須)用细(細)糸画(畫)出来(來)。
    - Zhège shèjìtú bìxū yòng xì mì huà chūlái.
    - This design drawing must be sketched with fine thread.
  - 我们(們)参(參)观(觀)了古代的织(織)布技术(術)，对(對)丝(絲)绸(綢)制(製)作产(產)生了兴(興)趣。
    - Wǒmen cānguānle gǔdài de zhībù jìshù, duì sīchóu zhìzuò chǎnshēngle xìngqù.
    - We visited ancient weaving techniques and developed an interest in silk production.
- **historical forms:**

## 同事
---
## colleague
### tóngshì
---
- **definition:** colleague
- **pinyin:** tóngshì
- **components:**
  - 同
    - tóng
    - together; same; with
  - 事
    - shì
    - affair; matter; work; business
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** compound word
  - **description:**
    - 同 (tóng, "together") + 事 (shì, "affair; matter") =
    - people doing affairs together ->
    - colleague
  - **interpretation:** 同 (tóng, "together") represents the idea of people or actions being united in purpose or place. 事 (shì, "affair; matter") refers to tasks or duties one engages in. Thus, 同事 (tóngshì) literally means 'together in affairs' or 'sharing a common task,' which conceptually leads to 'colleague,' as colleagues are those who work together on shared tasks and responsibilities within a workplace.
- **examples:**
  - 我和同事一起吃午饭(飯)。
    - Wǒ hé tóngshì yīqǐ chī wǔfàn.
    - I have lunch with my colleague.
  - 昨天晚上，我和同事加班到很晚。
    - Zuótiān wǎnshàng, wǒ hé tóngshì jiābān dào hěn wǎn.
    - Last night, I and my colleague worked overtime until late.
  - 她的新同事很友好。
    - Tā de xīn tóngshì hěn yǒuhǎo.
    - Her new colleague is very friendly.
### 同事 → 同
- **definition:** together; same; with
- **pinyin:** tóng
- **components:**
  - 口
    - kǒu
    - "mouth"
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** Pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Originally depicted as a pipe 筒 (tǒng, "pipe") ->
    - 口 added as decoration ->
    - interpreted as mouth 口 (kǒu, "mouth") giving orders ->
    - evolved to mean togetherness and unity
  - **interpretation:** The character 同 (tóng, "same; unity; together; common") originally depicted a pipe but later took on the symbolic meaning of unity, possibly influenced by the shared cooperation in activities like music or rigid group tasks. The addition of 口 (kǒu, "mouth") emphasizes communication and collaboration.
- **examples:**
  - 我们(們)同心协(協)力。
    - Wǒmen tóngxīn xiélì.
    - We work together with one heart and mind.
  - 他们(們)穿着(著)同款衣服，看起来(來)十分整齐(齊)。
    - Tāmen chuānzhe tóng kuǎn yīfú, kàn qǐlái shífēn zhěngqí.
    - They are wearing the same style of clothes and look very orderly.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 同](@media/glyph540c.png)
### 同事 → 同 → 口
- **definition:** "mouth"
- **pinyin:** kǒu
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts an open mouth.
  - **interpretation:** The character 口(kǒu, 'mouth') is a straightforward pictogram that visually represents an open mouth. It is a fundamental character in the Chinese language, often used both as an independent word and as a component in more complex characters, lending a semantic association to ideas relating to speech, openings, or enclosures.
- **examples:**
  - 他张(張)开(開)口，大声(聲)喊叫。
    - Tā zhāngkāi kǒu, dàshēng hǎnjiào.
    - He opened his mouth and shouted loudly.
  - 这(這)口饭(飯)入口即化。
    - Zhè kǒu fàn rùkǒu jíhuà.
    - This mouthful of food melts in your mouth.
  - 小女孩咬了一口苹(蘋)果，露出甜美的笑容。
    - Xiǎo nǚhái yǎole yī kǒu píngguǒ, lùchū tiánměi de xiàoróng.
    - The little girl took a bite of the apple and smiled sweetly.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 口](@media/glyph53e3.png)
### 同事 → 事
- **definition:** affair; matter; work; business
- **pinyin:** shì
- **components:**
  - 又
    - yòu
    - hand
  - 中
    - zhōng
    - a flagpole with a drum
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogrammic compound
  - **description:**
    - 又 (yòu, "hand") + 中 (zhōng, "a flagpole with a drum") =
    - flag in hand ->
    - to perform one's job
  - **interpretation:** The character 事 (shì, "matter") represents the concept of handling or managing affairs, symbolized by holding a flag, indicating a formal duty or role. The flagpole with a drum suggests organized activity or official matters.
- **examples:**
  - 这(這)件事很复(複)杂(雜)。
    - Zhè jiàn shì hěn fùzá.
    - This matter is very complicated.
  - 小事也能引发(發)大问(問)题(題)，我们(們)需要认(認)真对(對)待。
    - Xiǎo shì yě néng yǐn fā dà wèntí, wǒmen xūyào rènzhēn duìdài.
    - Even small matters can trigger big problems; we need to handle them seriously.
  - 他总(總)是处(處)理各种(種)事，不管大小。
    - Tā zǒng shì chǔlǐ gèzhǒng shì, bùguǎn dàxiǎo.
    - He always manages various affairs, regardless of their significance.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 事](@media/glyph4e8b.png)
### 同事 → 事 → 又
- **definition:** hand
- **pinyin:** yòu
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a right hand
  - **interpretation:** The character 又 (yòu, "hand") is a pictogram representing a right hand, showing the fingers and palm, which highlights its original meaning related to manual actions.
- **examples:**
  - 「又」这(這)个(個)字最早来(來)源于(於)手。
    - 「Yòu」 zhè gè zì zuì zǎo láiyuán yú shǒu。
    - The character '又' originally comes from the hand.
  - 很多汉(漢)字含有又部首，表示与(與)手有关(關)的动(動)作。
    - Hěn duō hànzì hányǒu Yòu bùshǒu, biǎoshì yǔ shǒu yǒuguān de dòngzuò。
    - Many Chinese characters include the '又' radical, indicating actions related to the hand.
  - 古人用又描绘(繪)手的形态(態)，体(體)现(現)了古汉(漢)字的独(獨)特魅力。
    - Gǔrén yòng Yòu miáohuì shǒu de xíngtài, tǐxiàn le gǔ hànzì de dútè mèilì。
    - Ancient people used '又' to depict the shape of the hand, showcasing the unique charm of ancient Chinese characters.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 又](@media/glyph53c8.png)
### 同事 → 事 → 中
- **definition:** a flagpole with a drum
- **pinyin:** zhōng
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts an arrow piercing through the center of a target
  - **interpretation:** The character 中 (zhōng, "middle") visually represents an arrow passing through the central point of a target, illustrating the concept of 'center' or 'middle' effectively. This visual imagery is straightforward and memorable, corresponding closely with its meaning of being at the center or middle of something.
- **examples:**
  - 他站在道路中，看着(著)远(遠)方。
    - tā zhàn zài dàolù zhōng, kànzhe yuǎnfāng.
    - He stands in the middle of the road, gazing into the distance.
  - 房间(間)正中，挂(掛)着(著)一幅名画(畫)。
    - fángjiān zhèng zhōng, guàzhe yī fú mínghuà.
    - A famous painting hangs in the exact center of the room.
- **historical forms:**

## 有时(時)
---
## sometimes
### yǒushí
---
- **traditional:** 有時
- **definition:** sometimes
- **pinyin:** yǒushí
- **components:**
  - 有
    - yǒu
    - have; there is
  - 时(時)
    - shí
    - time; o'clock; when; hour
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** compound word
  - **description:** 有 (yǒu, "have; there is") and 时(時) (shí, "time") combine to describe an occurrence that happens occasionally by having certain times or instances.
  - **interpretation:** The combination of 有 (yǒu, "have; there is") and 时(時) (shí, "time") conceptualizes the idea of having certain times, which translates to the occasional or non-regular occurrence of something.
- **examples:**
  - 有时(時)天气很热。
    - Yǒushí tiānqì hěn rè.
    - Sometimes the weather is very hot.
  - 他有时(時)会(會)在早上跑步。
    - Tā yǒushí huì zài zǎoshang pǎobù.
    - He sometimes goes running in the morning.
  - 我有时(時)在周末去看电(電)影。
    - Wǒ yǒushí zài zhōumò qù kàn diànyǐng.
    - I sometimes go to watch movies on weekends.
### 有时(時) → 有
- **definition:** have; there is
- **pinyin:** yǒu
- **components:**
  - 又
    - yòu
    - hand
  - ⺼(肉)
    - ròu
    - meat
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - Phonetic 又(yòu, 'hand') + Semantic ⺼(肉, 'meat') ->
    - abstracted form ->
    - meaning: possess, exist
  - **interpretation:** The character 有(yǒu, 'have') combines the form of a hand holding something, represented by 又(yòu, 'hand'), with the semantic idea of possession or content rooted in 肉(ròu, 'meat'). This symbolically implies having or being in possession of something. Although the original script does not explicitly show meat, the abstracted form represents the concept of existence or possession.
- **examples:**
  - 我有一本书(書)。
    - Wǒ yǒu yī běn shū.
    - I have a book.
  - 花园(園)里(裡)有许(許)多美丽(麗)的花，小鸟(鳥)也在唱歌。
    - Huāyuán lǐ yǒu xǔduō měilì de huā, xiǎo niǎo yě zài chànggē.
    - There are many beautiful flowers in the garden, and the little bird is also singing.
  - 桌上有一杯水。
    - Zhuō shàng yǒu yī bēi shuǐ.
    - There is a glass of water on the table.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 有](@media/glyph6709.png)
### 有时(時) → 有 → 又
- **definition:** hand
- **pinyin:** yòu
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a right hand
  - **interpretation:** The character 又 (yòu, "hand") is a pictogram representing a right hand, showing the fingers and palm, which highlights its original meaning related to manual actions.
- **examples:**
  - 「又」这(這)个(個)字最早来(來)源于(於)手。
    - 「Yòu」 zhè gè zì zuì zǎo láiyuán yú shǒu。
    - The character '又' originally comes from the hand.
  - 很多汉(漢)字含有又部首，表示与(與)手有关(關)的动(動)作。
    - Hěn duō hànzì hányǒu Yòu bùshǒu, biǎoshì yǔ shǒu yǒuguān de dòngzuò。
    - Many Chinese characters include the '又' radical, indicating actions related to the hand.
  - 古人用又描绘(繪)手的形态(態)，体(體)现(現)了古汉(漢)字的独(獨)特魅力。
    - Gǔrén yòng Yòu miáohuì shǒu de xíngtài, tǐxiàn le gǔ hànzì de dútè mèilì。
    - Ancient people used '又' to depict the shape of the hand, showcasing the unique charm of ancient Chinese characters.

### 有时(時) → 有 → ⺼(肉)
- **traditional:** 肉
- **definition:** meat
- **pinyin:** ròu
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts ribs of an animal's torso ->
    - physical representation of a slice of meat
  - **interpretation:** The character 肉 (ròu, 'meat') visually represents the structure of ribs or flesh, making its meaning clear and direct in relation to its shape. Over time, its form was stylized into other component shapes like 月 when combined with phonetic elements.
- **examples:**
  - 我喜欢(歡)吃肉。
    - Wǒ xǐhuān chī ròu.
    - I like to eat meat.
  - 妈(媽)妈(媽)做了一道红(紅)烧(燒)肉，味道鲜(鮮)美无(無)比。
    - Māmā zuòle yīdào hóngshāo ròu, wèidào xiānměi wúbǐ.
    - Mom prepared a dish of braised meat, and its flavor is extraordinarily delicious.
  - 聚会(會)时(時)，我点(點)了一份烤肉，大家都赞(讚)不绝(絕)口。
    - Jùhuì shí, wǒ diǎnle yī fèn kǎo ròu, dàjiā dōu zàn bù jué kǒu.
    - During the party, I ordered a portion of grilled meat, and everyone couldn't stop praising it.
### 有时(時) → 时(時)
- **traditional:** 時
- **definition:** time; o'clock; when; hour
- **pinyin:** shí
- **components:**
  - 日
    - rì
    - sun; day
  - 寺
    - sì
    - temple
  - 之
    - zhī
    - governing
  - 寸
    - cùn
    - inch
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - 日 (rì, 'sun; day') as semantic + 寺 as phonetic ->
    - associated with time; ancient form 旹 with 日 and 之 (zhī, 'governing'), referring to the passing of time ->
    - over time, 寸 (cùn, 'inch') added to form current 時
  - **interpretation:** The character 時 (shí, 'time; season') stems from the interplay between 日 (rì, 'sun; day'), which signifies the passage of time marked by the sun, and 寺 as the phonetic component capturing the sound. The historical forms show an evolution from 旹, merging 日 and 之 (zhī, 'governing') to imply governance over time, to its modern form, where 寸 ('inch') likely emphasizes precision or measurement in the concept of time.
  - **simplification:** In 时 (shí), the component 寺 was retained for phonetic purposes, while 日 (rì, 'sun; day') was simplified to resemble 日 with fewer strokes, streamlining the character.
- **examples:**
  - 我们(們)相识(識)时(時)，天已经(經)暗了。
    - Wǒmen xiāngshí shí, tiān yǐjīng àn le.
    - When we met, the sky was already dark.
  - 在这(這)样(樣)的时(時)刻，我们(們)需要团(團)结(結)。
    - Zài zhèyàng de shíkè, wǒmen xūyào tuánjié.
    - At such a time, we need to unite.
  - 时(時)光流逝，童年的回忆(憶)依然鲜(鮮)活。
    - Shíguāng liúshì, tóngnián de huíyì yīrán xiānhuó.
    - As time passes, childhood memories remain vivid.
### 有时(時) → 时(時) → 日
- **definition:** sun; day
- **pinyin:** rì
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts the sun; a dot or line added in the center to distinguish from similar characters e.g. 囗
  - **interpretation:** As a pictogram, 日(rì, 'sun') directly represents the sun. In ancient times, the added dot helped visually differentiate it from other characters. This is analogous to the astronomical symbol ☉ and Egyptian hieroglyph 𓇳, both depicting the sun.
- **examples:**
  - 晨曦来(來)临(臨)时(時)，日出东(東)方。
    - Chénxī láilín shí, rìchū dōngfāng.
    - At the break of dawn, the sun rises in the east.
  - 温(溫)暖的日光洒(灑)满(滿)大地。
    - Wēnnuǎn de rìguāng sǎ mǎn dàdì.
    - The warm sunlight spreads over the earth.
  - 中午时(時)分，日高挂(掛)天。
    - Zhōngwǔ shífēn, rì gāo guà tiān.
    - At noon, the sun hangs high in the sky.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 日](@media/glyph65e5.png)
### 有时(時) → 时(時) → 寺
- **definition:** temple
- **pinyin:** sì
- **components:**
  - 𡳿
    - zhī
    - to go; footprint
  - 寸
    - cùn
    - inch
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - phonetic 𡳿 ->
    - 之; 士 + semantic 又 (hand) ->
    - 寸 in Small Seal Script ->
    - 寺
  - **interpretation:** 寺(sì, 'temple') combines the semantic element 寸 (cùn, 'inch'), originally from 又 (yòu, 'hand'), to imply precision or holding, with the phonetic element that evolved into 士 (shì, 'scholar'). The phonetic component originally represented going or movement but later took on a more abstract form. This combination suggests a place of order and ritual, characteristic of temples.
- **examples:**
  - 他每天早晨去寺庙(廟)。
    - Tā měitiān zǎochén qù sìmiào.
    - He goes to the temple every morning.
  - 寺庙(廟)里(裡)的钟(鐘)声(聲)非常悠扬(揚)。
    - Sìmiào lǐ de zhōngshēng fēicháng yōuyáng.
    - The bell sounds in the temple are very melodious.
  - 我们(們)参(參)观(觀)了京都的古老寺庙(廟)，觉(覺)得很平静(靜)。
    - Wǒmen cānguānle Jīngdū de gǔlǎo sìmiào, juéde hěn píngjìng.
    - We visited an ancient temple in Kyoto and felt very peaceful.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 寺](@media/glyph5bfa.png)
### 有时(時) → 时(時) → 寺 → 𡳿
- **definition:** to go; footprint
- **pinyin:** zhī
- **components:**
  - 止
    - zhǐ
    - foot
  - 一
    - yī
    - the beginning place
  - 之
    - zhī
    - to go
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogrammic compound
  - **description:**
    - 止(“foot”) + 一(“the beginning place”) ->
    - originally 㞢 ->
    - similar to 出 ->
    - evolved as a variant of 之
  - **interpretation:** The character 𡳿 is a variant of 之 (zhī, "to go") and conveys the idea of movement or direction. The original form 㞢 combines 止 (zhǐ, "foot") representing a footprint with 一 (yī, "the beginning place"), symbolizing the commencement of movement or journey, leading to the meaning of 'to go'. Over time, components such as the footprint evolved into different forms, leading to variants such as 𡳿.
### 有时(時) → 时(時) → 寺 → 𡳿 → 止
- **definition:** foot
- **pinyin:** zhǐ
- **components:**
  - 趾
    - zhǐ
    - foot
  - 龰
    - yù
    - stylized feet
  - 手
    - shǒu
    - hand
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Original: Foot pointing up with 3 toes and a sole ->
    - Stylized as 龰 ->
    - Derivative 趾 refers to original 'foot' meaning
  - **interpretation:** Originally depicting a footprint with toes and a sole, 止 (zhǐ, "foot") represents the foot. The character's form resembles a foot with three toes, analogous to how the hand is represented with fingers in other characters.
- **examples:**
  - 他受伤(傷)的止需要静(靜)养(養)。
    - Tā shòu shāng de zhǐ xū yào jìng yǎng.
    - His injured foot needs adequate rest.
  - 他走路时(時)小心谨(謹)慎，因为(爲)止若受伤(傷)便难(難)前行。
    - Tā zǒu lù shí xiǎo xīn jǐn shèn, yīn wèi zhǐ ruò shòu shāng biàn nán qián xíng.
    - He walks carefully because if his foot gets injured, it becomes difficult to move forward.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 止](@media/glyph6b62.png)
### 有时(時) → 时(時) → 寺 → 𡳿 → 止 → 趾
- **definition:** foot
- **pinyin:** zhǐ
- **components:**
  - 足
    - zú
    - foot
  - 止
    - zhǐ
    - halt
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic 足 (zú, "foot") + phonetic 止 (zhǐ) ->
    - toe
  - **interpretation:** The character combines 足 (zú, "foot"), indicating the general area involved, with 止 (zhǐ) providing the sound and potentially suggesting the idea of a part of the foot that 'halts' or 'stops' progression, which naturally leads to the notion of a toe.
- **examples:**
  - 他的脚(腳)趾受伤(傷)了。
    - Tā de jiǎozhǐ shòushāng le.
    - His toe is injured.
  - 她用脚(腳)趾轻(輕)轻(輕)地踢了一下球。
    - Tā yòng jiǎozhǐ qīngqīng de tī le yīxià qiú.
    - She gently kicked the ball with her toe.
  - 在沙滩(灘)上散步时(時)，我感受到沙子在我的脚(腳)趾间(間)流动(動)。
    - Zài shātān shàng sànbù shí, wǒ gǎnshòu dào shāzi zài wǒ de jiǎozhǐ jiān liúdòng.
    - While walking on the beach, I felt the sand flowing between my toes.
### 有时(時) → 时(時) → 寺 → 𡳿 → 止 → 龰
- **definition:** stylized feet
- **pinyin:** yù
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a stylized footprint pointing upward ->
    - originally meaning 'foot' ->
    - later forms like 趾 (zhǐ, 'toe') refer back to original meaning
  - **interpretation:** 龰 (yù, 'stylized feet') is a pictogram showing a footprint pointing up, originally indicating the concept of a foot. The character 趾 (zhǐ, 'toe') evolved from this and retains the reference to the original meaning. It visually resembles a sole with three toes, similar to representations of the human hand in characters like 爪 (zhuǎ, 'claw'), 寸 (cùn, 'inch'), and 又 (yòu, 'again').
### 有时(時) → 时(時) → 寺 → 𡳿 → 止 → 手
- **definition:** hand
- **pinyin:** shǒu
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a hand with fingers; top stroke is a bent over middle finger, horizontal strokes represent fingers
  - **interpretation:** The character 手 (shǒu, "hand") is a direct pictorial representation of a human hand with all five fingers, which distinguishes it from similar characters representing claws or simplified fingers. This visually conveys its meaning as a hand clearly.
- **examples:**
  - 他用手写(寫)字。
    - Tā yòng shǒu xiě zì.
    - He writes with his hand.
  - 妈(媽)妈(媽)牵(牽)着(著)我的手走路。
    - Māmā qiān zhe wǒ de shǒu zǒu lù.
    - Mom holds my hand while walking.
  - 他的手很温(溫)暖，带(帶)给(給)我力量。
    - Tā de shǒu hěn wēn nuǎn, dài gěi wǒ lìliàng.
    - His hand is very warm, giving me strength.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 手](@media/glyph624b.png)
### 有时(時) → 时(時) → 寺 → 𡳿 → 一
- **definition:** the beginning place
- **pinyin:** yī
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogram
  - **description:** A horizontal stroke representing the concept of 'one'.
  - **interpretation:** The character 一(yī, "one") is a simple horizontal line signifying the singular and unified concept of 'one'. It directly represents being singular or the number one.
- **examples:**
  - 我有一个(個)苹(蘋)果。
    - Wǒ yǒu yī gè píngguǒ.
    - I have one apple.
  - 他只看到一只(隻)鸟(鳥)，飞(飛)进(進)了花园(園)。
    - Tā zhǐ kàn dào yī zhī niǎo, fēi jìn le huā yuán.
    - He only saw one bird, which flew into the garden.
  - 一条(條)直路通向远(遠)方。
    - Yī tiáo zhí lù tōng xiàng yuǎn fāng.
    - One straight road leads to the distance.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 一](@media/glyph4e00.png)
### 有时(時) → 时(時) → 寺 → 𡳿 → 之
- **definition:** to go
- **pinyin:** zhī
- **components:**
  - 止
    - zhǐ
    - foot
  - 一
    - yī
    - one; the beginning place
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogrammic compound
  - **description:**
    - 止 ('foot') + 一 ('beginning place') ->
    - originally 㞢 ('to go') ->
    - simplified to a point
  - **interpretation:** The original compound 㞢 depicted a foot 止 (zhǐ, 'foot') stepping on a line 一 (yī, 'one; the beginning place'), indicating the concept of 'to go'. The footprint evolving into a point symbolized direction or movement, ultimately abstracted into 之 (zhī, 'of; possessive particle'), representing directionality or connection, as in 'of'.
- **examples:**
  - 天空之蓝(藍)让(讓)人心旷(曠)神怡。
    - Tiānkōng zhī lán ràng rén xīnkuàngshényí.
    - The blue of the sky makes people feel relaxed and happy.
  - 树(樹)之影在湖面上摇(搖)曳。
    - Shù zhī yǐng zài húmiàn shàng yáoyè.
    - The shadow of the tree sways on the surface of the lake.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 之](@media/glyph4e4b.png)
### 有时(時) → 时(時) → 寺 → 寸
- **definition:** inch
- **pinyin:** cùn
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogram
  - **description:**
    - Line on the hand (ideographic) emphasizing the elbow ->
    - represents measurement unit between wrist and specific forearm position ->
    - meaning 'inch'
  - **interpretation:** 寸 (cùn, "inch") originated as a depiction of a line on the hand, indicating the area near the elbow. This specific placement was considered significant for pulse palpation, originally suggesting a forearm position, which then came to denote the measurement 'inch'.
- **examples:**
  - 这(這)块(塊)布每一寸都是精心制(製)作。
    - Zhè kuài bù měi yī cùn dōu shì jīngxīn zhìzuò.
    - Every inch of this cloth is crafted with care.
  - 请(請)用卷尺量一寸，每一寸数(數)据(據)都准(準)确(確)。
    - Qǐng yòng juǎnchǐ liàng yī cùn, měi yī cùn shùjù dōu zhǔnquè.
    - Please use a tape measure to measure an inch, every inch's data is accurate.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 寸](@media/glyph5bf8.png)

## 出现(現)
---
## appear
### chūxiàn
---
- **traditional:** 出現
- **definition:** appear
- **pinyin:** chūxiàn
- **components:**
  - 出
    - chū
    - go out; exit
  - 现(現)
    - xiàn
    - appear; present
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** compound word
  - **description:** 出 (chū, "go out; exit") and 現 (xiàn, "appear; present") together describe the act of coming into view or becoming visible.
  - **interpretation:** This word combines 出 (chū, "go out") with 現 (xiàn, "appear"), suggesting the action of emerging or manifesting into view, akin to 'coming out and becoming present'.
- **examples:**
  - 天空中出现(現)了彩虹。
    - Tiānkōng zhōng chūxiàn le cǎihóng.
    - A rainbow appeared in the sky.
  - 问(問)题(題)又出现(現)了，需要立即解决(決)。
    - Wèntí yòu chūxiàn le, xūyào lìjí jiějué.
    - The problem appeared again and needs to be resolved immediately.
  - 每当(當)他出现(現)时(時)，大家都会(會)很高兴(興)。
    - Měidāng tā chūxiàn shí, dàjiā dōu huì hěn gāoxìng.
    - Whenever he appears, everyone is very happy.
### 出现(現) → 出
- **definition:** go out; exit
- **pinyin:** chū
- **components:**
  - 止
    - zhǐ
    - foot
  - 凵
    - kǎn
    - cave
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogrammic compound
  - **description:**
    - 止 (zhǐ, "foot") + 凵 (kǎn, "cave") =
    - to step out of a cave ->
    - to exit
  - **interpretation:** The original depiction involved a foot 止 (zhǐ, "foot") stepping out of a cave 凵 (kǎn, "cave"), representing the act of exiting or going out. This visual concept naturally conveys the meaning of leaving an enclosed space.
- **examples:**
  - 我每天早上出门(門)。
    - Wǒ měitiān zǎoshang chūmén.
    - I go out every morning.
  - 他出去了，给(給)我留下了一封信。
    - Tā chūqù le, gěi wǒ liúxià le yī fēng xìn.
    - He went out and left me a letter.
  - 晚上出门(門)需要小心。
    - Wǎnshang chūmén xūyào xiǎoxīn.
    - Going out at night requires caution.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 出](@media/glyph51fa.png)
### 出现(現) → 出 → 止
- **definition:** foot
- **pinyin:** zhǐ
- **components:**
  - 趾
    - zhǐ
    - foot
  - 龰
    - yù
    - stylized feet
  - 手
    - shǒu
    - hand
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Original: Foot pointing up with 3 toes and a sole ->
    - Stylized as 龰 ->
    - Derivative 趾 refers to original 'foot' meaning
  - **interpretation:** Originally depicting a footprint with toes and a sole, 止 (zhǐ, "foot") represents the foot. The character's form resembles a foot with three toes, analogous to how the hand is represented with fingers in other characters.
- **examples:**
  - 他受伤(傷)的止需要静(靜)养(養)。
    - Tā shòu shāng de zhǐ xū yào jìng yǎng.
    - His injured foot needs adequate rest.
  - 他走路时(時)小心谨(謹)慎，因为(爲)止若受伤(傷)便难(難)前行。
    - Tā zǒu lù shí xiǎo xīn jǐn shèn, yīn wèi zhǐ ruò shòu shāng biàn nán qián xíng.
    - He walks carefully because if his foot gets injured, it becomes difficult to move forward.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 止](@media/glyph6b62.png)
### 出现(現) → 出 → 止 → 趾
- **definition:** foot
- **pinyin:** zhǐ
- **components:**
  - 足
    - zú
    - foot
  - 止
    - zhǐ
    - halt
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic 足 (zú, "foot") + phonetic 止 (zhǐ) ->
    - toe
  - **interpretation:** The character combines 足 (zú, "foot"), indicating the general area involved, with 止 (zhǐ) providing the sound and potentially suggesting the idea of a part of the foot that 'halts' or 'stops' progression, which naturally leads to the notion of a toe.
- **examples:**
  - 他的脚(腳)趾受伤(傷)了。
    - Tā de jiǎozhǐ shòushāng le.
    - His toe is injured.
  - 她用脚(腳)趾轻(輕)轻(輕)地踢了一下球。
    - Tā yòng jiǎozhǐ qīngqīng de tī le yīxià qiú.
    - She gently kicked the ball with her toe.
  - 在沙滩(灘)上散步时(時)，我感受到沙子在我的脚(腳)趾间(間)流动(動)。
    - Zài shātān shàng sànbù shí, wǒ gǎnshòu dào shāzi zài wǒ de jiǎozhǐ jiān liúdòng.
    - While walking on the beach, I felt the sand flowing between my toes.
### 出现(現) → 出 → 止 → 趾 → 足
- **definition:** foot
- **pinyin:** zú
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a leg ->
    - originally depicted as ⽦ ->
    - represents 'foot'
  - **interpretation:** The character 足(zú, 'foot') is a pictographic representation of a human leg, which directly portrays the concept of a 'foot'. The pictographic origin emphasizes its fundamental meaning in the language.
- **examples:**
  - 他受伤(傷)后(後)，他的足不能动(動)。
    - tā shòushāng hòu, tā de zú bù néng dòng。
    - After he was injured, his foot couldn't move.
  - 小明打球时(時)，不小心扭伤(傷)了足。
    - xiǎo míng dǎ qiú shí, bù xiǎoxīn niǔ shāng le zú。
    - When Xiaoming was playing ball, he accidentally twisted his foot.
  - 我每天锻(鍛)炼(鍊)足部。
    - wǒ měitiān duànliàn zúbù。
    - I exercise my foot muscles every day.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 足](@media/glyph8db3.png)
### 出现(現) → 出 → 止 → 龰
- **definition:** stylized feet
- **pinyin:** yù
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a stylized footprint pointing upward ->
    - originally meaning 'foot' ->
    - later forms like 趾 (zhǐ, 'toe') refer back to original meaning
  - **interpretation:** 龰 (yù, 'stylized feet') is a pictogram showing a footprint pointing up, originally indicating the concept of a foot. The character 趾 (zhǐ, 'toe') evolved from this and retains the reference to the original meaning. It visually resembles a sole with three toes, similar to representations of the human hand in characters like 爪 (zhuǎ, 'claw'), 寸 (cùn, 'inch'), and 又 (yòu, 'again').
### 出现(現) → 出 → 止 → 手
- **definition:** hand
- **pinyin:** shǒu
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a hand with fingers; top stroke is a bent over middle finger, horizontal strokes represent fingers
  - **interpretation:** The character 手 (shǒu, "hand") is a direct pictorial representation of a human hand with all five fingers, which distinguishes it from similar characters representing claws or simplified fingers. This visually conveys its meaning as a hand clearly.
- **examples:**
  - 他用手写(寫)字。
    - Tā yòng shǒu xiě zì.
    - He writes with his hand.
  - 妈(媽)妈(媽)牵(牽)着(著)我的手走路。
    - Māmā qiān zhe wǒ de shǒu zǒu lù.
    - Mom holds my hand while walking.
  - 他的手很温(溫)暖，带(帶)给(給)我力量。
    - Tā de shǒu hěn wēn nuǎn, dài gěi wǒ lìliàng.
    - His hand is very warm, giving me strength.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 手](@media/glyph624b.png)
### 出现(現) → 出 → 凵
- **definition:** cave
- **pinyin:** kǎn
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a cave
  - **interpretation:** The character 凵 (kǎn, "container") visually represents the shape of a cave, which is an enclosure or hollow space. This depiction is straightforward, illustrating the basic meaning through a simple, open-bottomed rectangular shape.
- **examples:**
  - 这(這)个(個)凵足以盛放鲜(鮮)花。
    - Zhège kǎn zúyǐ shèngfàng xiānhuā.
    - This container is sufficient for holding fresh flowers.
  - 妈(媽)妈(媽)买(買)了一个(個)大凵，用来(來)给(給)花浇(澆)水。
    - Māmā mǎile yīgè dà kǎn, yòng lái gěi huā jiāoshuǐ.
    - Mom bought a big container to water the flowers.
  - 老店里(裡)展示了古代的凵，象征(徵)着(著)智慧和传(傳)承。
    - Lǎo diàn lǐ zhǎnshì le gǔdài de kǎn, xiàngzhēngzhe zhìhuì hé chuánchéng.
    - The old shop displayed an ancient container, symbolizing wisdom and heritage.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 凵](@media/glyph51f5.png)
### 出现(現) → 现(現)
- **traditional:** 現
- **definition:** appear; present
- **pinyin:** xiàn
- **components:**
  - 玉
    - yù
    - jade
  - 見
    - jiàn
    - see
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic 玉 (yù, "jade") + phonetic 見 (jiàn, "see") ->
    - to appear
  - **interpretation:** 現 (jiàn, "see") acts as the phonetic component indicating pronunciation, while the semantic component 玉 (yù, "jade") suggests something valuable or significant that becomes visible, leading to the meaning 'to appear; now'.
  - **simplification:** 現 was simplified to 现(現) by replacing the semantic component 見 (jiàn, "see") with its simplified form 见.
- **examples:**
  - 现(現)在是时(時)候出发(發)了。
    - Xiànzài shì shíhòu chūfā le.
    - Now is the time to depart.
  - 他突然出现(現)在门(門)口。
    - Tā tūrán chūxiàn zài ménkǒu.
    - He suddenly appeared at the door.
  - 这(這)幅画(畫)在博物馆(館)中展现(現)。
    - Zhè fú huà zài bówùguǎn zhōng zhǎnxiàn.
    - This painting is exhibited in the museum.
### 出现(現) → 现(現) → 玉
- **definition:** jade
- **pinyin:** yù
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a picture of a cong (琮), a sort of ritual jade totem ->
    - dot added to differentiate from 王 (wáng, "king") ->
    - final form 玉 (yù, "jade")
  - **interpretation:** The character represents a picture of a jade cong, emphasizing its role in rituals and its cultural significance. The image eventually included a distinguishing dot to ensure clarity from similar characters like 王, underscoring the value jade held as a material in ancient contexts.
- **examples:**
  - 她收到了一个漂亮的玉手镯(鐲)。
    - Tā shōu dào le yī gè piàoliang de yù shǒuzhuó.
    - She received a beautiful jade bracelet.
  - 皇帝的王冠上镶(鑲)嵌着(著)闪(閃)耀的玉石。
    - Huángdì de wángguān shàng xiāngqiànzhe shǎnyào de yùshí.
    - The emperor's crown was inlaid with shining jade stones.
  - 古代的玉器常常被视(視)为(為)珍贵(貴)的艺(藝)术(術)品。
    - Gǔdài de yùqì chángcháng bèi shìwéi zhēnguì de yìshùpǐn.
    - Ancient jade artifacts are often regarded as precious works of art.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 玉](@media/glyph7389.png)
### 出现(現) → 现(現) → 見
- **definition:** see
- **pinyin:** jiàn
- **components:**
  - 目
    - mù
    - eye
  - 卩
    - jié
    - kneeling person
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogrammic compound
  - **description:**
    - 目 (mù, "eye") + 卩 (jié, "kneeling person") =
    - a kneeling figure with large eye ->
    - see
  - **interpretation:** The combination of a human figure and an eye visually represents the act of seeing. The eye symbolizes vision, while the person emphasizes the human context of this action, making the meaning intuitive.
  - **simplification:** 见(見) is derived from using a cursive variant of the character in place of the traditional form.
- **examples:**
  - 我昨天见(見)到她。
    - Wǒ zuótiān jiàn dào tā.
    - I saw her yesterday.
  - 太阳(陽)升起时(時)，我看见(見)了大海。
    - Tàiyáng shēng qǐ shí, wǒ kàn jiàn le dàhǎi.
    - When the sun rose, I saw the sea.
  - 在公园(園)里(裡)，我见(見)到了老朋友。
    - Zài gōngyuán lǐ, wǒ jiàn dào le lǎo péngyǒu.
    - In the park, I met an old friend.

### 出现(現) → 现(現) → 見 → 目
- **definition:** eye
- **pinyin:** mù
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a human eye, now represented and rotated 90 degrees ->
    - eye
  - **interpretation:** The character 目(mù, 'eye') is a pictogram representing a human eye. Its original orientation has changed over time, resembling an eye seen from a sideways view.
- **examples:**
  - 他的目光炯炯有神。
    - Tā de mùguāng jiǒngjiǒng yǒu shén.
    - His gaze is bright and full of spirit.
  - 她目不转(轉)睛，注视(視)前方。
    - Tā mù bù zhuǎn jīng, zhùshì qiánfāng.
    - She stared intently, gazing ahead.
  - 雄鹰(鷹)展翅，双(雙)目炯炯看天际(際)。
    - Xióng yīng zhǎn chì, shuāng mù jiǒngjiǒng kàn tiānjì.
    - The eagle spreads its wings, its eyes piercingly gaze at the horizon.

![Historical forms of 目](@media/glyph76ee.png)
### 出现(現) → 现(現) → 見 → 卩
- **definition:** kneeling person
- **pinyin:** jié
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a kneeling person from sideview
  - **interpretation:** The character 卩 (jié, "kneeling person") is a simple pictogram showing the silhouette of a person kneeling. It is unrelated to other kneeling or similar figures in different contexts such as 欠 (qiàn, "yawn") where the mouth is open, or 女 (nǚ, "woman") where the figure represents a female. Its form is solely based on the posture of kneeling.
- **examples:**
  - 那位卩正虔诚(誠)祈祷(禱)。
    - Nà wèi jié zhèng qiánchéng qídǎo.
    - That kneeling person is praying devoutly.
  - 礼(禮)仪(儀)师(師)指出，卩代表谦(謙)卑与(與)敬意。
    - Lǐyí shī zhǐchū, jié dàibiǎo qiānbēi yǔ jìngyì.
    - The ritual master pointed out that the kneeling person represents humility and respect.
  - 在庄(莊)严(嚴)仪(儀)式中，卩象征(徵)着(著)内(內)心的虔敬。
    - Zài zhuāngyán yíshì zhōng, jié xiàngzhēngzhe nèixīn de qiánjìng.
    - In the solemn ceremony, the kneeling figure symbolizes inner devotion.

## 比
---
## than; (superior or inferior) to
### bǐ
---
- **definition:** than; (superior or inferior) to
- **pinyin:** bǐ
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Two figures standing side by side ->
    - concept of comparison
  - **interpretation:** The character 比(bǐ, "compare") depicts two human figures standing side by side, illustrating the act of comparing one thing to another. It's a visual representation that captures the idea of juxtaposition and evaluation.
- **examples:**
  - 他比我跑得快。
    - Tā bǐ wǒ pǎo de kuài.
    - He runs faster than I do.
  - 这(這)件衣服比那件衣服便宜。
    - Zhè jiàn yīfu bǐ nà jiàn yīfu piányí.
    - This piece of clothing is cheaper than that one.
  - 他比我聪(聰)明，而且比她勤奋(奮)。
    - Tā bǐ wǒ cōngmíng, érqiě bǐ tā qínfèn.
    - He is smarter than I am, and also more hardworking than she is.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 比](@media/glyph6bd4.png)

## 比
### bǐ
---
## than; (superior or inferior) to
%%%
## 矮
---
## short (of stature)
### ǎi
---
- **definition:** short (of stature)
- **pinyin:** ǎi
- **components:**
  - 矢
    - shǐ
    - arrow
  - 委
    - wěi
    - to entrust
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic 矢 (shǐ, "arrow") + phonetic 委 (wěi) ->
    - short (of stature)
  - **interpretation:** 矢 (shǐ, "arrow") suggests something being straight and upright, while 委 (wěi) gives the sound. The use of an arrow, typically straight and long, juxtaposed in a context meaning 'short,' emphasizes a comparative sense of lower stature.
- **examples:**
  - 他的身材很矮。
    - Tā de shēncái hěn ǎi.
    - He is very short in stature.
  - 虽(雖)然他很矮，但他在篮(籃)球队(隊)里(裏)表现(現)出色。
    - Suīrán tā hěn ǎi, dàn tā zài lánqiú duì lǐ biǎoxiàn chūsè.
    - Although he is short, he performs excellently in the basketball team.
  - 那个(個)女孩比她的妹妹矮一些。
    - Nàgè nǚhái bǐ tā de mèimei ǎi yīxiē.
    - That girl is a bit shorter than her sister.
### 矮 → 矢
- **definition:** arrow
- **pinyin:** shǐ
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts an arrow
  - **interpretation:** The character 矢(shǐ, 'arrow') is a pictogram representing an arrow. Its resemblance to arrows was more evident in ancient script forms.
- **examples:**
  - 他拉开(開)弓，射出一支矢。
    - Tā lā kāi gōng, shè chū yī zhī shǐ.
    - He drew his bow and released an arrow.
  - 古代战(戰)士用矢，攻破敌(敵)阵(陣)。
    - Gǔdài zhànshì yòng shǐ, gōng pò dí zhèn.
    - Ancient warriors used arrows to breach enemy formations.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 矢](@media/glyph77e2.png)
### 矮 → 委
- **definition:** to entrust
- **pinyin:** wěi
- **components:**
  - 禾
    - hé
    - grain
  - 女
    - nǚ
    - woman
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - phonetic 禾 (hé, "grain") + semantic 女 (nǚ, "woman") ->
    - entrust
  - **interpretation:** The character 委 combines 禾 (hé, "grain") as the phonetic component to suggest sound, with 女 (nǚ, "woman") as the semantic component. Originally, the oracle bone representation used 𠃊, depicting a figure kneeling, which aligns with the idea of yielding or resigning. Hence, the combination implies entrusting or assigning a task, as one might with a trusted companion or subordinate.
- **examples:**
  - 我把重要的任务(務)委托(託)给(給)他。
    - Wǒ bǎ zhòngyào de rènwù wěituō gěi tā.
    - I entrusted the important task to him.
  - 经(經)理委任了一名新助理。
    - Jīnglǐ wěirèn le yī míng xīn zhùlǐ.
    - The manager appointed a new assistant.
  - 她被公司委以重任。
    - Tā bèi gōngsī wěi yǐ zhòngrèn.
    - She was entrusted with significant responsibilities by the company.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 委](@media/glyph59d4.png)
### 矮 → 委 → 禾
- **definition:** grain
- **pinyin:** hé
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a stalk of grain or cereal plant
  - **interpretation:** The character 禾 (hé, 'grain') visually represents a plant with roots and leaves, focusing on the appearance of staple crops like rice or millet. This clearly conveys its meaning as it resembles the actual shape of a plant grown for its grain.
- **examples:**
  - 收获(穫)的禾香弥(彌)漫在田野中。
    - Shōuhuò de hé xiāng mímàn zài tiányě zhōng.
    - The fragrance of grain filled the fields.
  - 农(農)民辛勤耕作，收割禾穗。
    - Nóngmín xīnqín gēngzuò, shōugē hé suì.
    - The hardworking farmers harvested the ears of grain.
  - 春雨滋润(潤)了禾苗，预(預)示着(著)丰(豐)收。
    - Chūnyǔ zīrùn le hé miáo, yùshì zhe fēngshōu.
    - The spring rain nourished the grain seedlings, foreshadowing a bountiful harvest.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 禾](@media/glyph79be.png)
### 矮 → 委 → 女
- **definition:** woman
- **pinyin:** nǚ
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a woman kneeling or standing ->
    - enclosed area as remnant of right breast
  - **interpretation:** The character 女(nǚ, "woman") is a pictogram originally depicting a woman with highlighted bodily features, such as the breasts, symbolizing femininity. Its orientation changed from the Oracle Bone script to face right, simplifying over time while still retaining the essence of its original depiction.
- **examples:**
  - 那位才华(華)横(橫)溢的女，赢(贏)得了全场(場)注目。
    - Nà wèi cáihuá héngyì de nǚ, yíng dé le quánchǎng zhùmù.
    - That talented woman won everyone's attention.
  - 古时(時)候‘女’常被用来(來)象征(徵)温(溫)柔，而如今它代表独(獨)立自信。
    - Gǔshíhòu ‘nǚ’ cháng bèi yòng lái xiàngzhēng wēnróu, ér rújīn tā dàibiǎo dúlì zìxìn.
    - In ancient times, the character '女' was often used to symbolize gentleness, whereas today it represents independence and confidence.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 女](@media/glyph5973.png)

## 双(雙)
---
## pair
### shuāng
---
- **traditional:** 雙
- **definition:** pair
- **pinyin:** shuāng
- **components:**
  - 雔
    - chóu
    - two birds
  - 又
    - yòu
    - hand
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogrammic compound
  - **description:**
    - 雔 (two birds) + 又 (hand) =
    - holding two birds in hand ->
    - pair
  - **interpretation:** The character depicts two birds (雔) held together by a hand (又), creating the image of a pair of birds, which conveys the meaning of 'pair' or 'double'. The concept of holding a pair of something is naturally associated with 'pair', reinforcing the meaning.
  - **simplification:** The traditional form 䨇 underwent simplification by eliminating the 雔 component, leading to the modern form 双 that retains the notion of duplicity through duplication of 又.
- **examples:**
  - 她买(買)了一双(雙)新鞋。
    - Tā mǎi le yī shuāng xīn xié.
    - She bought a new pair of shoes.
  - 我们(們)各吃了两(兩)个(個)苹(蘋)果，一人一双(雙)。
    - Wǒmen gè chī le liǎng gè píngguǒ, yī rén yī shuāng.
    - We each ate two apples, one pair per person.
  - 他给(給)我买(買)了一双(雙)手套，因为(為)天气(氣)冷了。
    - Tā gěi wǒ mǎi le yī shuāng shǒutào, yīnwèi tiānqì lěng le.
    - He bought me a pair of gloves because it's getting cold.
### 双(雙) → 雔
- **definition:** two birds
- **pinyin:** chóu
- **components:**
  - 隹
    - zhuī
    - short-tailed bird
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogrammic compound
  - **description:**
    - 隹 (zhuī, 'short-tailed bird') + 隹 (zhuī, 'short-tailed bird') =
    - two birds together ->
    - representation of gathering or flocking of birds
  - **interpretation:** The character represents two birds together, emphasizing the idea of a pair or group of birds. The repetition of 隹 (zhuī, 'short-tailed bird') suggests a flock or gathering, visually and conceptually reinforcing the notion of multiple birds.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 雔](@media/glyph96d4.png)
### 双(雙) → 雔 → 隹
- **definition:** short-tailed bird
- **pinyin:** zhuī
- **components:**
  - 鷕
    - yǎo
    - cry of a bird
  - 唯
    - wéi
    - only
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a short‐tailed bird (e.g., a sparrow) ->
    - also original form of 唯 (wéi, "only") before evolution into 鷕 (yǎo, "cry of a bird")
  - **interpretation:** 隹 (zhuī, "short-tailed bird") is a pictogram representing a bird with a short tail. Its depiction served as the foundation for other characters related to birds, such as 鷕 (yǎo, "cry of a bird").
- **examples:**
  - 这(這)只短尾的隹在树(樹)林中飞(飛)翔。
    - Zhè zhī duǎnwěi de zhuī zài shùlín zhōng fēixiáng.
    - This short-tailed bird flies in the forest.
  - 博物馆(館)里(裡)展出了一件以隹为(為)题(題)材的古代绘(繪)画(畫)。
    - Bówùguǎn lǐ zhǎnchūle yī jiàn yǐ zhuī wèi tícái de gǔdài huìhuà.
    - The museum displays an ancient painting themed on the short-tailed bird.
  - 远(遠)古诗(詩)篇中常用隹来(來)象征(徵)自由，寓意生动(動)。
    - Yuǎngǔ shīpiān zhōng cháng yòng zhuī lái xiàngzhēng zìyóu, yùyì shēngdòng.
    - In ancient poems, the short-tailed bird is often used to symbolize freedom, conveying vivid meaning.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 隹](@media/glyph96b9.png)
### 双(雙) → 雔 → 隹 → 鷕
- **definition:** cry of a bird
- **pinyin:** yǎo
- **components:**
  - 唯
    - wéi
    - only
  - 鳥
    - niǎo
    - bird
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - 唯 (phonetic) + 鳥 (semantic, "bird") ->
    - cry of a bird
  - **interpretation:** The character combines 唯 (wéi, used phonetically for its sound) with 鳥 (niǎo, "bird") to denote the specific sound relating to a bird's cry.
### 双(雙) → 雔 → 隹 → 鷕 → 唯
- **definition:** only
- **pinyin:** wéi
- **components:**
  - 口
    - kǒu
    - mouth
  - 隹
    - zhuī
    - short-tailed bird
  - 鷕
    - yǎo
    - cry of a bird
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic 口 (kǒu, "mouth") + phonetic 隹 (zhuī, "short-tailed bird") ->
    - original form of 鷕 ->
    - borrowed phonetically for 'only'
  - **interpretation:** The character 唯 originally represented the cry of a bird, with the mouth radical indicating the sound aspect. It was later phonetically borrowed for the abstract meaning 'only', without retaining its original context related to bird sounds.
- **examples:**
  - 唯有努力，才能成功。
    - Wéi yǒu nǔlì, cái néng chénggōng.
    - Only by working hard can one succeed.
  - 唯有在安静(靜)的夜晚，我才能听(聽)清自己的心声(聲)。
    - Wéi yǒu zài ānjìng de yèwǎn, wǒ cái néng tīng qīng zìjǐ de xīnshēng.
    - Only in the quiet of the night can I hear my own heart.
  - 我唯爱(愛)读(讀)书(書)，因为(為)书(書)籍能带(帶)给(給)我无(無)限的可能。
    - Wǒ wéi ài dúshū, yīnwèi shūjí néng dài gěi wǒ wúxiàn de kěnéng.
    - I only love reading, because books bring me infinite possibilities.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 唯](@media/glyph552f.png)
### 双(雙) → 雔 → 隹 → 鷕 → 唯 → 口
- **definition:** mouth
- **pinyin:** kǒu
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts an open mouth.
  - **interpretation:** The character 口(kǒu, 'mouth') is a straightforward pictogram that visually represents an open mouth. It is a fundamental character in the Chinese language, often used both as an independent word and as a component in more complex characters, lending a semantic association to ideas relating to speech, openings, or enclosures.
- **examples:**
  - 他张(張)开(開)口，大声(聲)喊叫。
    - Tā zhāngkāi kǒu, dàshēng hǎnjiào.
    - He opened his mouth and shouted loudly.
  - 这(這)口饭(飯)入口即化。
    - Zhè kǒu fàn rùkǒu jíhuà.
    - This mouthful of food melts in your mouth.
  - 小女孩咬了一口苹(蘋)果，露出甜美的笑容。
    - Xiǎo nǚhái yǎole yī kǒu píngguǒ, lùchū tiánměi de xiàoróng.
    - The little girl took a bite of the apple and smiled sweetly.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 口](@media/glyph53e3.png)
### 双(雙) → 雔 → 隹 → 鷕 → 鳥
- **definition:** bird
- **pinyin:** niǎo
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a bird with a prominent beak and tail feathers
  - **interpretation:** The character 鳥 (niǎo, "bird") visually represents a bird, featuring distinct elements such as a beak and tail feathers, capturing its essence through its graphical form.
- **examples:**
  - 花园(園)里(裡)有许(許)多鸟(鳥)，在空中翱翔。
    - Huāyuán lǐ yǒu xǔduō niǎo, zài kōngzhōng áoxiáng.
    - Many birds soar in the garden.
  - 树(樹)林中有一只(隻)鸟(鳥)，在枝头(頭)跳跃(躍)。
    - Shùlín zhōng yǒu yī zhī niǎo, zài zhītóu tiàoyuè.
    - A bird hops on a branch in the forest.
  - 海边(邊)的天空中飞(飛)翔着(著)鸟(鳥)。
    - Hǎibiān de tiānkōng zhōng fēixiáng zhe niǎo.
    - A bird soars in the sky by the seaside.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 鳥](@media/glyph9ce5.png)
### 双(雙) → 又
- **definition:** hand
- **pinyin:** yòu
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a right hand
  - **interpretation:** The character 又 (yòu, "hand") is a pictogram representing a right hand, showing the fingers and palm, which highlights its original meaning related to manual actions.
- **examples:**
  - 「又」这(這)个(個)字最早来(來)源于(於)手。
    - 「Yòu」 zhè gè zì zuì zǎo láiyuán yú shǒu。
    - The character '又' originally comes from the hand.
  - 很多汉(漢)字含有又部首，表示与(與)手有关(關)的动(動)作。
    - Hěn duō hànzì hányǒu Yòu bùshǒu, biǎoshì yǔ shǒu yǒuguān de dòngzuò。
    - Many Chinese characters include the '又' radical, indicating actions related to the hand.
  - 古人用又描绘(繪)手的形态(態)，体(體)现(現)了古汉(漢)字的独(獨)特魅力。
    - Gǔrén yòng Yòu miáohuì shǒu de xíngtài, tǐxiàn le gǔ hànzì de dútè mèilì。
    - Ancient people used '又' to depict the shape of the hand, showcasing the unique charm of ancient Chinese characters.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 又](@media/glyph53c8.png)
