## 年级(級)
---
## grade; year (in school, etc.)
### niánjí
---
- **traditional:** 年級
- **definition:** grade; year (in school, etc.)
- **pinyin:** niánjí
- **components:**
  - 年
    - nián
    - year
  - 级(級)
    - jí
    - level; grade
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** compound word
  - **description:** 年 (nián, "year") + 級 (jí, "level; grade") forms a compound word that refers to a specific year level within educational systems, such as "grade" or "year" in school.
  - **interpretation:** 年 (nián, "year") indicates the passage of time, while 級 (jí, "level; grade") signifies a rank or stage in a sequence. Therefore, 年級 (niánjí, "grade; year") refers to a student's current stage or year in their educational journey.
- **examples:**
  - 他今年上五年级(級)。
    - Tā jīnnián shàng wǔ niánjí.
    - He is in the fifth grade this year.
  - 六年级(級)的学(學)生正在准(準)备(備)考试(試)。
    - Liù niánjí de xuéshēng zhèngzài zhǔnbèi kǎoshì.
    - The sixth-grade students are preparing for the exam.
  - 每个(個)年级(級)都有自己的活动(動)。
    - Měi gè niánjí dōu yǒu zìjǐ de huódòng.
    - Each grade has its own activities.
### 年级(級) → 年
- **definition:** year
- **pinyin:** nián
- **components:**
  - 禾
    - hé
    - grain
  - 人
    - rén
    - person
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - 禾(“wheat; grain”) + 人(“person”) as phonetic ->
    - originally “harvest” ->
    - later “year”
  - **interpretation:** The character 年 (nián, "year") originally depicted a harvest of grains, linking the concept of agricultural cycles with the passing of a year. Over time, the form evolved, retaining the semantic component 禾 (hé, "grain") and using 人 (rén, "person") for its phonetic sound in early stages, which later transformed into the current form through script evolution.
- **examples:**
  - 今年是兔年。
    - Jīnnián shì tùnián.
    - This year is the Year of the Rabbit.
  - 他今年二十岁(歲)。
    - Tā jīnnián èrshí suì.
    - He is twenty years old this year.
  - 五年后(後)我希望能去旅行。
    - Wǔ nián hòu wǒ xīwàng néng qù lǚxíng.
    - I hope to travel in five years.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 年](@media/glyph5e74.png)
### 年级(級) → 年 → 禾
- **definition:** grain
- **pinyin:** hé
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a stalk of grain or cereal plant
  - **interpretation:** The character 禾 (hé, 'grain') visually represents a plant with roots and leaves, focusing on the appearance of staple crops like rice or millet. This clearly conveys its meaning as it resembles the actual shape of a plant grown for its grain.
- **examples:**
  - 收获(穫)的禾香弥(彌)漫在田野中。
    - Shōuhuò de hé xiāng mímàn zài tiányě zhōng.
    - The fragrance of grain filled the fields.
  - 农(農)民辛勤耕作，收割禾穗。
    - Nóngmín xīnqín gēngzuò, shōugē hé suì.
    - The hardworking farmers harvested the ears of grain.
  - 春雨滋润(潤)了禾苗，预(預)示着(著)丰(豐)收。
    - Chūnyǔ zīrùn le hé miáo, yùshì zhe fēngshōu.
    - The spring rain nourished the grain seedlings, foreshadowing a bountiful harvest.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 禾](@media/glyph79be.png)
### 年级(級) → 年 → 人
- **definition:** person
- **pinyin:** rén
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts side view of a standing man, highlighting an arm and a leg ->
    - visual representation of a person
  - **interpretation:** The character 人 (rén, 'person') effectively uses simple lines to depict the essential form of a human, making it immediately recognizable and intuitive as meaning 'person.'
- **examples:**
  - 他是个(個)好人。
    - Tā shì gè hǎo rén.
    - He is a good person.
  - 每个(個)人都有责(責)任，为(為)社会(會)作出贡(貢)献(獻)。
    - Měi gè rén dōu yǒu zérèn, wèi shèhuì zuòchū gòngxiàn.
    - Every person has a responsibility to contribute to society.
  - 人在旅途中，心灵(靈)获(獲)得了成长(長)。
    - Rén zài lǚtú zhōng, xīnlíng huòdé le chéngzhǎng.
    - People gain growth along their journey.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 人](@media/glyph4eba.png)
### 年级(級) → 级(級)
- **traditional:** 級
- **definition:** level; grade
- **pinyin:** jí
- **components:**
  - 糹(糸)
    - mì
    - silk; thread
  - 及
    - jí
    - to reach
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic 糹 (mì, "silk; thread") + phonetic 及 (jí) ->
    - thread sequence ->
    - level; grade
  - **interpretation:** The character 級 (jí, "level; grade") combines 糹 (mì, "silk; thread") for the idea of a sequence, such as threads being arranged, with 及 (jí) providing the sound. The association with a sequence of threads leads to the concept of progression or arrangement, hence the meaning of level or grade.
  - **simplification:** 級 (jí, "level; grade") was simplified by replacing 糹 (mì, "silk; thread") with 纟 for ease of writing while retaining the other component 及 (jí).
- **examples:**
  - 学(學)生们(們)的成绩(績)很好，达(達)到了及格的级(級)别(別)。
    - Xuéshēngmen de chéngjī hěn hǎo, dádào le jígé de jíbié.
    - The students' grades are good, reaching a passing level.
  - 这(這)条(條)河流的水位已经(經)超过(過)了警戒级(級)别(別)。
    - Zhè tiáo héliú de shuǐwèi yǐjīng chāoguòle jǐngjiè jíbié.
    - The water level of this river has already exceeded the warning level.
  - 这(這)个(個)考试(試)分为(為)多个(個)难(難)度级(級)，学(學)生可以根据(據)自己的水平选(選)择(擇)。
    - Zhège kǎoshì fēn wéi duō gè nándù jí, xuéshēng kěyǐ gēnjù zìjǐ de shuǐpíng xuǎnzé.
    - This test is divided into multiple difficulty levels, and students can choose based on their own level.
### 年级(級) → 级(級) → 糹
- **definition:** silk; thread
- **pinyin:** mì
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts threads of silk arranged vertically, representing fine silk
  - **interpretation:** The character 糹 (mì, "fine silk") visually represents fine strands of silk with vertical lines suggesting the texture and thinness of silk threads.
  - **simplification:** The traditional form 糹 was simplified to 纟 by retaining only three vertical strokes, capturing the essence of silk threads.
- **examples:**
  - 这(這)种(種)糹制(製)作的衣服格外精美。
    - Zhè zhǒng mì zhìzuò de yīfú géwài jīngměi。
    - Clothes made from this fine silk are exceptionally exquisite.
  - 古代使用糹编(編)织(織)华(華)服，现(現)代依然欣赏(賞)糹质(質)的魅力。
    - Gǔdài shǐyòng mì biānzhī huáfú, xiàndài yírán xīnshǎng mì zhì de mèilì。
    - In ancient times, fine silk was used to weave splendid garments, and even today, its texture is admired.
### 年级(級) → 级(級) → 及
- **definition:** to reach
- **pinyin:** jí
- **components:**
  - 人
    - rén
    - person
  - 又
    - yòu
    - hand
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogrammic compound
  - **description:**
    - 人 (rén, "person") + 又 (yòu, "hand") =
    - a hand grabbing a person ->
    - to reach
  - **interpretation:** The character 及(jí, "and; to reach") combines 人 (rén, "person") with 又 (yòu, "hand") to depict the idea of a hand catching up to or reaching for a person. This visual metaphor effectively communicates the concept of reaching or arriving at something.
- **examples:**
  - 他的表现(現)及格了。
    - Tā de biǎoxiàn jígé le.
    - His performance reached the passing mark.
  - 会(會)议(議)时(時)间(間)及地点(點)会(會)提前通知。
    - Huìyì shíjiān jí dìdiǎn huì tíqián tōngzhī.
    - The meeting time and location will be notified in advance.
  - 我们(們)可以提供餐饮(飲)及住宿服务(務)。
    - Wǒmen kěyǐ tígōng cānyǐn jí zhùsù fúwù.
    - We can provide catering and accommodation services.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 及](@media/glyph53ca.png)
### 年级(級) → 级(級) → 及 → 人
- **definition:** person
- **pinyin:** rén
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts side view of a standing man, highlighting an arm and a leg ->
    - visual representation of a person
  - **interpretation:** The character 人 (rén, 'person') effectively uses simple lines to depict the essential form of a human, making it immediately recognizable and intuitive as meaning 'person.'
- **examples:**
  - 他是个(個)好人。
    - Tā shì gè hǎo rén.
    - He is a good person.
  - 每个(個)人都有责(責)任，为(為)社会(會)作出贡(貢)献(獻)。
    - Měi gè rén dōu yǒu zérèn, wèi shèhuì zuòchū gòngxiàn.
    - Every person has a responsibility to contribute to society.
  - 人在旅途中，心灵(靈)获(獲)得了成长(長)。
    - Rén zài lǚtú zhōng, xīnlíng huòdé le chéngzhǎng.
    - People gain growth along their journey.
- **historical forms:**

### 年级(級) → 级(級) → 及 → 又
- **definition:** hand
- **pinyin:** yòu
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a right hand
  - **interpretation:** The character 又 (yòu, "hand") is a pictogram representing a right hand, showing the fingers and palm, which highlights its original meaning related to manual actions.
- **examples:**
  - 「又」这(這)个(個)字最早来(來)源于(於)手。
    - 「Yòu」 zhè gè zì zuì zǎo láiyuán yú shǒu。
    - The character '又' originally comes from the hand.
  - 很多汉(漢)字含有又部首，表示与(與)手有关(關)的动(動)作。
    - Hěn duō hànzì hányǒu Yòu bùshǒu, biǎoshì yǔ shǒu yǒuguān de dòngzuò。
    - Many Chinese characters include the '又' radical, indicating actions related to the hand.
  - 古人用又描绘(繪)手的形态(態)，体(體)现(現)了古汉(漢)字的独(獨)特魅力。
    - Gǔrén yòng Yòu miáohuì shǒu de xíngtài, tǐxiàn le gǔ hànzì de dútè mèilì。
    - Ancient people used '又' to depict the shape of the hand, showcasing the unique charm of ancient Chinese characters.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 又](@media/glyph53c8.png)

## 年级(級)
### niánjí
---
## grade; year (in school, etc.)

## 年龄(齡)
---
## age (of a person, animal or plant, etc.)
### niánlíng
---
- **traditional:** 年齡
- **definition:** age (of a person, animal or plant, etc.)
- **pinyin:** niánlíng
- **components:**
  - 年
    - nián
    - year
  - 龄(齡)
    - líng
    - age
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** compound word
  - **description:** 年 (nián, "year") refers to the passage of time in terms of years, marking the cycle of seasons. 齡 (líng, "age") denotes the number of years a person, animal, or plant has lived, derived from the idea of teeth, which metaphorically reflects stages in life as teeth emerge in cycles across different age milestones.
  - **interpretation:** 年 (nián, "year") represents the passage of time as measured in increments of years, essential for counting the duration of life. 齡 (líng, "age") uses the metaphor of teeth, which grow and change in well-defined stages, to denote life stages; thus, 'age' is the count of annual cycles a being has experienced. Combining these gives 年齡 (niánlíng, "age") as the measure of how many year-cycles a person, animal, or plant has traversed.
- **examples:**
  - 他的年龄(齡)比我大。
    - Tā de niánlíng bǐ wǒ dà.
    - He is older than me.
  - 在这(這)个(個)年龄(齡)，开(開)始学(學)习(習)新东(東)西是很重要的。
    - Zài zhège niánlíng, kāishǐ xuéxí xīn dōngxī shì hěn zhòngyào de.
    - At this age, it is important to start learning new things.
  - 树(樹)的年龄(齡)可以通过(過)年轮(輪)来(來)判断(斷)。
    - Shù de niánlíng kěyǐ tōngguò niánlún lái pànduàn.
    - The age of a tree can be determined by its rings.
### 年龄(齡) → 年
- **definition:** year
- **pinyin:** nián
- **components:**
  - 禾
    - hé
    - grain
  - 人
    - rén
    - person
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - 禾(“wheat; grain”) + 人(“person”) as phonetic ->
    - originally “harvest” ->
    - later “year”
  - **interpretation:** The character 年 (nián, "year") originally depicted a harvest of grains, linking the concept of agricultural cycles with the passing of a year. Over time, the form evolved, retaining the semantic component 禾 (hé, "grain") and using 人 (rén, "person") for its phonetic sound in early stages, which later transformed into the current form through script evolution.
- **examples:**
  - 今年是兔年。
    - Jīnnián shì tùnián.
    - This year is the Year of the Rabbit.
  - 他今年二十岁(歲)。
    - Tā jīnnián èrshí suì.
    - He is twenty years old this year.
  - 五年后(後)我希望能去旅行。
    - Wǔ nián hòu wǒ xīwàng néng qù lǚxíng.
    - I hope to travel in five years.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 年](@media/glyph5e74.png)
### 年龄(齡) → 年 → 禾
- **definition:** grain
- **pinyin:** hé
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a stalk of grain or cereal plant
  - **interpretation:** The character 禾 (hé, 'grain') visually represents a plant with roots and leaves, focusing on the appearance of staple crops like rice or millet. This clearly conveys its meaning as it resembles the actual shape of a plant grown for its grain.
- **examples:**
  - 收获(穫)的禾香弥(彌)漫在田野中。
    - Shōuhuò de hé xiāng mímàn zài tiányě zhōng.
    - The fragrance of grain filled the fields.
  - 农(農)民辛勤耕作，收割禾穗。
    - Nóngmín xīnqín gēngzuò, shōugē hé suì.
    - The hardworking farmers harvested the ears of grain.
  - 春雨滋润(潤)了禾苗，预(預)示着(著)丰(豐)收。
    - Chūnyǔ zīrùn le hé miáo, yùshì zhe fēngshōu.
    - The spring rain nourished the grain seedlings, foreshadowing a bountiful harvest.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 禾](@media/glyph79be.png)
### 年龄(齡) → 年 → 人
- **definition:** person
- **pinyin:** rén
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts side view of a standing man, highlighting an arm and a leg ->
    - visual representation of a person
  - **interpretation:** The character 人 (rén, 'person') effectively uses simple lines to depict the essential form of a human, making it immediately recognizable and intuitive as meaning 'person.'
- **examples:**
  - 他是个(個)好人。
    - Tā shì gè hǎo rén.
    - He is a good person.
  - 每个(個)人都有责(責)任，为(為)社会(會)作出贡(貢)献(獻)。
    - Měi gè rén dōu yǒu zérèn, wèi shèhuì zuòchū gòngxiàn.
    - Every person has a responsibility to contribute to society.
  - 人在旅途中，心灵(靈)获(獲)得了成长(長)。
    - Rén zài lǚtú zhōng, xīnlíng huòdé le chéngzhǎng.
    - People gain growth along their journey.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 人](@media/glyph4eba.png)
### 年龄(齡) → 龄(齡)
- **traditional:** 齡
- **definition:** age
- **pinyin:** líng
- **components:**
  - 齒
    - chǐ
    - tooth
  - 令
    - lìng
    - order
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic 齒 (chǐ, "tooth") + phonetic 令 (lìng) ->
    - meaning related to counting years
  - **interpretation:** The character 齡 (líng, "age") is formed by combining 齒 (chǐ, "tooth"), which represents 'age' through the symbolism of teeth as a marker of maturity, with the phonetic 令 (lìng), which contributes the sound. Teeth are often associated with stages of life, lending themselves naturally to the concept of age or duration.
  - **simplification:** Simplified to 龄 by changing 齒 (chǐ, "tooth") to its simplified form 齿.
- **examples:**
  - 她的年龄(齡)不大。
    - Tā de niánlíng bù dà.
    - She is not very old.
  - 他的实(實)际(際)年龄(齡)比看起来(來)要大。
    - Tā de shíjì niánlíng bǐ kàn qǐlái yào dà.
    - His actual age is older than he looks.
  - 这(這)份工作的最低年龄(齡)要求是十八岁(歲)。
    - Zhè fèn gōngzuò de zuìdī niánlíng yāoqiú shì shíbā suì.
    - The minimum age requirement for this job is eighteen years old.
### 年龄(齡) → 龄(齡) → 齒
- **definition:** tooth
- **pinyin:** chǐ
- **components:**
  - 止
    - zhǐ
    - stop
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - Originally a pictogram depicting a mouth full of teeth ->
    - phonetic 止 (zhǐ, "stop") added to aid pronunciation
  - **interpretation:** The character started as a visual representation of teeth and later incorporated 止 as a phonetic component to reinforce its pronunciation while maintaining the original pictographic representation.
- **examples:**
  - 他每天早上刷齒，晚上睡覺前再刷齒。
    - Tā měitiān zǎoshang shuā chǐ, wǎnshàng shuìjiào qián zài shuā chǐ.
    - He brushes his teeth every morning, and brushes them again before bed.
  - 医(醫)生检(檢)查齒。
    - Yīshēng jiǎnchá chǐ.
    - The doctor examined the tooth.
  - 小猫(貓)露出洁(潔)白的齒，显(顯)得十分可爱(愛)。
    - Xiǎo māo lùchū jiébái de chǐ, xiǎn de shífēn kě'ài.
    - The little cat shows its white tooth, looking very cute.
### 年龄(齡) → 龄(齡) → 齒 → 止
- **definition:** stop
- **pinyin:** zhǐ
- **components:**
  - 趾
    - zhǐ
    - foot
  - 龰
    - yù
    - stylized feet
  - 手
    - shǒu
    - hand
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Original: Foot pointing up with 3 toes and a sole ->
    - Stylized as 龰 ->
    - Derivative 趾 refers to original 'foot' meaning
  - **interpretation:** Originally depicting a footprint with toes and a sole, 止 (zhǐ, "foot") represents the foot. The character's form resembles a foot with three toes, analogous to how the hand is represented with fingers in other characters.
- **examples:**
  - 他受伤(傷)的止需要静(靜)养(養)。
    - Tā shòu shāng de zhǐ xū yào jìng yǎng.
    - His injured foot needs adequate rest.
  - 他走路时(時)小心谨(謹)慎，因为(爲)止若受伤(傷)便难(難)前行。
    - Tā zǒu lù shí xiǎo xīn jǐn shèn, yīn wèi zhǐ ruò shòu shāng biàn nán qián xíng.
    - He walks carefully because if his foot gets injured, it becomes difficult to move forward.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 止](@media/glyph6b62.png)
### 年龄(齡) → 龄(齡) → 齒 → 止 → 趾
- **definition:** foot
- **pinyin:** zhǐ
- **components:**
  - 足
    - zú
    - foot
  - 止
    - zhǐ
    - halt
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic 足 (zú, "foot") + phonetic 止 (zhǐ) ->
    - toe
  - **interpretation:** The character combines 足 (zú, "foot"), indicating the general area involved, with 止 (zhǐ) providing the sound and potentially suggesting the idea of a part of the foot that 'halts' or 'stops' progression, which naturally leads to the notion of a toe.
- **examples:**
  - 他的脚(腳)趾受伤(傷)了。
    - Tā de jiǎozhǐ shòushāng le.
    - His toe is injured.
  - 她用脚(腳)趾轻(輕)轻(輕)地踢了一下球。
    - Tā yòng jiǎozhǐ qīngqīng de tī le yīxià qiú.
    - She gently kicked the ball with her toe.
  - 在沙滩(灘)上散步时(時)，我感受到沙子在我的脚(腳)趾间(間)流动(動)。
    - Zài shātān shàng sànbù shí, wǒ gǎnshòu dào shāzi zài wǒ de jiǎozhǐ jiān liúdòng.
    - While walking on the beach, I felt the sand flowing between my toes.
### 年龄(齡) → 龄(齡) → 齒 → 止 → 趾 → 足
- **definition:** foot
- **pinyin:** zú
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a leg ->
    - originally depicted as ⽦ ->
    - represents 'foot'
  - **interpretation:** The character 足(zú, 'foot') is a pictographic representation of a human leg, which directly portrays the concept of a 'foot'. The pictographic origin emphasizes its fundamental meaning in the language.
- **examples:**
  - 他受伤(傷)后(後)，他的足不能动(動)。
    - tā shòushāng hòu, tā de zú bù néng dòng。
    - After he was injured, his foot couldn't move.
  - 小明打球时(時)，不小心扭伤(傷)了足。
    - xiǎo míng dǎ qiú shí, bù xiǎoxīn niǔ shāng le zú。
    - When Xiaoming was playing ball, he accidentally twisted his foot.
  - 我每天锻(鍛)炼(鍊)足部。
    - wǒ měitiān duànliàn zúbù。
    - I exercise my foot muscles every day.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 足](@media/glyph8db3.png)
### 年龄(齡) → 龄(齡) → 齒 → 止 → 龰
- **definition:** stylized feet
- **pinyin:** yù
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a stylized footprint pointing upward ->
    - originally meaning 'foot' ->
    - later forms like 趾 (zhǐ, 'toe') refer back to original meaning
  - **interpretation:** 龰 (yù, 'stylized feet') is a pictogram showing a footprint pointing up, originally indicating the concept of a foot. The character 趾 (zhǐ, 'toe') evolved from this and retains the reference to the original meaning. It visually resembles a sole with three toes, similar to representations of the human hand in characters like 爪 (zhuǎ, 'claw'), 寸 (cùn, 'inch'), and 又 (yòu, 'again').
### 年龄(齡) → 龄(齡) → 齒 → 止 → 手
- **definition:** hand
- **pinyin:** shǒu
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a hand with fingers; top stroke is a bent over middle finger, horizontal strokes represent fingers
  - **interpretation:** The character 手 (shǒu, "hand") is a direct pictorial representation of a human hand with all five fingers, which distinguishes it from similar characters representing claws or simplified fingers. This visually conveys its meaning as a hand clearly.
- **examples:**
  - 他用手写(寫)字。
    - Tā yòng shǒu xiě zì.
    - He writes with his hand.
  - 妈(媽)妈(媽)牵(牽)着(著)我的手走路。
    - Māmā qiān zhe wǒ de shǒu zǒu lù.
    - Mom holds my hand while walking.
  - 他的手很温(溫)暖，带(帶)给(給)我力量。
    - Tā de shǒu hěn wēn nuǎn, dài gěi wǒ lìliàng.
    - His hand is very warm, giving me strength.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 手](@media/glyph624b.png)
### 年龄(齡) → 龄(齡) → 令
- **definition:** order
- **pinyin:** lìng
- **components:**
  - 人
    - rén
    - person
  - 卩
    - jié
    - seal
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - 人 (rén, "person") + 卩 (jié, "seal") =
    - person with seal ->
    - issuing orders or commands
  - **interpretation:** The character 令 (lǐng, "order") combines 人 (rén, "person") and 卩 (jié, "seal") to depict someone with a seal or authority, signifying the power to issue orders or commands.
- **examples:**
  - 将(將)军(軍)令部队(隊)保持警戒，士兵严(嚴)格服从(從)。
    - jiāngjūn lǐng bùduì bǎochí jǐngjiè, shìbīng yángé fúcóng.
    - The general orders the troops to maintain vigilance, and the soldiers strictly obey.
  - 老师(師)令学(學)生认(認)真听(聽)讲(講)。
    - lǎoshī lǐng xuéshēng rènzhēn tīngjiǎng.
    - The teacher orders the students to listen attentively.
  - 国(國)王令大臣速速筹(籌)备(備)，迎接远(遠)方使节(節)。
    - guówáng lǐng dàchén sùsù chóubèi, yíngjiē yuǎnfāng shǐjié.
    - The king orders his ministers to quickly make preparations to welcome the foreign envoy.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 令](@media/glyph4ee4.png)
### 年龄(齡) → 龄(齡) → 令 → 人
- **definition:** person
- **pinyin:** rén
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts side view of a standing man, highlighting an arm and a leg ->
    - visual representation of a person
  - **interpretation:** The character 人 (rén, 'person') effectively uses simple lines to depict the essential form of a human, making it immediately recognizable and intuitive as meaning 'person.'
- **examples:**
  - 他是个(個)好人。
    - Tā shì gè hǎo rén.
    - He is a good person.
  - 每个(個)人都有责(責)任，为(為)社会(會)作出贡(貢)献(獻)。
    - Měi gè rén dōu yǒu zérèn, wèi shèhuì zuòchū gòngxiàn.
    - Every person has a responsibility to contribute to society.
  - 人在旅途中，心灵(靈)获(獲)得了成长(長)。
    - Rén zài lǚtú zhōng, xīnlíng huòdé le chéngzhǎng.
    - People gain growth along their journey.

### 年龄(齡) → 龄(齡) → 令 → 卩
- **definition:** seal
- **pinyin:** jié
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a kneeling person from sideview
  - **interpretation:** The character 卩 (jié, "kneeling person") is a simple pictogram showing the silhouette of a person kneeling. It is unrelated to other kneeling or similar figures in different contexts such as 欠 (qiàn, "yawn") where the mouth is open, or 女 (nǚ, "woman") where the figure represents a female. Its form is solely based on the posture of kneeling.
- **examples:**
  - 那位卩正虔诚(誠)祈祷(禱)。
    - Nà wèi jié zhèng qiánchéng qídǎo.
    - That kneeling person is praying devoutly.
  - 礼(禮)仪(儀)师(師)指出，卩代表谦(謙)卑与(與)敬意。
    - Lǐyí shī zhǐchū, jié dàibiǎo qiānbēi yǔ jìngyì.
    - The ritual master pointed out that the kneeling person represents humility and respect.
  - 在庄(莊)严(嚴)仪(儀)式中，卩象征(徵)着(著)内(內)心的虔敬。
    - Zài zhuāngyán yíshì zhōng, jié xiàngzhēngzhe nèixīn de qiánjìng.
    - In the solemn ceremony, the kneeling figure symbolizes inner devotion.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 卩](@media/glyph5369.png)

## 年龄(齡)
### niánlíng
---
## age (of a person, animal or plant, etc.)
%%%
## 马(馬)路
---
## road; street
### mǎlù
---
- **traditional:** 馬路
- **definition:** road; street
- **pinyin:** mǎlù
- **components:**
  - 马(馬)
    - mǎ
    - horse
  - 路
    - lù
    - road; path; journey
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** compound word
  - **description:** 馬 (mǎ, "horse") refers to horses, which were the primary mode of transport in historical times, and 路 (lù, "road") signifies a path or street. This combination conveys the concept of a 'road' or 'street' suitable for vehicles, originally horse-drawn.
  - **interpretation:** The word 馬路 (mǎlù) draws on the historical imagery of roads used for horse-drawn vehicles. Horses symbolize travel and movement, making them a natural fit for 路 (lù, "road"), which defines the structured path meant for them. Thus, 馬路 (mǎlù) captures the essence of a thoroughfare built for transit.
- **examples:**
  - 马(馬)路上有很多汽车(車)。
    - Mǎlù shàng yǒu hěn duō qìchē.
    - There are many cars on the road.
  - 儿(兒)童不应(應)该(該)在马(馬)路上玩耍。
    - Értóng bù yīnggāi zài mǎlù shàng wánshuǎ.
    - Children should not play on the street.
  - 这(這)条(條)马(馬)路通向城中心。
    - Zhè tiáo mǎlù tōng xiàng chéng zhōngxīn.
    - This road leads to the city center.
### 马(馬)路 → 马(馬)
- **traditional:** 馬
- **definition:** horse
- **pinyin:** mǎ
- **components:**
  - 目
    - mù
    - eye
  - 火
    - huǒ
    - fire
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a horse with head facing left and flowing mane ->
    - head often simplified into an eye 目 (mù, "eye") ->
    - legs evolved into four dots 灬 unrelated to 火 (huǒ, "fire")
  - **interpretation:** The character represents a horse with its mane flowing sideways, and the simplification over time captured the essence of its most visible features.
  - **simplification:** 馬 was simplified to 马(馬) by fusing the head and body, using the simplified line forms and dots to represent its features more compactly.
- **examples:**
  - 小马(馬)在草地上奔跑。
    - Xiǎo mǎ zài cǎodì shàng bēnpǎo.
    - The little horse runs on the grassland.
  - 我骑(騎)马(馬)看风(風)景，感觉(覺)非常自在。
    - Wǒ qí mǎ kàn fēngjǐng, gǎnjué fēicháng zìzài.
    - I ride a horse to enjoy the scenery, feeling very at ease.
  - 马(馬)是人类(類)历(歷)史上的好伙(夥)伴。
    - Mǎ shì rénlèi lìshǐ shàng de hǎo huǒbàn.
    - Horses are good companions in human history.
### 马(馬)路 → 马(馬) → 目
- **definition:** eye
- **pinyin:** mù
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a human eye, now represented and rotated 90 degrees ->
    - eye
  - **interpretation:** The character 目(mù, 'eye') is a pictogram representing a human eye. Its original orientation has changed over time, resembling an eye seen from a sideways view.
- **examples:**
  - 他的目光炯炯有神。
    - Tā de mùguāng jiǒngjiǒng yǒu shén.
    - His gaze is bright and full of spirit.
  - 她目不转(轉)睛，注视(視)前方。
    - Tā mù bù zhuǎn jīng, zhùshì qiánfāng.
    - She stared intently, gazing ahead.
  - 雄鹰(鷹)展翅，双(雙)目炯炯看天际(際)。
    - Xióng yīng zhǎn chì, shuāng mù jiǒngjiǒng kàn tiānjì.
    - The eagle spreads its wings, its eyes piercingly gaze at the horizon.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 目](@media/glyph76ee.png)
### 马(馬)路 → 马(馬) → 火
- **definition:** fire
- **pinyin:** huǒ
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts flames rising from a fire
  - **interpretation:** The character 火 (huǒ, "fire") visually represents flames flickering upwards, which intuitively conveys the essence of fire. This simple depiction is an effective way to capture the dynamic and essential nature of fire.
- **examples:**
  - 火在壁炉(爐)中熊熊燃烧(燒)。
    - Huǒ zài bìlú zhōng xióngxióng ránshāo.
    - The fire burns fiercely in the fireplace.
  - 野外露营(營)时(時)，火能驱(驅)走寒冷。
    - Yěwài lùyíng shí, huǒ néng qūzǒu hánlěng.
    - When camping outdoors, the fire can drive away the cold.
  - 遇到火灾(災)时(時)，迅速疏散最为(為)重要。
    - Yù dào huǒzāi shí, xùnsù shū sàn zuìwéi zhòngyào.
    - In case of a fire, evacuating quickly is of utmost importance.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 火](@media/glyph706b.png)
### 马(馬)路 → 路
- **definition:** road; path; journey
- **pinyin:** lù
- **components:**
  - 足
    - zú
    - foot
  - 各
    - gè
    - each
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic 足 (zú, 'foot') + phonetic 各 (gè) ->
    - road
  - **interpretation:** The semantic component 足 (zú, 'foot') represents walking or movement, suggesting the idea of a path or road. 各 (gè) serves as the phonetic component, contributing to the pronunciation of the character.
  - **simplification:** The character retains its form in simplified Chinese, with no changes.
- **examples:**
  - 这(這)里(裡)的路很宽(寬)敞。
    - Zhèlǐ de lù hěn kuānchǎng.
    - The road here is very wide.
  - 他选(選)择(擇)了一条(條)不同的路。
    - Tā xuǎnzéle yī tiáo bùtóng de lù.
    - He chose a different path.
  - 走这(這)条(條)路会(會)更快。
    - Zǒu zhè tiáo lù huì gèng kuài.
    - Taking this road will be faster.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 路](@media/glyph8def.png)
### 马(馬)路 → 路 → 足
- **definition:** foot
- **pinyin:** zú
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a leg ->
    - originally depicted as ⽦ ->
    - represents 'foot'
  - **interpretation:** The character 足(zú, 'foot') is a pictographic representation of a human leg, which directly portrays the concept of a 'foot'. The pictographic origin emphasizes its fundamental meaning in the language.
- **examples:**
  - 他受伤(傷)后(後)，他的足不能动(動)。
    - tā shòushāng hòu, tā de zú bù néng dòng。
    - After he was injured, his foot couldn't move.
  - 小明打球时(時)，不小心扭伤(傷)了足。
    - xiǎo míng dǎ qiú shí, bù xiǎoxīn niǔ shāng le zú。
    - When Xiaoming was playing ball, he accidentally twisted his foot.
  - 我每天锻(鍛)炼(鍊)足部。
    - wǒ měitiān duànliàn zúbù。
    - I exercise my foot muscles every day.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 足](@media/glyph8db3.png)
### 马(馬)路 → 路 → 各
- **definition:** each
- **pinyin:** gè
- **components:**
  - 口
    - kǒu
    - mouth
  - 夂(夊)
    - zhǐ
    - go
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - 口 (kǒu, "mouth") + phonetic: 夂(夊) (zhǐ, "go") =
    - sound element ->
    - "each"
  - **interpretation:** The character 各 (gè, "each") combines 口 (kǒu, "mouth") representing a semantic element with 夂(夊) (zhǐ, "go") for the phonetic aspect, suggesting the pronunciation and semantic concept of different mouths taking separate paths.
- **examples:**
  - 他们(們)各自承担(擔)责(責)任。
    - Tāmen gèzì chéngdān zérèn.
    - They each take responsibility.
  - 老师(師)将(將)试(試)卷分给(給)各个(個)学(學)生。
    - Lǎoshī jiāng shìjuàn fēn gěi gègè xuésheng.
    - The teacher distributed the test papers to each student.
  - 会(會)议(議)上，各部门(門)各显(顯)其能。
    - Huìyì shàng, gè bùmén gè xiǎn qí néng.
    - At the meeting, each department exhibited its capabilities.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 各](@media/glyph5404.png)
### 马(馬)路 → 路 → 各 → 口
- **definition:** mouth
- **pinyin:** kǒu
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts an open mouth.
  - **interpretation:** The character 口(kǒu, 'mouth') is a straightforward pictogram that visually represents an open mouth. It is a fundamental character in the Chinese language, often used both as an independent word and as a component in more complex characters, lending a semantic association to ideas relating to speech, openings, or enclosures.
- **examples:**
  - 他张(張)开(開)口，大声(聲)喊叫。
    - Tā zhāngkāi kǒu, dàshēng hǎnjiào.
    - He opened his mouth and shouted loudly.
  - 这(這)口饭(飯)入口即化。
    - Zhè kǒu fàn rùkǒu jíhuà.
    - This mouthful of food melts in your mouth.
  - 小女孩咬了一口苹(蘋)果，露出甜美的笑容。
    - Xiǎo nǚhái yǎole yī kǒu píngguǒ, lùchū tiánměi de xiàoróng.
    - The little girl took a bite of the apple and smiled sweetly.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 口](@media/glyph53e3.png)
### 马(馬)路 → 路 → 各 → 夂
- **definition:** go
- **pinyin:** zhǐ
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a footprint pointing down
  - **interpretation:** The character 夂 (zhǐ, 'foot pointing down') is a pictogram representing a footprint facing downward, often associated with motion or directionality. This depiction intuitively aligns with its meaning of indicating a downward step or path.
- **examples:**
  - 汉(漢)字中‘夂’常被用作偏旁，象征(徵)步伐朝下。
    - Hànzì zhōng ‘zhǐ’ cháng bèi yòng zuò piān páng, xiàng zhēng bù fá cháo xià.
    - In Chinese characters, '夂' is often used as a radical to symbolize downward steps.
  - 书(書)法中‘夂’的结(結)构(構)犹(猶)如足尖向下。
    - Shūfǎ zhōng ‘zhǐ’ de jiégòu yóurú zújiān xiàng xià.
    - In calligraphy, the structure of '夂' resembles a foot pointing downward.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 夂](@media/glyph5902.png)

## 闭(閉)
---
## shut; close
### bì
---
- **traditional:** 閉
- **definition:** shut; close
- **pinyin:** bì
- **components:**
  - 門
    - mén
    - door
  - 材
    - cái
    - material; timber
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogrammic compound
  - **description:**
    - 門 (mén, "door") + abbreviated 材 (cái, "material; timber") =
    - a door with material blocking it ->
    - shut; close
  - **interpretation:** The character depicts a door being obstructed by some material, symbolizing the act of shutting or closing it.
  - **simplification:** The traditional form 閉 was simplified by reducing 門 (mén, "door") to 门 in the simplified character 闭.
- **examples:**
  - 请(請)把门(門)闭(閉)上。
    - Qǐng bǎ mén bì shàng.
    - Please shut the door.
  - 他闭(閉)了一只(隻)眼睛，假装(裝)在睡觉(覺)。
    - Tā bìle yī zhī yǎnjīng, jiǎzhuāng zài shuìjiào.
    - He closed one eye, pretending to sleep.
  - 这(這)个(個)窗户(戶)很难(難)闭(閉)上，你需要用点(點)力气(氣)。
    - Zhège chuānghù hěn nán bì shàng, nǐ xūyào yòng diǎn lìqi.
    - This window is hard to close; you need to use some force.
### 闭(閉) → 門
- **definition:** door
- **pinyin:** mén
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a double-door gate
  - **interpretation:** The character depicts a pair of doors, visually representing the concept of a door or gate, which is fundamental in indicating entrance and exit points in structures.
- **examples:**
  - 我走到门(門)口。
    - Wǒ zǒu dào ménkǒu.
    - I walk to the door.
  - 门(門)轻(輕)轻(輕)打开(開)，房客进(進)来(來)了。
    - Mén qīngqīng dǎkāi, fángkè jìn láile.
    - The door opened gently, and the tenant came in.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 門](@media/glyph9580.png)
### 闭(閉) → 材
- **definition:** material; timber
- **pinyin:** cái
- **components:**
  - 木
    - mù
    - tree
  - 才
    - cái
    - talent
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic 木 (mù, "tree") + phonetic 才 (cái, "talent (phonetic)") ->
    - material; timber
  - **interpretation:** The character combines 木 (mù, "tree") as the semantic component, representing trees or wood, with 才 (cái), which provides the phonetic element. The combination indicates timber as processed wood material, derived from trees, and this extends metaphorically to 'material' in general as a resource or substance that can be worked with, much like wood.
- **examples:**
  - 这(這)座房子是用优(優)质(質)的木材建造的。
    - Zhè zuò fángzi shì yòng yōuzhì de mùcái jiànzào de.
    - This house is built with high-quality timber.
  - 他具备(備)成为(為)优(優)秀工程师(師)的材料。
    - Tā jùbèi chéngwéi yōuxiù gōngchéngshī de cáiliào.
    - He has the material to become an excellent engineer.
### 闭(閉) → 材 → 木
- **definition:** tree
- **pinyin:** mù
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a tree with branches and roots
  - **interpretation:** The character 木(mù) depicts a tree, showing the trunk in the center and two slanting lines representing branches or roots. It directly signifies the concept of wood or a tree.
- **examples:**
  - 这(這)把椅子的主要材料是木。
    - Zhè bǎ yǐzi de zhǔyào cáiliào shì mù.
    - The main material of this chair is wood.
  - 工匠精心雕刻木，制成精美家具。
    - Gōngjiàng jīngxīn diāo kè mù, zhìchéng jīngměi jiājù.
    - The craftsman carefully carved the wood, crafting exquisite furniture.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 木](@media/glyph6728.png)
### 闭(閉) → 材 → 才
- **definition:** talent
- **pinyin:** cái
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a sharp peg ->
    - originally referred to pegs used in board games ->
    - conceptually extended to 'talent' as skill pegs straight into a task
  - **interpretation:** The character 才 (cái) initially depicted a sharp peg, which was associated with playing board games that required skill. This sense of skill was then extended metaphorically to mean 'talent'. The leap to 'only then' likely comes from the notion that one's capabilities are unlocked or recognized through achievement, akin to placing the right peg in the right spot.
- **examples:**
  - 他的音乐(樂)才华(華)令人惊(驚)叹(嘆)。
    - Tā de yīnyuè cáihuá lìngrén jīngtàn.
    - His musical talent is astonishing.
  - 我刚(剛)刚(剛)才知道这(這)个(個)消息。
    - Wǒ gānggāng cái zhīdào zhège xiāoxi.
    - I just now found out about this news.
  - 只有努力工作才能取得成功。
    - Zhǐyǒu nǔlì gōngzuò cái néng qǔdé chénggōng.
    - Only by working hard can one achieve success.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 才](@media/glyph624d.png)
---
## 闭(閉)
### bì
---
## shut; close

## 领(領)
---
## lead; usher; take
### lǐng
---
- **traditional:** 領
- **definition:** lead; usher; take
- **pinyin:** lǐng
- **components:**
  - 令
    - lìng
    - order
  - 頁
    - yè
    - head
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic 頁 (yè, "head") + phonetic 令 (lìng, "order") ->
    - lead; usher; take
  - **interpretation:** Semantic 頁 (yè, "head") suggests direction or leadership, as the head leads the body. Phonetic 令 (lìng, "order") provides the sound, enhancing the concept of directing or leading, where orders are followed. The combination reflects the idea of guiding or taking the lead, akin to a head giving direction to an order.
  - **simplification:** 領 was simplified by reducing 頁 to 页(頁), decreasing stroke count without altering phonetic 令.
- **examples:**
  - 他带(帶)领(領)我们(們)去参(參)观(觀)博物馆(館)。
    - Tā dàilǐng wǒmen qù cānguān bówùguǎn.
    - He led us to visit the museum.
  - 她在课(課)堂上总(總)是能领(領)会(會)到老师(師)的意思。
    - Tā zài kètáng shàng zǒng shì néng lǐnghuì dào lǎoshī de yìsi.
    - She always grasps the teacher's meaning in class.
  - 经(經)过(過)他的领(領)导(導)，团(團)队(隊)取得了巨大进(進)步。
    - Jīngguò tā de lǐngdǎo, tuánduì qǔdéle jùdà jìnbù.
    - Under his leadership, the team made significant progress.
### 领(領) → 令
- **definition:** order
- **pinyin:** lìng
- **components:**
  - 人
    - rén
    - person
  - 卩
    - jié
    - seal
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - 人 (rén, "person") + 卩 (jié, "seal") =
    - person with seal ->
    - issuing orders or commands
  - **interpretation:** The character 令 (lǐng, "order") combines 人 (rén, "person") and 卩 (jié, "seal") to depict someone with a seal or authority, signifying the power to issue orders or commands.
- **examples:**
  - 将(將)军(軍)令部队(隊)保持警戒，士兵严(嚴)格服从(從)。
    - jiāngjūn lǐng bùduì bǎochí jǐngjiè, shìbīng yángé fúcóng.
    - The general orders the troops to maintain vigilance, and the soldiers strictly obey.
  - 老师(師)令学(學)生认(認)真听(聽)讲(講)。
    - lǎoshī lǐng xuéshēng rènzhēn tīngjiǎng.
    - The teacher orders the students to listen attentively.
  - 国(國)王令大臣速速筹(籌)备(備)，迎接远(遠)方使节(節)。
    - guówáng lǐng dàchén sùsù chóubèi, yíngjiē yuǎnfāng shǐjié.
    - The king orders his ministers to quickly make preparations to welcome the foreign envoy.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 令](@media/glyph4ee4.png)
### 领(領) → 令 → 人
- **definition:** person
- **pinyin:** rén
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts side view of a standing man, highlighting an arm and a leg ->
    - visual representation of a person
  - **interpretation:** The character 人 (rén, 'person') effectively uses simple lines to depict the essential form of a human, making it immediately recognizable and intuitive as meaning 'person.'
- **examples:**
  - 他是个(個)好人。
    - Tā shì gè hǎo rén.
    - He is a good person.
  - 每个(個)人都有责(責)任，为(為)社会(會)作出贡(貢)献(獻)。
    - Měi gè rén dōu yǒu zérèn, wèi shèhuì zuòchū gòngxiàn.
    - Every person has a responsibility to contribute to society.
  - 人在旅途中，心灵(靈)获(獲)得了成长(長)。
    - Rén zài lǚtú zhōng, xīnlíng huòdé le chéngzhǎng.
    - People gain growth along their journey.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 人](@media/glyph4eba.png)
### 领(領) → 令 → 卩
- **definition:** seal
- **pinyin:** jié
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a kneeling person from sideview
  - **interpretation:** The character 卩 (jié, "kneeling person") is a simple pictogram showing the silhouette of a person kneeling. It is unrelated to other kneeling or similar figures in different contexts such as 欠 (qiàn, "yawn") where the mouth is open, or 女 (nǚ, "woman") where the figure represents a female. Its form is solely based on the posture of kneeling.
- **examples:**
  - 那位卩正虔诚(誠)祈祷(禱)。
    - Nà wèi jié zhèng qiánchéng qídǎo.
    - That kneeling person is praying devoutly.
  - 礼(禮)仪(儀)师(師)指出，卩代表谦(謙)卑与(與)敬意。
    - Lǐyí shī zhǐchū, jié dàibiǎo qiānbēi yǔ jìngyì.
    - The ritual master pointed out that the kneeling person represents humility and respect.
  - 在庄(莊)严(嚴)仪(儀)式中，卩象征(徵)着(著)内(內)心的虔敬。
    - Zài zhuāngyán yíshì zhōng, jié xiàngzhēngzhe nèixīn de qiánjìng.
    - In the solemn ceremony, the kneeling figure symbolizes inner devotion.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 卩](@media/glyph5369.png)
### 领(領) → 頁
- **definition:** head
- **pinyin:** yè
- **components:**
  - 首
    - shǒu
    - head; first
  - 卩
    - jié
    - kneeling person
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - 首 (head/face) + 卩 (kneeling person) ->
    - depicts a person's head and body
  - **interpretation:** Originally represented a head and its body in a kneeling posture, emphasizing “head”. The depiction was extended semantically to represent a 'page', as pages bear leading information like a head does for a body. The concept of 'head' is also reflected in its modern usage as a radical in characters related to parts of the head or face.
  - **simplification:** 页 is a cursive shorthand of the traditional 頁, simplifying the structure while maintaining the core shape of a head.
- **examples:**
  - 请(請)打开(開)书(書)的第十页(頁)。
    - Qǐng dǎkāi shū de dì shí yè.
    - Please open to page ten of the book.
  - 这(這)本书(書)每一页(頁)都有插图(圖)。
    - Zhè běn shū měi yī yè dōu yǒu chātú.
    - Every page of this book has illustrations.
  - 我昨天晚上读(讀)了三十页(頁)。
    - Wǒ zuótiān wǎnshang dúle sānshí yè.
    - I read thirty pages last night.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 頁](@media/glyph9801.png)
### 领(領) → 頁 → 首
- **definition:** head; first
- **pinyin:** shǒu
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts the head of an animal with a long mouth and horns, often shown with or without hair ( 巛) ->
    - perpetuated as 𩠐 (form with hair) ->
    - streamlined to 首
  - **interpretation:** The character depicts the head of an animal, with prominent features like a long mouth and horns, emphasizing the notion of a 'head' both physically and symbolically as the foremost part.
- **examples:**
  - 他是这(這)个(個)团(團)队(隊)的首领(領)。
    - Tā shì zhège tuánduì de shǒulǐng.
    - He is the head of this team.
  - 这(這)首歌是我最喜欢(歡)的歌曲。
    - Zhè shǒu gē shì wǒ zuì xǐhuān de gēqǔ.
    - This song is my favorite track.
  - 他抬起头(頭)，看向远(遠)方的山。
    - Tā tái qǐ tóu, kàn xiàng yuǎnfāng de shān.
    - He raised his head and looked towards the distant mountains.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 首](@media/glyph9996.png)
---
## 领(領)
### lǐng
---
## lead; usher; take
%%%
## 照顾(顧)
---
## take care of; look after
### zhàogù
---
- **traditional:** 照顧
- **definition:** take care of; look after
- **pinyin:** zhàogù
- **components:**
  - 照
    - zhào
    - shine; illuminate; reflect
  - 顾(顧)
    - gù
    - look after; attend to; care for
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** compound word
  - **description:** 照 (zhào, "shine; illuminate; reflect") refers to the act of shining or projecting light, suggesting awareness and consideration. 顾(顧) (gù, "look after; attend to; care for") means to look in a certain direction or turn the head to regard something, implying attention and concern.
  - **interpretation:** 照 (zhào, "shine; illuminate") involves the projection of light, which can be linked to the notion of providing attention and insight, as if 'shining a light' on someone; this connects to the idea of looking after. 顾(顧) (gù, "look after; attend to") literally means turning the head to look, indicating focus and care. Together, 照顾(顧) (zhàogù, "take care of; look after") conveys the concept of paying careful attention to someone or something, as if continually illuminating and tending to it with care.
- **examples:**
  - 妈(媽)妈(媽)每天都照顾(顧)我。
    - Māma měitiān dōu zhàogù wǒ.
    - Mom takes care of me every day.
  - 请(請)多多照顾(顧)新来(來)的同事。
    - Qǐng duōduō zhàogù xīn lái de tóngshì.
    - Please take good care of the new colleague.
  - 他生病了，需要有人照顾(顧)他。
    - Tā shēngbìng le, xūyào yǒurén zhàogù tā.
    - He is sick and needs someone to take care of him.
### 照顾(顧) → 照
- **definition:** shine; illuminate; reflect
- **pinyin:** zhào
- **components:**
  - 灬
    - huǒ
    - fire
  - 昭
    - zhāo
    - bright
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic 灬 ("fire") + phonetic 昭 ->
    - illuminate; shine
  - **interpretation:** The character 照 (zhào, "illuminate") uses 灬 ("fire") to represent light or brightness, combined with the phonetic 昭 (zhāo) to suggest its pronunciation. The association with fire indicates brightness or acting as a source of light, leading naturally to meanings such as "illuminate" and "shine." This brightness reflects onto surfaces or scenes, hence the character's extension to "reflect" and "take (photo)," as capturing an illuminated image.
- **examples:**
  - 早晨的阳(陽)光照在窗户(戶)上。
    - Zǎochén de yángguāng zhào zài chuānghu shàng.
    - The morning sunlight shines on the window.
  - 请(請)把灯(燈)打开(開)，以便更好地照清楚。
    - Qǐng bǎ dēng dǎkāi, yǐbiàn gèng hǎo de zhào qīngchǔ.
    - Please turn on the light to illuminate more clearly.
  - 我们(們)去公园(園)照相。
    - Wǒmen qù gōngyuán zhàoxiàng.
    - We are going to the park to take photos.
- **historical forms:**

### 照顾(顧) → 照 → 灬
- **definition:** fire
- **pinyin:** huǒ
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts flames or fire at the bottom of a character
  - **interpretation:** The character 灬(biāo, 'fire') visually resembles flames and is used to represent fire-related concepts, especially as a radical component in many Chinese characters.
- **examples:**
  - 灬是燃烧(燒)的象征(徵)。
    - biāo shì ránshāo de xiàngzhēng.
    - Fire is a symbol of burning.
  - 夜幕降临(臨)时(時)，灬映出温(溫)暖的光芒。
    - yè mù jiàng lín shí, biāo yìng chū wēnnuǎn de guāngmáng.
    - When night falls, fire radiates a warm glow.
  - 狂风(風)暴雨后(後)，灬象征(徵)重生。
    - kuáng fēng bào yǔ hòu, biāo xiàngzhēng chóngshēng.
    - After the storm, fire symbolizes rebirth.
### 照顾(顧) → 照 → 昭
- **definition:** bright
- **pinyin:** zhāo
- **components:**
  - 日
    - rì
    - sun
  - 召
    - zhào
    - summon
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic: 日 (rì, "sun") + phonetic: 召 (zhào, "summon") ->
    - clear, bright
  - **interpretation:** The character 昭 (zhāo, "clear, bright") combines 日 (rì, "sun"), suggesting clarity or brightness, with 召 (zhào, "summon"), providing the phonetic component. The sun's light is often associated with clarity and brightness.
- **examples:**
  - 他的意图(圖)非常昭然若揭。
    - Tā de yìtú fēicháng zhāorán ruò jiē.
    - His intentions were very clear and obvious.
  - 阳(陽)光照耀使一切变(變)得清晰明了。
    - Yángguāng zhàoyào shǐ yīqiè biàn de qīngxī míngliǎo.
    - The sunlight made everything clear and bright.
  - 这(這)段历(歷)史在书(書)中被描述得非常昭明。
    - Zhè duàn lìshǐ zài shū zhōng bèi miáoshù de fēicháng zhāomíng.
    - This part of history is described very clearly in the book.
### 照顾(顧) → 照 → 昭 → 日
- **definition:** sun
- **pinyin:** rì
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts the sun; a dot or line added in the center to distinguish from similar characters e.g. 囗
  - **interpretation:** As a pictogram, 日(rì, 'sun') directly represents the sun. In ancient times, the added dot helped visually differentiate it from other characters. This is analogous to the astronomical symbol ☉ and Egyptian hieroglyph 𓇳, both depicting the sun.
- **examples:**
  - 晨曦来(來)临(臨)时(時)，日出东(東)方。
    - Chénxī láilín shí, rìchū dōngfāng.
    - At the break of dawn, the sun rises in the east.
  - 温(溫)暖的日光洒(灑)满(滿)大地。
    - Wēnnuǎn de rìguāng sǎ mǎn dàdì.
    - The warm sunlight spreads over the earth.
  - 中午时(時)分，日高挂(掛)天。
    - Zhōngwǔ shífēn, rì gāo guà tiān.
    - At noon, the sun hangs high in the sky.

### 照顾(顧) → 照 → 昭 → 召
- **definition:** summon
- **pinyin:** zhào
- **components:**
  - 刀
    - dāo
    - knife
  - 口
    - kǒu
    - mouth
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - original hands over a wine vessel ->
    - phonetic 刀 (dāo) + semantic 口 (kǒu, 'mouth') ->
    - summon
  - **interpretation:** Originally, 召 depicted hands over a wine vessel, linked to the practice of serving wine to guests. The character evolved by adding a phonetic component 刀 (dāo) and a semantic component 口 (kǒu, 'mouth'). The mouth element implies calling out, and the knife contributes the zhào sound. The meaning extended to 'summoning' due to both calling out and the attentiveness required in serving. The concept of welcoming and calling guests informs its modern sense of summoning or calling.
- **examples:**
  - 国(國)王召集大臣们(們)商讨(討)对(對)策。
    - Guówáng zhàojí dàchénmen shāngtǎo duìcè.
    - The king summoned the ministers to discuss strategies.
  - 他被召回故乡(鄉)接受新的任务(務)。
    - Tā bèi zhào huí gùxiāng jiēshòu xīn de rènwù.
    - He was called back to his hometown to accept a new assignment.
  - 战(戰)争(爭)爆发(發)后(後)，军(軍)队(隊)迅速召集士兵。
    - Zhànzhēng bàofā hòu, jūnduì xùnsù zhàojí shìbīng.
    - After the outbreak of war, the army quickly summoned soldiers.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 召](@media/glyph53ec.png)

  - **description:** Depicts a knife
  - **interpretation:** 刀 (dāo, "knife") is a pictographic representation of a knife or blade, with a sharp edge and a handle, resembling the form of a basic cutting tool.

    - zhè bǎ dāo fēicháng fēnglì.
    - This knife is very sharp.

### 照顾(顧) → 照 → 昭 → 召 → 口
- **definition:** mouth
- **pinyin:** kǒu
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts an open mouth.
  - **interpretation:** The character 口(kǒu, 'mouth') is a straightforward pictogram that visually represents an open mouth. It is a fundamental character in the Chinese language, often used both as an independent word and as a component in more complex characters, lending a semantic association to ideas relating to speech, openings, or enclosures.
- **examples:**
  - 他张(張)开(開)口，大声(聲)喊叫。
    - Tā zhāngkāi kǒu, dàshēng hǎnjiào.
    - He opened his mouth and shouted loudly.
  - 这(這)口饭(飯)入口即化。
    - Zhè kǒu fàn rùkǒu jíhuà.
    - This mouthful of food melts in your mouth.
  - 小女孩咬了一口苹(蘋)果，露出甜美的笑容。
    - Xiǎo nǚhái yǎole yī kǒu píngguǒ, lùchū tiánměi de xiàoróng.
    - The little girl took a bite of the apple and smiled sweetly.

### 照顾(顧) → 顾(顧)
- **traditional:** 顧
- **definition:** look after; attend to; care for
- **pinyin:** gù
- **components:**
  - 雇
    - gù
    - hire
  - 頁
    - yè
    - head
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - Phonetic 雇 (gù, "hire") + Semantic 頁 (yè, "head") ->
    - idea of turning one's head to look ->
    - look after or visit
  - **interpretation:** The character 顧 (gù, "look after") combines the phonetic element 雇 (gù, "hire") with the semantic element 頁 (yè, "head"), suggesting the action of turning one's head, which ties to the meanings of paying attention and consideration.
  - **simplification:** 顧 was simplified by retaining the overall structure but reducing the complexity of 頁 (yè, "head") for ease of writing.
- **examples:**
  - 他总(總)是很细(細)心地照顾(顧)他的家人。
    - Tā zǒngshì hěn xìxīn de zhàogù tā de jiārén.
    - He always carefully looks after his family.
  - 在忙碌的工作中，他从(從)不忽视(視)顾(顧)及家人的感受。
    - Zài mánglù de gōngzuò zhōng, tā cóng bù hūshì gùjí jiārén de gǎnshòu.
    - Amidst his busy work, he never neglects to take into consideration his family's feelings.
  - 他路过(過)时(時)，顺(順)便去顾(顧)客经(經)理那边(邊)拜访(訪)。
    - Tā lùguò shí, shùnbiàn qù gùkè jīnglǐ nà biān bàifǎng.
    - As he passed by, he took the opportunity to visit the customer manager.

  - **description:**
    - phonetic 戶 (hù) + semantic 隹 (zhuī, "short-tailed bird") ->
    - hire
  - **interpretation:** The character 雇(gù, "hire") uses 戶 (hù, "door") phonetically to contribute the sound, while 隹 (zhuī, "short-tailed bird") suggests oversight or vigilance, as in managing or overseeing hired services.
- **examples:**

### 照顾(顧) → 顾(顧) → 雇 → 戶
- **definition:** door
- **pinyin:** hù
- **components:**
  - 門
    - mén
    - gate
  - 𠁣
    - unknown
    - unknown
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts one-half of 門 (mén, "gate") ->
    - stylized as 𠁣 ->
    - final form 戶 (hù, "door")
  - **interpretation:** The character 戶 (hù, "door") represents a single door panel, derived from the depiction of half a gate, symbolizing entry or a threshold.
  - **simplification:** 户 is a simplified and variant traditional form of 戶, streamlining the pictorial elements to a more abstract representation, but retaining the symbolic essence of a door or entrance.
- **examples:**

### 照顾(顧) → 顾(顧) → 雇 → 隹

  - **interpretation:** 隹 (zhuī, "short-tailed bird") is a pictogram representing a bird with a short tail. Its depiction served as the foundation for other characters related to birds, such as 鷕 (yǎo, "cry of a bird").
- **examples:**

    - The museum displays an ancient painting themed on the short-tailed bird.
  - 远(遠)古诗(詩)篇中常用隹来(來)象征(徵)自由，寓意生动(動)。
    - Yuǎngǔ shīpiān zhōng cháng yòng zhuī lái xiàngzhēng zìyóu, yùyì shēngdòng.

    - cry of a bird

### 照顾(顧) → 顾(顧) → 雇 → 隹 → 鷕 → 唯
- **definition:** only
- **pinyin:** wéi
- **components:**
  - 口
    - kǒu
    - mouth
  - 隹
    - zhuī
    - short-tailed bird
  - 鷕
    - yǎo
    - cry of a bird
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic 口 (kǒu, "mouth") + phonetic 隹 (zhuī, "short-tailed bird") ->
    - original form of 鷕 ->
    - borrowed phonetically for 'only'
  - **interpretation:** The character 唯 originally represented the cry of a bird, with the mouth radical indicating the sound aspect. It was later phonetically borrowed for the abstract meaning 'only', without retaining its original context related to bird sounds.
- **examples:**

### 照顾(顧) → 顾(顧) → 頁
- **definition:** head
- **pinyin:** yè
- **components:**
  - 首
    - shǒu
    - head; first
  - 卩
    - jié
    - kneeling person
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - 首 (head/face) + 卩 (kneeling person) ->
    - depicts a person's head and body
  - **interpretation:** Originally represented a head and its body in a kneeling posture, emphasizing “head”. The depiction was extended semantically to represent a 'page', as pages bear leading information like a head does for a body. The concept of 'head' is also reflected in its modern usage as a radical in characters related to parts of the head or face.
  - **simplification:** 页 is a cursive shorthand of the traditional 頁, simplifying the structure while maintaining the core shape of a head.
- **examples:**
  - 请(請)打开(開)书(書)的第十页(頁)。
    - Qǐng dǎkāi shū de dì shí yè.
    - Please open to page ten of the book.
  - 这(這)本书(書)每一页(頁)都有插图(圖)。
    - Zhè běn shū měi yī yè dōu yǒu chātú.
    - Every page of this book has illustrations.
  - 我昨天晚上读(讀)了三十页(頁)。
    - Wǒ zuótiān wǎnshang dúle sānshí yè.
    - I read thirty pages last night.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 頁](@media/glyph9801.png)
### 照顾(顧) → 顾(顧) → 頁 → 首
- **definition:** head; first
- **pinyin:** shǒu
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts the head of an animal with a long mouth and horns, often shown with or without hair ( 巛) ->
    - perpetuated as 𩠐 (form with hair) ->
    - streamlined to 首
  - **interpretation:** The character depicts the head of an animal, with prominent features like a long mouth and horns, emphasizing the notion of a 'head' both physically and symbolically as the foremost part.
- **examples:**
  - 他是这(這)个(個)团(團)队(隊)的首领(領)。
    - Tā shì zhège tuánduì de shǒulǐng.
    - He is the head of this team.
  - 这(這)首歌是我最喜欢(歡)的歌曲。
    - Zhè shǒu gē shì wǒ zuì xǐhuān de gēqǔ.
    - This song is my favorite track.
  - 他抬起头(頭)，看向远(遠)方的山。
    - Tā tái qǐ tóu, kàn xiàng yuǎnfāng de shān.
    - He raised his head and looked towards the distant mountains.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 首](@media/glyph9996.png)
### 照顾(顧) → 顾(顧) → 頁 → 卩
- **definition:** kneeling person
- **pinyin:** jié
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a kneeling person from sideview
  - **interpretation:** The character 卩 (jié, "kneeling person") is a simple pictogram showing the silhouette of a person kneeling. It is unrelated to other kneeling or similar figures in different contexts such as 欠 (qiàn, "yawn") where the mouth is open, or 女 (nǚ, "woman") where the figure represents a female. Its form is solely based on the posture of kneeling.
- **examples:**
  - 那位卩正虔诚(誠)祈祷(禱)。
    - Nà wèi jié zhèng qiánchéng qídǎo.
    - That kneeling person is praying devoutly.
  - 礼(禮)仪(儀)师(師)指出，卩代表谦(謙)卑与(與)敬意。
    - Lǐyí shī zhǐchū, jié dàibiǎo qiānbēi yǔ jìngyì.
    - The ritual master pointed out that the kneeling person represents humility and respect.
  - 在庄(莊)严(嚴)仪(儀)式中，卩象征(徵)着(著)内(內)心的虔敬。
    - Zài zhuāngyán yíshì zhōng, jié xiàngzhēngzhe nèixīn de qiánjìng.
    - In the solemn ceremony, the kneeling figure symbolizes inner devotion.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 卩](@media/glyph5369.png)

## 拉手
---
## hold (hands)
### lā (shǒu)
---
- **definition:** hold (hands)
- **pinyin:** lā (shǒu)
- **components:**
  - 拉
    - lā
    - pull; drag; haul
  - 手
    - shǒu
    - hand
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** compound word
  - **description:** 拉手 (lāshǒu, "hold hands") consists of 拉 (lā, "pull") + 手 (shǒu, "hand").
  - **interpretation:** 拉 (lā, "pull") involves motion toward oneself, evoking closeness or connection when applied to 手 (shǒu, "hand"). Therefore, 拉手 (lāshǒu) literally describes the action of pulling hands together, thus intuitively depicting the act of holding hands.
- **examples:**
  - 在公园(園)里(裏)，我们(們)常常拉手。
    - Zài gōngyuán lǐ, wǒmen chángcháng lāshǒu.
    - In the park, we often hold hands.
  - 小孩拉着(著)手，一起过(過)马(馬)路。
    - Xiǎohái lāzhe shǒu, yīqǐ guò mǎlù.
    - The children hold hands while crossing the road.
  - 他们(們)见(見)面时(時)，总(總)是会(會)拉手。
    - Tāmen jiànmiàn shí, zǒng shì huì lāshǒu.
    - When they meet, they always hold hands.
### 拉手 → 拉
- **definition:** pull; drag; haul
- **pinyin:** lā
- **components:**
  - 手
    - shǒu
    - hand
  - 立
    - lì
    - stand
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic 手 (shǒu, "hand") + phonetic 立 (lì) ->
    - pull
  - **interpretation:** The character 拉 (lā, "pull; drag; draw out") combines 手 (shǒu, "hand") as the semantic element, suggesting an action performed with the hand, with 立 (lì) as the phonetic component, providing the 'lā' sound. The intuitive image is a hand performing the action of pulling or dragging.
- **examples:**
  - 请(請)帮(幫)我把椅子拉过(過)来(來)。
    - Qǐng bāng wǒ bǎ yǐzi lā guòlái.
    - Please help me pull the chair over.
  - 他喜欢(歡)在地上拉着(著)玩具车(車)。
    - Tā xǐhuān zài dìshàng lā zhe wánjùchē.
    - He likes to drag toy cars on the floor.
  - 我们(們)要用力把船拉到岸边(邊)。
    - Wǒmen yào yònglì bǎ chuán lā dào ànbiān.
    - We need to pull the boat to the shore with force.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 拉](@media/glyph62c9.png)
### 拉手 → 拉 → 手
- **definition:** hand
- **pinyin:** shǒu
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a hand with fingers; top stroke is a bent over middle finger, horizontal strokes represent fingers
  - **interpretation:** The character 手 (shǒu, "hand") is a direct pictorial representation of a human hand with all five fingers, which distinguishes it from similar characters representing claws or simplified fingers. This visually conveys its meaning as a hand clearly.
- **examples:**
  - 他用手写(寫)字。
    - Tā yòng shǒu xiě zì.
    - He writes with his hand.
  - 妈(媽)妈(媽)牵(牽)着(著)我的手走路。
    - Māmā qiān zhe wǒ de shǒu zǒu lù.
    - Mom holds my hand while walking.
  - 他的手很温(溫)暖，带(帶)给(給)我力量。
    - Tā de shǒu hěn wēn nuǎn, dài gěi wǒ lìliàng.
    - His hand is very warm, giving me strength.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 手](@media/glyph624b.png)
### 拉手 → 拉 → 立
- **definition:** stand
- **pinyin:** lì
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a person standing on the ground
  - **interpretation:** The character 立 (lì, 'stand') intuitively represents the concept of standing by depicting a person in an upright position, emphasizing the posture.
- **examples:**
  - 小王立在窗前，等待朋友到来(來)。
    - Xiǎo Wáng lì zài chuāng qián, děngdài péngyǒu dàolái.
    - Xiao Wang stands at the window, waiting for his friend to arrive.
  - 园(園)中雕像静(靜)立于(於)石台(臺)上。
    - Yuán zhōng diāoxiàng jìng lì yú shí tái shàng.
    - The statue in the garden stands quietly on the stone platform.
  - 士兵集合后(後)，整齐(齊)地立定阵(陣)型。
    - Shìbīng jíhé hòu, zhěngqí de lì dìng zhènxíng.
    - After the soldiers assemble, they stand in formation neatly.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 立](@media/glyph7acb.png)
### 拉手 → 手
- **definition:** hand
- **pinyin:** shǒu
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a hand with fingers; top stroke is a bent over middle finger, horizontal strokes represent fingers
  - **interpretation:** The character 手 (shǒu, "hand") is a direct pictorial representation of a human hand with all five fingers, which distinguishes it from similar characters representing claws or simplified fingers. This visually conveys its meaning as a hand clearly.
- **examples:**
  - 他用手写(寫)字。
    - Tā yòng shǒu xiě zì.
    - He writes with his hand.

    - Māmā qiān zhe wǒ de shǒu zǒu lù.
    - Mom holds my hand while walking.

    - Tā de shǒu hěn wēn nuǎn, dài gěi wǒ lìliàng.

## 使劲(勁)儿(兒)
---
## exert oneself (physically)
### shǐ jìnr
---
- **traditional:** 使勁兒
- **definition:** exert oneself (physically)
- **pinyin:** shǐ jìnr
- **components:**
  - 使
    - shǐ
    - cause; send; enable
  - 劲(勁)
    - jìn
    - strength; energy; enthusiasm
  - 儿(兒)
    - ér
    - child; diminutive; nominal suffix
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** compound word
  - **description:** 使 (shǐ, "cause or send") is a verb meaning 'to cause' or 'send', often used to denote initiating an action. 勁 (jìn, "strength") refers to physical strength or energy. 兒 (ér, "child; diminutive or nominal suffix") is a common suffix in Chinese, often used in northern dialects to denote the diminutive or a casual tone.
  - **interpretation:** The phrase 使劲(勁)儿(兒) (shǐ jìnr) translates to 'exert oneself' by combining the notion of causing or using 使 (shǐ, 'cause or send') with 勁 (jìn, 'strength'), implying putting forth effort or using one's full strength. The added 兒 (ér) gives it a casual or colloquial tone. Commonly used in contexts requiring physical exertion.
- **examples:**
  - 他使劲(勁)儿(兒)推门(門)。
    - Tā shǐ jìnr tuī mén.
    - He exerted himself to push the door.
  - 请(請)使劲(勁)儿(兒)拉绳(繩)子。
    - Qǐng shǐ jìnr lā shéngzi.
    - Please pull the rope with all your strength.
  - 他使劲(勁)儿(兒)地跑，但还(還)是迟(遲)到了。
    - Tā shǐ jìnr de pǎo, dàn háishì chídào le.
    - He ran with all his might, but he was still late.
### 使劲(勁)儿(兒) → 使
- **definition:** cause; send; enable
- **pinyin:** shǐ
- **components:**
  - 亻
    - rén
    - person
  - 吏
    - lì
    - official
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - 亻 (rén, "person") as semantic + 吏 (lì, "official") as phonetic ->
    - causing or enabling something as an official or representative action
  - **interpretation:** The character 使 (shǐ, "cause; send; enable") combines the semantic component 亻 (rén, "person"), implying an action performed by a person, with the phonetic component 吏 (lì, "official"), which represents a hand holding a representative object. This combination suggests the meaning of sending or enabling as carried out by an ambassador or representative.
- **examples:**
  - 这(這)种(種)药(藥)使他的病情好转(轉)。
    - Zhè zhǒng yào shǐ tā de bìngqíng hǎozhuǎn.
    - This medicine caused his condition to improve.
  - 父亲(親)使我去城里买(買)东(東)西。
    - Fùqīn shǐ wǒ qù chéng lǐ mǎi dōngxi.
    - Father sent me to the city to buy things.
  - 新的法律使公司必须(須)遵循更严(嚴)格的标(標)准(準)。
    - Xīn de fǎlǜ shǐ gōngsī bìxū zūnxún gèng yángé de biāozhǔn.
    - The new law requires companies to adhere to stricter standards.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 使](@media/glyph4f7f.png)
### 使劲(勁)儿(兒) → 使 → 亻
- **definition:** person
- **pinyin:** rén
- **components:**
  - 人
    - rén
    - person
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Stylization of 人 (rén, "person") as a side radical to depict a person
  - **interpretation:** 亻 is a stylized form of 人 (rén, "person") used to indicate human-related meanings when combined with other components in characters as a radical. It visually represents a standing person, maintaining the core meaning of 'person' while facilitating the construction of complex characters.
- **examples:**
  - 他是一个(個)热(熱)心的人。
    - Tā shì yī gè rèxīn de rén.
    - He is a kind-hearted person.
  - 这(這)座城市里(裡)住着(著)很多优(優)秀的人。
    - Zhè zuò chéngshì lǐ zhùzhe hěn duō yōuxiù de rén.
    - There are many outstanding people living in this city.
  - 每个(個)人都有梦(夢)想。
    - Měi gè rén dōu yǒu mèngxiǎng.
    - Everyone has dreams.
### 使劲(勁)儿(兒) → 使 → 亻 → 人
- **definition:** person
- **pinyin:** rén
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts side view of a standing man, highlighting an arm and a leg ->
    - visual representation of a person
  - **interpretation:** The character 人 (rén, 'person') effectively uses simple lines to depict the essential form of a human, making it immediately recognizable and intuitive as meaning 'person.'
- **examples:**
  - 他是个(個)好人。
    - Tā shì gè hǎo rén.
    - He is a good person.
  - 每个(個)人都有责(責)任，为(為)社会(會)作出贡(貢)献(獻)。
    - Měi gè rén dōu yǒu zérèn, wèi shèhuì zuòchū gòngxiàn.
    - Every person has a responsibility to contribute to society.
  - 人在旅途中，心灵(靈)获(獲)得了成长(長)。
    - Rén zài lǚtú zhōng, xīnlíng huòdé le chéngzhǎng.
    - People gain growth along their journey.
- **historical forms:**

### 使劲(勁)儿(兒) → 使 → 吏
- **definition:** official
- **pinyin:** lì
- **components:**
  - 又
    - yòu
    - hand
  - 史
    - shǐ
    - history
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts 又 (yòu, "hand") holding a stylized flag or stick
  - **interpretation:** The character 吏(lì, "official") represents a hand holding a flag or stick, which is indicative of an official or ambassador role. It shares historical roots with 史 (shǐ, "history"), which originally depicted a similar figure. In 吏(lì), the stylized depiction of a tool in a hand signifies the function of an official or representative.
- **examples:**
  - 古代的官吏负(負)责(責)管理地方事务(務)。
    - Gǔdài de guānlì fùzé guǎnlǐ dìfāng shìwù.
    - Officials in ancient times were responsible for managing local affairs.
  - 这(這)位吏员(員)在衙门(門)工作。
    - Zhè wèi lì yuán zài yámén gōngzuò.
    - This official works in the government office.
  - 官吏的职(職)责(責)是为(為)百姓服务(務)。
    - Guānlì de zhízé shì wèi bǎixìng fúwù.
    - The duty of officials is to serve the people.

### 使劲(勁)儿(兒) → 使 → 吏 → 又
- **definition:** hand
- **pinyin:** yòu
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a right hand
  - **interpretation:** The character 又 (yòu, "hand") is a pictogram representing a right hand, showing the fingers and palm, which highlights its original meaning related to manual actions.
- **examples:**
  - 「又」这(這)个(個)字最早来(來)源于(於)手。
    - 「Yòu」 zhè gè zì zuì zǎo láiyuán yú shǒu。
    - The character '又' originally comes from the hand.
  - 很多汉(漢)字含有又部首，表示与(與)手有关(關)的动(動)作。
    - Hěn duō hànzì hányǒu Yòu bùshǒu, biǎoshì yǔ shǒu yǒuguān de dòngzuò。
    - Many Chinese characters include the '又' radical, indicating actions related to the hand.
  - 古人用又描绘(繪)手的形态(態)，体(體)现(現)了古汉(漢)字的独(獨)特魅力。
    - Gǔrén yòng Yòu miáohuì shǒu de xíngtài, tǐxiàn le gǔ hànzì de dútè mèilì。
    - Ancient people used '又' to depict the shape of the hand, showcasing the unique charm of ancient Chinese characters.

### 使劲(勁)儿(兒) → 使 → 吏 → 史
- **definition:** history
- **pinyin:** shǐ
- **components:**
  - 又
    - yòu
    - hand
  - 中
    - zhōng
    - middle
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a hand 又 holding a stylized flag 中 ->
    - original meaning 'representative, ambassador' ->
    - evolved to mean 'history'
  - **interpretation:** The character 史(shǐ, 'history') originated from the depiction of a hand holding a flag, symbolizing a representative or ambassador who would record events. Over time, this idea evolved to represent the recording of events as history.
- **examples:**
  - 中国(國)的历(歷)史悠久。
    - Zhōngguó de lìshǐ yōujiǔ.
    - China's history is long and rich.
  - 他对(對)世界历(歷)史很感兴(興)趣。
    - Tā duì shìjiè lìshǐ hěn gǎn xìngqù.
    - He is very interested in world history.
  - 历(歷)史可以教会(會)我们(們)很多东(東)西。
    - Lìshǐ kěyǐ jiāohuì wǒmen hěn duō dōngxī.
    - History can teach us many things.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 史](@media/glyph53f2.png)
### 使劲(勁)儿(兒) → 使 → 吏 → 史 → 中
- **definition:** middle
- **pinyin:** zhōng
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts an arrow piercing through the center of a target
  - **interpretation:** The character 中 (zhōng, "middle") visually represents an arrow passing through the central point of a target, illustrating the concept of 'center' or 'middle' effectively. This visual imagery is straightforward and memorable, corresponding closely with its meaning of being at the center or middle of something.
- **examples:**
  - 他站在道路中，看着(著)远(遠)方。
    - tā zhàn zài dàolù zhōng, kànzhe yuǎnfāng.
    - He stands in the middle of the road, gazing into the distance.
  - 房间(間)正中，挂(掛)着(著)一幅名画(畫)。
    - fángjiān zhèng zhōng, guàzhe yī fú mínghuà.
    - A famous painting hangs in the exact center of the room.

### 使劲(勁)儿(兒) → 劲(勁)
- **traditional:** 勁
- **definition:** strength; energy; enthusiasm
- **pinyin:** jìn
- **components:**
  - 力
    - lì
    - strength
  - 巠
    - jīng
    - stream
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:** semantic 力 (lì, "strength") + phonetic 巠 (jīng, "stream")
  - **interpretation:** The semantic component 力 (lì, "strength") directly conveys the meaning of physical power or strength. The phonetic component 巠 (jīng, "stream") contributes the pronunciation, connecting the imagery of flowing energy, which aligns with the sense of strength or vitality. This combination gives the character 勁(劲) (jìn, "strength; energy; enthusiasm"), carrying the sense of both physical and enthusiastic vigor.
  - **simplification:** 劲 is the simplified form of 勁, where the character 巠 (jīng, "stream") was removed, simplifying the stroke count while retaining 力 (lì, "strength") to maintain the core meaning.
- **examples:**
  - 他踢足球的时(時)候非常有劲(勁)。
    - Tā tī zúqiú de shíhòu fēicháng yǒu jìn.
    - He is very energetic when playing football.
  - 这(這)道菜有一种(種)特别(別)的劲(勁)。
    - Zhè dào cài yǒu yī zhǒng tèbié de jìn.
    - This dish has a special kick.
  - 加油！我们(們)还(還)有劲(勁)。
    - Jiāyóu! Wǒmen hái yǒu jìn.
    - Keep it up! We still have energy.
### 使劲(勁)儿(兒) → 劲(勁) → 力
- **definition:** strength
- **pinyin:** lì
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts either an arm bending out from the side of the body, or a wooden plough
  - **interpretation:** The character 力(lì, 'strength') visually represents physical power through the image of an arm or tool, emphasizing the fundamental concept of muscular force.
- **examples:**
  - 他用尽(盡)全力，赢(贏)得比赛(賽)。
    - Tā yòng jìn quánlì, yíng dé bǐsài.
    - He used all his strength to win the competition.
  - 他把力气(氣)用在学(學)习(習)上。
    - Tā bǎ lìqì yòng zài xuéxí shàng.
    - He applies his strength to his studies.
  - 面对(對)困难(難)，他毫不退缩(縮)，全力以赴。
    - Miànduì kùnnán, tā háo bù tuìsuō, quánlì yǐ fù.
    - Facing difficulties, he neither retreats nor gives up, but goes all out.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 力](@media/glyph529b.png)
### 使劲(勁)儿(兒) → 劲(勁) → 巠
- **definition:** stream
- **pinyin:** jīng
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts vertical threads passing through the top of a loom ->
    - ancient form of 經 (jīng, 'to abide by, to comply with')
  - **interpretation:** The character 巠(jīng, 'a rivulet') originally depicted threads going through a loom, symbolizing a path or guide. Over time, its application expanded in meaning to include the idea of things running or flowing through, thus lending itself to the concept of a small stream or rivulet.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 巠](@media/glyph5de0.png)
### 使劲(勁)儿(兒) → 儿(兒)
- **traditional:** 兒
- **definition:** child; diminutive; nominal suffix
- **pinyin:** ér
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts an infant with an imperfect cranium (fontanelle)
  - **interpretation:** The character 兒 (ér, "child") is a pictogram representing a child with a distinctive fontanelle, highlighting the child's young age and the characteristic soft spot on the head. This reflects the character's meaning as 'child.'
  - **simplification:** 儿 is a simplified and cursive form of 兒, representing a stylistic reduction of strokes while still retaining the essence of a child's figure.
- **examples:**
  - 这(這)个(個)小女孩喜欢(歡)唱歌。
    - Zhè gè xiǎo nǚhái xǐhuān chànggē.
    - This little girl likes to sing.
  - 他有一个(個)聪(聰)明的儿(兒)子。
    - Tā yǒu yī gè cōngmíng de érzi.
    - He has a smart son.
  - 每个(個)父母都希望自己的孩子健康快乐(樂)。
    - Měi gè fùmǔ dōu xīwàng zìjǐ de háizi jiànkāng kuàilè.
    - Every parent hopes their child is healthy and happy.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 儿](@media/glyph513f.png)
---
## 使劲(勁)儿(兒)
### shǐ jìnr
---
## exert oneself (physically)

## 亲(親)
---
## kiss
### qīn
---
- **traditional:** 親
- **definition:** kiss
- **pinyin:** qīn
- **components:**
  - 辛
    - xīn
    - bitter
  - 見
    - jiàn
    - see
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - phonetic 辛 (chisel) + semantic 見 (see) ->
    - stylized as 亲 (variant of 辛) ->
    - 親
  - **interpretation:** 親 (qīn, 'kiss') combines 辛 (xīn, 'chisel') phonetically with 見 (jiàn, 'see') semantically. The character suggests a close action that involves attentiveness, like seeing. The association with kissing likely comes from the intimate gesture of 'coming close to see'.
  - **simplification:** The traditional character 親 is simplified to 亲 by replacing 見 with the simpler component 见.
- **examples:**
  - 他轻(輕)轻(輕)地亲(親)了她的额(額)头(頭)。
    - Tā qīngqīng de qīn le tā de étóu.
    - He gently kissed her forehead.
  - 分手之后(後)，他们(們)没(沒)有再联(聯)系(繫)，也没(沒)有再亲(親)吻过(過)。
    - Fēnshǒu zhīhòu tāmen méiyǒu zài liánxì, yě méiyǒu zài qīnwěn guò.
    - After the breakup, they didn't contact each other again nor did they kiss anymore.
  - 他习(習)惯(慣)在睡前亲(親)她的脸(臉)颊(頰)。
    - Tā xíguàn zài shuì qián qīn tā de liǎnjiá.
    - He got used to kissing her cheek before sleep.
### 亲(親) → 辛
- **definition:** bitter
- **pinyin:** xīn
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a tool—chisel or awl—used to mark slaves and criminals ->
    - 辛
  - **interpretation:** The character 辛 (xīn) originally depicted a tool such as a chisel, used for marking or branding. The association with a sharp tool helps explain its extended meaning of 'spice,' as spices can have a pungent, sharp quality reminiscent of a tool's point or effect.
- **examples:**
  - 这(這)个(個)菜有一种(種)辛辣的味道。
    - Zhège cài yǒu yī zhǒng xīnlà de wèidào.
    - This dish has a spicy taste.
  - 他喜欢(歡)在食物里(裡)添加辛香料。
    - Tā xǐhuān zài shíwù lǐ tiānjiā xīn xiāngliào.
    - He likes to add spices to the food.
  - 这(這)种(種)辛口的调(調)料非常受欢(歡)迎。
    - Zhè zhǒng xīnkǒu de tiáoliào fēicháng shòu huānyíng.
    - This type of spicy seasoning is very popular.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 辛](@media/glyph8f9b.png)
### 亲(親) → 見
- **definition:** see
- **pinyin:** jiàn
- **components:**
  - 目
    - mù
    - eye
  - 卩
    - jié
    - kneeling person
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogrammic compound
  - **description:**
    - 目 (mù, "eye") + 卩 (jié, "kneeling person") =
    - a kneeling figure with large eye ->
    - see
  - **interpretation:** The combination of a human figure and an eye visually represents the act of seeing. The eye symbolizes vision, while the person emphasizes the human context of this action, making the meaning intuitive.
  - **simplification:** 见(見) is derived from using a cursive variant of the character in place of the traditional form.
- **examples:**
  - 我昨天见(見)到她。
    - Wǒ zuótiān jiàn dào tā.
    - I saw her yesterday.
  - 太阳(陽)升起时(時)，我看见(見)了大海。
    - Tàiyáng shēng qǐ shí, wǒ kàn jiàn le dàhǎi.
    - When the sun rose, I saw the sea.
  - 在公园(園)里(裡)，我见(見)到了老朋友。
    - Zài gōngyuán lǐ, wǒ jiàn dào le lǎo péngyǒu.
    - In the park, I met an old friend.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 見](@media/glyph898b.png)
### 亲(親) → 見 → 目
- **definition:** eye
- **pinyin:** mù
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a human eye, now represented and rotated 90 degrees ->
    - eye
  - **interpretation:** The character 目(mù, 'eye') is a pictogram representing a human eye. Its original orientation has changed over time, resembling an eye seen from a sideways view.
- **examples:**
  - 他的目光炯炯有神。
    - Tā de mùguāng jiǒngjiǒng yǒu shén.
    - His gaze is bright and full of spirit.
  - 她目不转(轉)睛，注视(視)前方。
    - Tā mù bù zhuǎn jīng, zhùshì qiánfāng.
    - She stared intently, gazing ahead.
  - 雄鹰(鷹)展翅，双(雙)目炯炯看天际(際)。
    - Xióng yīng zhǎn chì, shuāng mù jiǒngjiǒng kàn tiānjì.
    - The eagle spreads its wings, its eyes piercingly gaze at the horizon.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 目](@media/glyph76ee.png)
### 亲(親) → 見 → 卩
- **definition:** kneeling person
- **pinyin:** jié
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a kneeling person from sideview
  - **interpretation:** The character 卩 (jié, "kneeling person") is a simple pictogram showing the silhouette of a person kneeling. It is unrelated to other kneeling or similar figures in different contexts such as 欠 (qiàn, "yawn") where the mouth is open, or 女 (nǚ, "woman") where the figure represents a female. Its form is solely based on the posture of kneeling.
- **examples:**
  - 那位卩正虔诚(誠)祈祷(禱)。
    - Nà wèi jié zhèng qiánchéng qídǎo.
    - That kneeling person is praying devoutly.
  - 礼(禮)仪(儀)师(師)指出，卩代表谦(謙)卑与(與)敬意。
    - Lǐyí shī zhǐchū, jié dàibiǎo qiānbēi yǔ jìngyì.
    - The ritual master pointed out that the kneeling person represents humility and respect.
  - 在庄(莊)严(嚴)仪(儀)式中，卩象征(徵)着(著)内(內)心的虔敬。
    - Zài zhuāngyán yíshì zhōng, jié xiàngzhēngzhe nèixīn de qiánjìng.
    - In the solemn ceremony, the kneeling figure symbolizes inner devotion.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 卩](@media/glyph5369.png)
