## 打听(聽)
### dǎtīng
---
## ask about; inquire about
%%%
## 消息
---
## news; information
### xiāoxi
---
- **definition:** news; information
- **pinyin:** xiāoxi
- **components:**
  - 消
    - xiāo
    - to disappear; to eliminate
  - 息
    - xī
    - rest; interest; news
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** compound word
  - **description:** 消 (xiāo, "to disappear; to eliminate") + 息 (xī, "rest; interest; news")
  - **interpretation:** The word 消息 (xiāoxi) combines 消 (xiāo, "to disappear; to eliminate") with 息 (xī, "rest; interest; news") to imply the concept of news or information as something that comes and goes, flows, or spreads, much like the elimination of silence with the arrival of sound or news.
- **examples:**
  - 我收到了一条(條)好消息。
    - Wǒ shōudào le yī tiáo hǎo xiāoxi.
    - I received a piece of good news.
  - 他打电(電)话(話)告诉(訴)我一个(個)重要的消息。
    - Tā dǎ diànhuà gàosù wǒ yī gè zhòngyào de xiāoxi.
    - He called to tell me an important piece of information.
  - 这(這)条(條)消息引起了广(廣)泛的关(關)注。
    - Zhè tiáo xiāoxi yǐnqǐ le guǎngfàn de guānzhù.
    - This news attracted widespread attention.
### 消息 → 消
- **definition:** to disappear; to eliminate
- **pinyin:** xiāo
- **components:**
  - 氵(水)
    - shuǐ
    - water
  - 肖
    - xiāo
    - to resemble
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic 氵(水) (shuǐ, "water") + phonetic 肖 (xiāo) ->
    - to extinguish something (with water) ->
    - disappear; eliminate
  - **interpretation:** The character combines the semantic component 氵(水) (shuǐ, "water"), symbolizing extinguishing or quenching, with the phonetic component 肖 (xiāo) to convey the sense of causing something to disappear or be eliminated, similar to how water can extinguish a fire.
- **examples:**
  - 冰块(塊)在阳(陽)光下很快消失。
    - Bīngkuài zài yángguāng xià hěn kuài xiāoshī.
    - The ice cubes disappear quickly under the sunlight.
  - 那些负(負)面情绪(緒)慢慢地消散了。
    - Nàxiē fùmiàn qíngxù mànmàn de xiāosàn le.
    - Those negative emotions gradually dissipated.
  - 药(藥)物可以帮(幫)助消除疼痛。
    - Yàowù kěyǐ bāngzhù xiāochú téngtòng.
    - The medication can help eliminate pain.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 消](@media/glyph6d88.png)
### 消息 → 消 → 氵
- **definition:** water
- **pinyin:** shuǐ
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - 氵is the radical form of 水 (shuǐ, "water") ->
    - depicts flowing water, compressed and stylized next to characters.
  - **interpretation:** The character 氵is a simplified variant used as a radical to represent water-related meanings in other characters. It retains the flowing water depiction of 水 (shuǐ, "water") but is stylized to fit alongside other components.
- **examples:**
  - 水是生命之源。
    - Shuǐ shì shēngmìng zhī yuán.
    - Water is the source of life.
  - 汉(漢)字中偏旁氵，代表水。
    - Hànzì zhōng piān páng shuǐ, dàibiǎo shuǐ.
    - In Chinese characters, the radical '氵' signifies water.
  - 河水清澈透明，鱼(魚)儿(兒)欢(歡)快戏(戲)水。
    - Hé shuǐ qīngchè tòumíng, yú er huānkuaì xì shuǐ.
    - The river water is clear and transparent, and the fish happily play in it.
### 消息 → 消 → 肖
- **definition:** to resemble
- **pinyin:** xiāo
- **components:**
  - 小
    - xiǎo
    - small
  - 肉
    - ròu
    - meat
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - phonetic 小(xiǎo, "small") + semantic 肉(ròu, "meat") ->
    - resemble
  - **interpretation:** 肖(xiào, "resemble") combines the phonetic element 小(xiǎo, "small") to suggest its pronunciation with the semantic element 肉(ròu, "meat") indicating a connection to physical appearance. The core meaning 'resemble' arises from the idea of something appearing similar to another, as meat can take on various appearances, enhanced by the phonetic component.
- **examples:**
  - 这(這)幅画(畫)很好地描绘(繪)了他的肖像。
    - Zhè fú huà hěn hǎo de miáohuì le tā de xiàoxiàng.
    - This painting excellently depicts his likeness.
  - 他长(長)得很像他的父亲(親)。
    - Tā zhǎng de hěn xiàng tā de fùqīn.
    - He greatly resembles his father.
  - 这(這)个(個)模型逼真地模仿了原物。
    - Zhège móxíng bīzhēn de mófǎng le yuánwù.
    - This model realistically imitates the original.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 肖](@media/glyph8096.png)
### 消息 → 消 → 肖 → 小
- **definition:** small
- **pinyin:** xiǎo
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts three small dots arranged symmetrically to represent something small
  - **interpretation:** The character 小(xiǎo, 'small') uses three small strokes to symbolize size or quantity, visually capturing the essence of 'smallness'.
- **examples:**
  - 这(這)个(個)小猫(貓)很可爱(愛)。
    - Zhège xiǎo māo hěn kě'ài.
    - This small cat is very cute.
  - 这(這)座小桥(橋)横(橫)跨河流，连(連)接两(兩)岸。
    - Zhè zuò xiǎo qiáo héngkuà héliú, liánjiē liǎng àn.
    - This small bridge spans the river, connecting both banks.
  - 请(請)给(給)我一小杯水。
    - Qǐng gěi wǒ yī xiǎo bēi shuǐ.
    - Please give me a small cup of water.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 小](@media/glyph5c0f.png)
### 消息 → 消 → 肖 → 肉
- **definition:** meat
- **pinyin:** ròu
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a piece of flesh or meat with stripes representing texture.
  - **interpretation:** The character 肉(ròu, "flesh") depicts a piece of meat, meant to evoke the concept of flesh through its visual resemblance to a striped or sectioned piece of meat.
- **examples:**
  - 我喜欢(歡)吃肉。
    - Wǒ xǐhuān chī ròu.
    - I like eating meat.
  - 这(這)块(塊)肉很鲜(鮮)美，营(營)养(養)丰(豐)富。
    - Zhè kuài ròu hěn xiānměi, yíngyǎng fēngfù.
    - This piece of meat is very fresh and delicious, and it is nutritious.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 肉](@media/glyph8089.png)
### 消息 → 息
- **definition:** rest; interest; news
- **pinyin:** xī
- **components:**
  - 自
    - zì
    - nose
  - 心
    - xīn
    - heart
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogrammic compound
  - **description:**
    - 自 (zì, "nose") + 心 (xīn, "heart") =
    - breathe through one's nose ->
    - rest ->
    - extension to 'interest' and 'news'
  - **interpretation:** The character 息 (xī, "rest") combines 自 (zì, "nose") and 心 (xīn, "heart") to depict the act of breathing, emphasizing relaxation and rejuvenation. This concept naturally extends to 'interest', as interest accumulates steadily like breath, and 'news', which circulates and spreads like shared breaths.
- **examples:**
  - 我累了，需要休息。
    - Wǒ lèi le, xūyào xiūxī.
    - I am tired and need to rest.
  - 他在银(銀)行的存款有很高的利息。
    - Tā zài yínháng de cúnkuǎn yǒu hěn gāo de lìxī.
    - His bank deposit earns high interest.
  - 有人传(傳)来(來)了一则(則)趣闻(聞)，我们(們)都笑了。
    - Yǒurén chuánlái le yī zé qùwén, wǒmen dōu xiào le.
    - Someone shared an interesting piece of news, and we all laughed.
### 消息 → 息 → 自
- **definition:** nose
- **pinyin:** zì
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a nose ->
    - nose
  - **interpretation:** The character 自 (zì, "nose") is a pictogram representing the human nose, often used in ancient times to symbolize oneself, as pointing to the nose was a way of indicating oneself.
- **examples:**
  - 狗的自非常灵(靈)敏。
    - Gǒu de zì fēicháng língmǐn.
    - The dog's nose is very sensitive.
  - 他闻(聞)到花香，用自轻(輕)拂脸(臉)庞(龐)。
    - Tā wéndào huāxiāng, yòng zì qīngfú liǎnpáng.
    - He smelled the scent of flowers and softly brushed his nose against his cheek.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 自](@media/glyph81ea.png)
### 消息 → 息 → 心
- **definition:** heart
- **pinyin:** xīn
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a heart
  - **interpretation:** The character 心(xīn, "heart") originally depicted the shape of an actual heart, representing thoughts, emotions, and the core of a person. Over time, it has become highly stylized, but it continues to convey the notion of the heart as the center of emotions and consciousness.
- **examples:**
  - 她的心一直都在帮(幫)助别(別)人。
    - Tā de xīn yīzhí dōu zài bāngzhù biérén.
    - Her heart is always in helping others.
  - 在城市的中心，有一个(個)美丽(麗)的公园(園)。
    - Zài chéngshì de zhōngxīn, yǒu yí gè měilì de gōngyuán.
    - At the center of the city, there is a beautiful park.
  - 对(對)于(於)许(許)多人来(來)说(說)，家庭是生活的核心。
    - Duìyú xǔduō rén lái shuō, jiātíng shì shēnghuó de héxīn.
    - For many people, family is the core of life.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 心](@media/glyph5fc3.png)

## 广(廣)东(東)话(話)
---
## Cantonese; a Chinese dialect
### Guǎngdōnghuà
---
- **traditional:** 廣東話
- **definition:** Cantonese; a Chinese dialect
- **pinyin:** Guǎngdōnghuà
- **components:**
  - 廣
    - guǎng
    - broad
  - 東
    - dōng
    - east
  - 話
    - huà
    - speech; language
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** compound word
  - **description:** 廣 (guǎng, "broad") + 東 (dōng, "east") + 話 (huà, "speech; language") forms the name for a specific regional dialect often used by the people in the Guangdong province, leading to its designation.
  - **interpretation:** 廣 (guǎng, "broad") and 東 (dōng, "east") together refer to the Guangdong province, a region in the southeastern part of China known for its expanse to the east. 話 (huà, "speech; language") indicates the spoken language. Thus, 廣東話 (Guǎngdōnghuà) signifies the language of the broad eastern region, i.e., Cantonese, the specific language used predominantly by people in Guangdong.
- **examples:**
  - 很多香港人会(會)说(說)广(廣)东(東)话(話)。
    - Hěnduō Xiānggǎng rén huì shuō Guǎngdōnghuà.
    - Many people in Hong Kong can speak Cantonese.
  - 我学(學)习(習)广(廣)东(東)话(話)，因为(為)我想去广(廣)东(東)旅行。
    - Wǒ xuéxí Guǎngdōnghuà, yīnwèi wǒ xiǎng qù Guǎngdōng lǚxíng.
    - I study Cantonese because I want to travel to Guangdong.
  - 听(聽)懂广(廣)东(東)话(話)对(對)我来(來)说(說)有点(點)难(難)。
    - Tīng dǒng Guǎngdōnghuà duì wǒ lái shuō yǒudiǎn nán.
    - Understanding Cantonese is a bit difficult for me.
### 广(廣)东(東)话(話) → 廣
- **definition:** broad
- **pinyin:** guǎng
- **components:**
  - 广
    - guǎng
    - roof; shelter
  - 黃
    - huáng
    - yellow
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic 广 (roof; shelter) + phonetic 黃 (huáng, sound) ->
    - shelter
  - **interpretation:** The character 廣 (guǎng, 'shelter') combines the semantic component 广, which suggests the idea of covering or enclosure like a roof, with the phonetic component 黃 (huáng). The enclosure aspect of 广 underlines the meaning of providing shelter or an expansive space.
  - **simplification:** 廣 was simplified to 广 by retaining the roof radical but removing 黃, simplifying the structure considerably.
- **examples:**
  - 我们正在寻找一个可以提供广(廣)的地方。
    - Wǒmen zhèngzài xúnzhǎo yī gè kěyǐ tígōng guǎng de dìfāng.
    - We are looking for a place that can provide shelter.
  - 那里的广(廣)设施非常完善，适合长时间停留。
    - Nàlǐ de guǎng shèshī fēicháng wánshàn, shìhé cháng shíjiān tíngliú.
    - The shelter facilities there are very complete, suitable for long stays.
  - 如果有恶劣天气，我们需要一个广(廣)来保护自己。
    - Rúguǒ yǒu èliè tiānqì, wǒmen xūyào yī gè guǎng lái bǎohù zìjǐ.
    - If there is bad weather, we need a shelter to protect ourselves.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 廣](@media/glyph5ee3.png)
### 广(廣)东(東)话(話) → 廣 → 广(廣)
- **traditional:** 廣
- **definition:** roof; shelter
- **pinyin:** guǎng
- **components:**
  - 廣
    - guǎng
    - broad
  - 黃
    - huáng
    - yellow
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic 广(廣) (guǎng, "broad") + phonetic 黃 (huáng, "yellow") ->
    - broad
  - **interpretation:** The character 廣 (guǎng, "broad") combines the semantic element 广(廣), depicting a broad area or structure, with the phonetic element 黃 (huáng), which lends its sound. This combination signifies the idea of something wide or expansive.
  - **simplification:** 廣 was simplified to 广 by removing the 黃 (huáng, "yellow") phonetic component, leaving only the semantic element.
- **examples:**
  - 这(這)条(條)河非常广(廣)阔(闊)。
    - Zhè tiáo hé fēicháng guǎngkuò.
    - This river is very broad.
  - 他的知识(識)面很广(廣)，总(總)是能解决(決)问(問)题(題)。
    - Tā de zhīshì miàn hěn guǎng, zǒng shì néng jiějué wèntí.
    - His knowledge is broad, and he is always able to solve problems.
  - 在学(學)校里(裡)，他参(參)加了许(許)多广(廣)泛的活动(動)。
    - Zài xuéxiào lǐ, tā cānjiāle xǔduō guǎngfàn de huódòng.
    - At school, he participated in many broad activities.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 广](@media/glyph5e7f.png)
### 广(廣)东(東)话(話) → 廣 → 广(廣) → 黃
- **definition:** yellow
- **pinyin:** huáng
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Originally a pictogram depicting a disabled person or man with a ring of jade on the chest ->
    - phonetically borrowed for 'yellow' ->
    - 黃
  - **interpretation:** The character 黃 (huáng, 'yellow') originated from a pictogram representing either a disabled person or a man with a jade ring, showing a connection to cultural rituals or symbols of status. It was later phonetically borrowed to represent the color 'yellow' without semantic connection to its original depiction. In modern Chinese, its primary use is to denote the color yellow, disconnecting entirely from its debated pictographic origins.
- **examples:**
  - 这(這)朵花是黄(黃)色的。
    - Zhè duǒ huā shì huángsè de.
    - This flower is yellow.
  - 秋天来(來)临(臨)时(時)，树(樹)叶(葉)变(變)成金黄(黃)色。
    - Qiūtiān láilín shí, shùyè biàn chéng jīnhuáng sè.
    - When autumn arrives, the leaves turn golden yellow.
  - 他穿了一件黄(黃)色的外套。
    - Tā chuānle yī jiàn huángsè de wàitào.
    - He wore a yellow jacket.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 黃](@media/glyph9ec3.png)
### 广(廣)东(東)话(話) → 東
- **definition:** east
- **pinyin:** dōng
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a bundle or bag tied at both ends
  - **interpretation:** Originally depicting a bundle or bag tied at both ends, it suggests convergence or collection, visually resembling a tied shape. This pictorial representation is historically connected to the direction 'east', as a bag captures and holds items, analogous to the rising sun being 'held' in the east. Despite alternative interpretations involving the sun and tree, the pictogram of a bundle remains the most direct visual link.
- **examples:**
  - 他的東里(裏)装(裝)满(滿)了书(書)。
    - Tā de dōng lǐ zhuāng mǎn le shū.
    - His bag is full of books.
  - 她买(買)了一个(個)新的東。
    - Tā mǎi le yī gè xīn de dōng.
    - She bought a new bag.
  - 在办(辦)公室里(裏)，他的東总(總)是放在椅子后(後)面。
    - Zài bàngōngshì lǐ, tā de dōng zǒng shì fàng zài yǐzi hòumiàn.
    - In the office, his bag is always placed behind the chair.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 東](@media/glyph6771.png)
### 广(廣)东(東)话(話) → 話
- **definition:** speech; language
- **pinyin:** huà
- **components:**
  - 言
    - yán
    - word
  - 𠯑
    - gro
    - carry out, perform
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic 言 (yán, "word") + phonetic 𠯑 ->
    - speech; language
  - **interpretation:** The character 話 (huà) combines the semantic component 言 (yán, "word"), indicating speech or language, with a phonetic component 𠯑, which provides the sound. The semantic link with 言 aligns with the character's meaning of speech or language.
  - **simplification:** 話 was simplified to 话 by replacing 言 with 讠, reducing strokes using a cursive shorthand for the speech radical.
- **examples:**
  - 老师(師)正在讲(講)课(課)，学(學)生们(們)认(認)真听(聽)话(話)。
    - Lǎoshī zhèngzài jiǎngkè, xuéshēngmen rènzhēn tīnghuà.
    - The teacher is giving a lecture, and the students are listening attentively.
  - 他说(說)了一句感人的话(話)，让(讓)大家都为(為)之动(動)容。
    - Tā shuōle yī jù gǎnrén de huà, ràng dàjiā dōu wèi zhī dòngróng.
    - He said a moving statement, which touched everyone deeply.
  - 我们(們)每天都用普通话(話)交流。
    - Wǒmen měitiān dōu yòng pǔtōnghuà jiāoliú.
    - We use Mandarin to communicate every day.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 話](@media/glyph8a71.png)
### 广(廣)东(東)话(話) → 話 → 言
- **definition:** word
- **pinyin:** yán
- **components:**
  - 舌
    - shé
    - tongue
  - 口
    - kǒu
    - mouth
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogram
  - **description:**
    - 舌 (mouth with a forked tongue) with added stroke at top to suggest tongue movement ->
    - speech
  - **interpretation:** The character 言(yán, "speech") depicts the addition of a horizontal stroke to the ancient form of 舌(shé, "tongue") to indicate the motion of the tongue as it moves to articulate speech. This directly connects the organ involved in speaking to the concept of speech itself.
- **examples:**
  - 他的言语(語)充满(滿)智慧。
    - Tā de yányǔ chōngmǎn zhìhuì.
    - His speech is full of wisdom.
  - 我们(們)应(應)该(該)以行动(動)证(證)明我们(們)的言词(詞)。
    - Wǒmen yīnggāi yǐ xíngdòng zhèngmíng wǒmen de yáncí.
    - We should prove our words with actions.
  - 他说(說)话(話)的方式显(顯)示了他的修养(養)。
    - Tā shuōhuà de fāngshì xiǎnshìle tā de xiūyǎng.
    - The way he speaks shows his refinement.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 言](@media/glyph8a00.png)
### 广(廣)东(東)话(話) → 話 → 言 → 舌
- **definition:** tongue
- **pinyin:** shé
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a forked tongue emerging upwards from a mouth
  - **interpretation:** The character 舌(shé, 'tongue') visually represents a tongue extending out from a mouth, which aligns with its meaning. This direct depiction makes it easy to remember its association with speech and taste in its semantic family, also relating to words like 言(yán, 'word').
- **examples:**
  - 他的舌非常灵(靈)敏。
    - Tā de shé fēicháng língmǐn.
    - His tongue is very sensitive.
  - 品尝(嚐)美食时(時)，他的舌细(細)品滋味。
    - Pǐncháng měishí shí, tā de shé xì pǐn zīwèi.
    - While tasting delicious food, his tongue savors every flavor.
  - 他长(長)舌无(無)忌，经(經)常泄露秘密。
    - Tā chángshé wújì, jīngcháng xièlòu mìmì.
    - He is talkative and often spills secrets.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 舌](@media/glyph820c.png)
### 广(廣)东(東)话(話) → 話 → 言 → 口
- **definition:** mouth
- **pinyin:** kǒu
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts an open mouth.
  - **interpretation:** The character 口(kǒu, 'mouth') is a straightforward pictogram that visually represents an open mouth. It is a fundamental character in the Chinese language, often used both as an independent word and as a component in more complex characters, lending a semantic association to ideas relating to speech, openings, or enclosures.
- **examples:**
  - 他张(張)开(開)口，大声(聲)喊叫。
    - Tā zhāngkāi kǒu, dàshēng hǎnjiào.
    - He opened his mouth and shouted loudly.
  - 这(這)口饭(飯)入口即化。
    - Zhè kǒu fàn rùkǒu jíhuà.
    - This mouthful of food melts in your mouth.
  - 小女孩咬了一口苹(蘋)果，露出甜美的笑容。
    - Xiǎo nǚhái yǎole yī kǒu píngguǒ, lùchū tiánměi de xiàoróng.
    - The little girl took a bite of the apple and smiled sweetly.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 口](@media/glyph53e3.png)
### 广(廣)东(東)话(話) → 話 → 𠯑
- **definition:** carry out, perform
- **pinyin:** gro
- **components:**
  - 氏
    - shì
    - movement
  - 日
    - rì
    - sun
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogrammic compound
  - **description:**
    - 氏氏 (movement) + 日 (sun) ->
    - twilight or nightfall, when sun is lowered
  - **interpretation:** The character 𠯑 combines 氏 (shì, "movement") with 日 (rì, "sun") to visually represent the concept of twilight or nightfall, a time when the sun lowers below the horizon. As the sun transitions into this downward position, it symbolically signifies the idea of concluding or carrying out activities as the day ends, which connects to broader meanings of performing or carrying out tasks.
### 广(廣)东(東)话(話) → 話 → 𠯑 → 氏
- **definition:** movement
- **pinyin:** shì
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a man bending over or holding an object ->
    - later forms included decoration ->
    - final form with a stroke
  - **interpretation:** The character 氏 (shì, "clan") is a pictogram that has undergone several interpretations. It may represent a figure bending over to sow a field or other activities, capturing the act of forming or being part of a group or collective effort, which aligns with the meaning of 'clan' as an extended family or group.
- **examples:**
  - 这(這)个(個)村庄(莊)所有的人都是李氏。
    - Zhège cūnzhuāng suǒyǒu de rén dōu shì Lǐ shì.
    - Everyone in this village belongs to the Li clan.
  - 春秋时(時)期，各个(個)氏族之间(間)常常发(發)生冲(衝)突。
    - Chūnqiū shíqī, gège shìzú zhījiān chángcháng fāshēng chōngtú.
    - During the Spring and Autumn period, conflicts often occurred between different clans.
  - 她是一个(個)非常古老氏族的后(後)裔。
    - Tā shì yīgè fēicháng gǔlǎo shìzú de hòuyì.
    - She is a descendant of a very ancient clan.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 氏](@media/glyph6c0f.png)
### 广(廣)东(東)话(話) → 話 → 𠯑 → 日
- **definition:** sun
- **pinyin:** rì
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts the sun; a dot or line added in the center to distinguish from similar characters e.g. 囗
  - **interpretation:** As a pictogram, 日(rì, 'sun') directly represents the sun. In ancient times, the added dot helped visually differentiate it from other characters. This is analogous to the astronomical symbol ☉ and Egyptian hieroglyph 𓇳, both depicting the sun.
- **examples:**
  - 晨曦来(來)临(臨)时(時)，日出东(東)方。
    - Chénxī láilín shí, rìchū dōngfāng.
    - At the break of dawn, the sun rises in the east.
  - 温(溫)暖的日光洒(灑)满(滿)大地。
    - Wēnnuǎn de rìguāng sǎ mǎn dàdì.
    - The warm sunlight spreads over the earth.
  - 中午时(時)分，日高挂(掛)天。
    - Zhōngwǔ shífēn, rì gāo guà tiān.
    - At noon, the sun hangs high in the sky.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 日](@media/glyph65e5.png)

## 广(廣)东(東)话(話)
### Guǎngdōnghuà

## Cantonese; a Chinese dialect
%%%
## 进(進)入
---
## enter; get into
### jìnrù
---
- **traditional:** 進入
- **definition:** enter; get into
- **pinyin:** jìnrù
- **components:**
  - 进(進)
    - jìn
    - advance; move forward
  - 入
    - rù
    - enter; join; get into; go in
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** compound word
  - **description:** 進 (jìn, "advance") conveys moving forward or ahead, suggesting motion or progression into something. 入 (rù, "enter") directly means to step into or become part of a space or realm, conveying entry.
  - **interpretation:** 進 (jìn, "advance") implies moving forward towards a destination. 入 (rù, "enter") suggests completing the motion of crossing a boundary into a new space. Combine these to express the idea of 'entering' as moving forward into a space or state.
- **examples:**
  - 我们(們)进(進)入公园(園)。
    - Wǒmen jìnrù gōngyuán.
    - We entered the park.
  - 请(請)在进(進)入房间(間)前脱(脫)鞋。
    - Qǐng zài jìnrù fángjiān qián tuōxié.
    - Please remove your shoes before entering the room.
  - 他进(進)入大学(學)后(後)学(學)习(習)很勤奋(奮)。
    - Tā jìnrù dàxué hòu xuéxí hěn qínfèn.
    - He studied diligently after entering the university.
### 进(進)入 → 进(進)
- **traditional:** 進
- **definition:** advance; move forward
- **pinyin:** jìn
- **components:**
  - 辵
    - chuò
    - walk; movement
  - 隹
    - zhuī
    - short-tail bird
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogrammic compound
  - **description:**
    - 辵 ('walk/movement') + 隹 (zhuī, 'short-tail bird') =
    - a bird that can only move forward
  - **interpretation:** The character 進 (jìn, 'to advance') combines the idea of movement with the imagery of a bird, symbolizing forward movement, as the bird naturally progresses forward on foot.
  - **simplification:** 進 was simplified to 进(進) by replacing the phonetic component 隹 (zhuī, 'short-tail bird') with 井 (jǐng, 'well') to reduce strokes.
- **examples:**
  - 他决(決)定继(繼)续(續)努力，以便在职(職)业(業)生涯中进(進)步。
    - Tā juédìng jìxù nǔlì, yǐbiàn zài zhíyè shēngyá zhōng jìnbù.
    - He decided to keep working hard in order to advance in his career.
  - 在我们(們)进(進)入隧道时(時)，速度变(變)得越来(來)越快。
    - Zài wǒmen jìnrù suìdào shí, sùdù biàn de yuè lái yuè kuài.
    - As we entered the tunnel, the speed became faster and faster.
  - 大门(門)刚(剛)一打开(開)，他就立刻走了进(進)去。
    - Dàmén gāng yī dǎkāi, tā jiù lìkè zǒu le jìnqù.
    - As soon as the door opened, he immediately walked in.
### 进(進)入 → 进(進) → 辵
- **definition:** walk; movement
- **pinyin:** chuò
- **components:**
  - 彳
    - chì
    - walk
  - 止
    - zhǐ
    - foot
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogrammic compound
  - **description:**
    - 彳 (chì, "walk") + 止 (zhǐ, "foot" or "to stop") ->
    - 𣥆 ->
    - stylized as 龰 ->
    - 辵
  - **interpretation:** The character 辵 combines 彳 (chì, "walk"), which represents movement, with 止 (zhǐ, "foot" or "to stop"), suggesting the concept of stepping or traveling forward. This character represents the idea of movement, particularly the action of walking or traveling, as originally depicted by the more conservative form 𣥆. Over time, the bottom component has been stylized as 龰, forming the current representation.
- **examples:**
  - 他辵在乡(鄉)间(間)的小路上。
    - Tā chuò zài xiāngjiān de xiǎolù shàng.
    - He walks on the rural path.
  - 晨光洒(灑)满(滿)大地，他辵出门(門)开(開)始旅程。
    - Chén guāng sǎ mǎn dàdì, tā chuò chūmén kāishǐ lǚchéng.

### 进(進)入 → 进(進) → 辵 → 止
- **definition:** foot
- **pinyin:** zhǐ
- **components:**
  - 趾
    - zhǐ
    - foot
  - 龰
    - yù
    - stylized feet
  - 手
    - shǒu
    - hand
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Original: Foot pointing up with 3 toes and a sole ->
    - Stylized as 龰 ->
    - Derivative 趾 refers to original 'foot' meaning
  - **interpretation:** Originally depicting a footprint with toes and a sole, 止 (zhǐ, "foot") represents the foot. The character's form resembles a foot with three toes, analogous to how the hand is represented with fingers in other characters.
- **examples:**
  - 他受伤(傷)的止需要静(靜)养(養)。
    - Tā shòu shāng de zhǐ xū yào jìng yǎng.

### 进(進)入 → 进(進) → 辵 → 止 → 趾
- **definition:** foot
- **pinyin:** zhǐ
- **components:**
  - 足
    - zú
    - foot
  - 止
    - zhǐ
    - halt
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic 足 (zú, "foot") + phonetic 止 (zhǐ) ->
    - toe
  - **interpretation:** The character combines 足 (zú, "foot"), indicating the general area involved, with 止 (zhǐ) providing the sound and potentially suggesting the idea of a part of the foot that 'halts' or 'stops' progression, which naturally leads to the notion of a toe.
- **examples:**
  - 他的脚(腳)趾受伤(傷)了。
    - Tā de jiǎozhǐ shòushāng le.
    - His toe is injured.
  - 她用脚(腳)趾轻(輕)轻(輕)地踢了一下球。
    - Tā yòng jiǎozhǐ qīngqīng de tī le yīxià qiú.
    - She gently kicked the ball with her toe.
  - 在沙滩(灘)上散步时(時)，我感受到沙子在我的脚(腳)趾间(間)流动(動)。
    - Zài shātān shàng sànbù shí, wǒ gǎnshòu dào shāzi zài wǒ de jiǎozhǐ jiān liúdòng.
    - While walking on the beach, I felt the sand flowing between my toes.
### 进(進)入 → 进(進) → 辵 → 止 → 趾 → 足
- **definition:** foot
- **pinyin:** zú
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a leg ->
    - originally depicted as ⽦ ->
    - represents 'foot'
  - **interpretation:** The character 足(zú, 'foot') is a pictographic representation of a human leg, which directly portrays the concept of a 'foot'. The pictographic origin emphasizes its fundamental meaning in the language.
- **examples:**
  - 他受伤(傷)后(後)，他的足不能动(動)。

### 进(進)入 → 进(進) → 辵 → 止 → 龰
- **definition:** stylized feet
- **pinyin:** yù
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a stylized footprint pointing upward ->
    - originally meaning 'foot' ->
    - later forms like 趾 (zhǐ, 'toe') refer back to original meaning
  - **interpretation:** 龰 (yù, 'stylized feet') is a pictogram showing a footprint pointing up, originally indicating the concept of a foot. The character 趾 (zhǐ, 'toe') evolved from this and retains the reference to the original meaning. It visually resembles a sole with three toes, similar to representations of the human hand in characters like 爪 (zhuǎ, 'claw'), 寸 (cùn, 'inch'), and 又 (yòu, 'again').
### 进(進)入 → 进(進) → 辵 → 止 → 手
- **definition:** hand
- **pinyin:** shǒu
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a hand with fingers; top stroke is a bent over middle finger, horizontal strokes represent fingers
  - **interpretation:** The character 手 (shǒu, "hand") is a direct pictorial representation of a human hand with all five fingers, which distinguishes it from similar characters representing claws or simplified fingers. This visually conveys its meaning as a hand clearly.
- **examples:**
  - 他用手写(寫)字。
    - Tā yòng shǒu xiě zì.
    - He writes with his hand.
  - 妈(媽)妈(媽)牵(牽)着(著)我的手走路。
    - Māmā qiān zhe wǒ de shǒu zǒu lù.
    - Mom holds my hand while walking.
  - 他的手很温(溫)暖，带(帶)给(給)我力量。
    - Tā de shǒu hěn wēn nuǎn, dài gěi wǒ lìliàng.
    - His hand is very warm, giving me strength.

    - yǎo

    - wéi
    - only

  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a short‐tailed bird (e.g., a sparrow) ->
    - also original form of 唯 (wéi, "only") before evolution into 鷕 (yǎo, "cry of a bird")
  - **interpretation:** 隹 (zhuī, "short-tailed bird") is a pictogram representing a bird with a short tail. Its depiction served as the foundation for other characters related to birds, such as 鷕 (yǎo, "cry of a bird").
- **examples:**
  - 这(這)只短尾的隹在树(樹)林中飞(飛)翔。

    - Bówùguǎn lǐ zhǎnchūle yī jiàn yǐ zhuī wèi tícái de gǔdài huìhuà.
    - The museum displays an ancient painting themed on the short-tailed bird.
  - 远(遠)古诗(詩)篇中常用隹来(來)象征(徵)自由，寓意生动(動)。
    - Yuǎngǔ shīpiān zhōng cháng yòng zhuī lái xiàngzhēng zìyóu, yùyì shēngdòng.
    - In ancient poems, the short-tailed bird is often used to symbolize freedom, conveying vivid meaning.

    - only

    - niǎo
    - bird

    - cry of a bird

### 进(進)入 → 进(進) → 隹 → 鷕 → 唯
- **definition:** only
- **pinyin:** wéi
- **components:**
  - 口
    - kǒu
    - mouth
  - 隹
    - zhuī
    - short-tailed bird
  - 鷕
    - yǎo
    - cry of a bird
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic 口 (kǒu, "mouth") + phonetic 隹 (zhuī, "short-tailed bird") ->
    - original form of 鷕 ->
    - borrowed phonetically for 'only'
  - **interpretation:** The character 唯 originally represented the cry of a bird, with the mouth radical indicating the sound aspect. It was later phonetically borrowed for the abstract meaning 'only', without retaining its original context related to bird sounds.
- **examples:**
  - 唯有努力，才能成功。
    - Wéi yǒu nǔlì, cái néng chénggōng.

    - Wéi yǒu zài ānjìng de yèwǎn, wǒ cái néng tīng qīng zìjǐ de xīnshēng.
    - Only in the quiet of the night can I hear my own heart.
  - 我唯爱(愛)读(讀)书(書)，因为(為)书(書)籍能带(帶)给(給)我无(無)限的可能。
    - Wǒ wéi ài dúshū, yīnwèi shūjí néng dài gěi wǒ wúxiàn de kěnéng.

### 进(進)入 → 进(進) → 隹 → 鷕 → 唯 → 口

- **pinyin:** kǒu
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts an open mouth.
  - **interpretation:** The character 口(kǒu, 'mouth') is a straightforward pictogram that visually represents an open mouth. It is a fundamental character in the Chinese language, often used both as an independent word and as a component in more complex characters, lending a semantic association to ideas relating to speech, openings, or enclosures.
- **examples:**

  - 小女孩咬了一口苹(蘋)果，露出甜美的笑容。
    - Xiǎo nǚhái yǎole yī kǒu píngguǒ, lùchū tiánměi de xiàoróng.

## 进(進)入
### jìnrù

## enter; get into

## 梦(夢)
---
## dream
### mèng
---
- **traditional:** 夢
- **definition:** dream
- **pinyin:** mèng
- **components:**
  - 爿
    - pán
    - bed
  - 人
    - rén
    - person
  - 目
    - mù
    - eye
  - 夕
    - xī
    - night
  - 瞢
    - méng
    - bewildered
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - Oracle bone script: person 人 (rén, 'person') lying on bed 爿 (pán, 'bed') + eye 目 (mù, 'eye') with emphasis ->
    - Bronze inscriptions: 目 with eyebrows 眉 + person as dots + moon 夕 (xī, 'night') added ->
    - 夢: eyebrows 卝 + eyes 罒 + person's body 冖 + 夕 ->
    - phono-semantic compound: phonetic 瞢 + semantic 夕
  - **interpretation:** In the oracle bone script, 夢 evokes a person on a bed with an emphasized eye, suggesting a state of being where one's vision is active despite resting, which aligns with dreaming. By the Bronze inscriptions, with the addition of 夕, it highlights the nocturnal and unconscious nature of dreams. Modern 夢 combines phonetic 瞢 with semantic 夕, reflecting dreaming as something occurring at night.
  - **simplification:** 梦 is a simplified form of 夢 where 目 + 冖 is simplified to a simpler eye component and 冖.
- **examples:**
  - 我昨晚做了一个(個)美好的梦(夢)。
    - Wǒ zuó wǎn zuò le yī gè měihǎo de mèng.
    - I had a wonderful dream last night.
  - 她希望有一天能实(實)现(現)自己的梦(夢)想。
    - Tā xīwàng yǒu yī tiān néng shíxiàn zìjǐ de mèngxiǎng.
    - She hopes to fulfill her dreams one day.
  - 每个(個)人都应(應)该(該)追寻(尋)自己的梦(夢)。
    - Měi gè rén dōu yīnggāi zhuīxún zìjǐ de mèng.
    - Everyone should pursue their own dreams.
### 梦(夢) → 爿
- **definition:** bed
- **pinyin:** pán
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a bed ->
    - original form of 牀 (chuáng, "bed") ->
    - contracted form in 臧 (zāng, "possess")
  - **interpretation:** The character 爿 (pán, "bed") visually represents a bed, emphasizing its usage in denoting places for resting or sleeping. It served as the original form for the character 牀 (chuáng, "bed"), reinforcing its meaning. Additionally, in the character 臧 (zāng, "possess"), it appears as a contracted form, reflecting its historical usage in composite forms.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 爿](@media/glyph723f.png)
### 梦(夢) → 人
- **definition:** person
- **pinyin:** rén
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts side view of a standing man, highlighting an arm and a leg ->
    - visual representation of a person
  - **interpretation:** The character 人 (rén, 'person') effectively uses simple lines to depict the essential form of a human, making it immediately recognizable and intuitive as meaning 'person.'
- **examples:**
  - 他是个(個)好人。
    - Tā shì gè hǎo rén.
    - He is a good person.
  - 每个(個)人都有责(責)任，为(為)社会(會)作出贡(貢)献(獻)。
    - Měi gè rén dōu yǒu zérèn, wèi shèhuì zuòchū gòngxiàn.
    - Every person has a responsibility to contribute to society.
  - 人在旅途中，心灵(靈)获(獲)得了成长(長)。
    - Rén zài lǚtú zhōng, xīnlíng huòdé le chéngzhǎng.

### 梦(夢) → 目
- **definition:** eye
- **pinyin:** mù
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a human eye, now represented and rotated 90 degrees ->
    - eye
  - **interpretation:** The character 目(mù, 'eye') is a pictogram representing a human eye. Its original orientation has changed over time, resembling an eye seen from a sideways view.
- **examples:**
  - 他的目光炯炯有神。
    - Tā de mùguāng jiǒngjiǒng yǒu shén.
    - His gaze is bright and full of spirit.
  - 她目不转(轉)睛，注视(視)前方。
    - Tā mù bù zhuǎn jīng, zhùshì qiánfāng.
    - She stared intently, gazing ahead.

    - Xióng yīng zhǎn chì, shuāng mù jiǒngjiǒng kàn tiānjì.

### 梦(夢) → 夕
- **definition:** night
- **pinyin:** xī
- **components:**
  - 月
    - yuè
    - moon
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a moon crescent
  - **interpretation:** The character 夕 (xī, 'evening') is a pictogram that represents a crescent moon, capturing the image of the moon in the evening sky. The comparison to 月 (yuè, 'moon') underscores its depiction of the moon phase commonly associated with evening.
- **examples:**
  - 夕阳(陽)西下。
    - xī yáng xīxià.
    - The setting sun descends.
  - 夕阳(陽)西下，晚风(風)徐徐。
    - xī yáng xīxià, wǎn fēng xúxú.
    - The sun sets as the gentle evening breeze blows.

### 梦(夢) → 夕 → 月
- **definition:** moon
- **pinyin:** yuè
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a crescent moon
  - **interpretation:** The character 月(yuè, "moon") is a pictographic representation of a crescent moon, straightforwardly capturing the curved shape often associated with the moon's appearance. Though interchangeable with 夕 (xī, "evening") in the past, it distinctly represents the moon in this usage.
- **examples:**
  - 夜空挂(掛)着(著)明月。
    - Yè kōng guà zhe míng yuè.
    - The bright moon hangs in the night sky.
  - 人们(們)赏(賞)月，寄托(託)相思。
    - Rén men shǎng yuè, jì tuō xiāng sī.
    - People enjoy the moon, expressing their longing.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 月](@media/glyph6708.png)
### 梦(夢) → 瞢
- **definition:** bewildered
- **pinyin:** méng
- **components:**
  - 目
    - mù
    - eye
  - 亡
    - wáng
    - departed; gone; lost
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic 目 (mù, "eye") + phonetic 亡 (wáng) ->
    - sense of being lost or disoriented, particularly in vision ->
    - bewildered
  - **interpretation:** The character combines 目 (mù, "eye") as the semantic component with 亡 (wáng) as the phonetic component, suggesting a state where one's vision is metaphorically lost or confused, reflecting the meaning of being bewildered.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 瞢](@media/glyph77a2.png)
### 梦(夢) → 瞢 → 亡
- **definition:** departed; gone; lost
- **pinyin:** wáng
- **components:**
  - 刀
    - dāo
    - knife
  - 芒
    - máng
    - edge of a knife
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogram
  - **description:**
    - A line on 刀 (dāo, 'knife') ->
    - cutting edge of a knife ->
    - original form of 芒 (máng, 'edge of a knife')
  - **interpretation:** The character depicts a line on a knife, representing the sharp edge. This connection to sharpness and cutting leads to the concept of 'perish,' as an edge can cut or end something, symbolically indicating destruction or the end of life.
- **examples:**
  - 战(戰)士们(們)在战(戰)场(場)上英勇战(戰)斗(鬥)，许(許)多人不幸亡。
    - Zhànshìmen zài zhànchǎng shàng yīngyǒng zhàndòu, xǔduō rén bùxìng wáng.
    - The soldiers fought bravely on the battlefield, and many unfortunately perished.
  - 如果不努力经(經)营(營)，这(這)家公司可能会(會)亡。
    - Rúguǒ bù nǔlì jīngyíng, zhè jiā gōngsī kěnéng huì wáng.
    - If the company does not operate diligently, it may perish.
  - 古代帝国(國)由于(於)内(內)外问(問)题(題)而一朝亡。
    - Gǔdài dìguó yóuyú nèiwài wèntí ér yī zhāo wáng.
    - The ancient empire perished overnight due to internal and external issues.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 亡](@media/glyph4ea1.png)
### 梦(夢) → 瞢 → 亡 → 刀
- **definition:** knife
- **pinyin:** dāo
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a knife
  - **interpretation:** 刀 (dāo, "knife") is a pictographic representation of a knife or blade, with a sharp edge and a handle, resembling the form of a basic cutting tool.
- **examples:**
  - 他用锋(鋒)利的刀，切开(開)蔬菜。
    - tā yòng fēnglì de dāo, qiē kāi shūcài.
    - He uses a sharp knife to cut vegetables.
  - 这(這)把刀非常锋(鋒)利。
    - zhè bǎ dāo fēicháng fēnglì.
    - This knife is very sharp.
  - 厨(廚)师(師)小心地持刀，为(為)客人切肉。
    - chúshī xiǎoxīn de chí dāo, wèi kèrén qiē ròu.
    - The chef holds the knife carefully and slices meat for the guest.

### 梦(夢) → 瞢 → 亡 → 芒
- **definition:** edge of a knife
- **pinyin:** máng
- **components:**
  - 艹
    - cǎo
    - grass
  - 亡
    - wáng
    - to flee
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic 艹 (cǎo, "grass") + phonetic 亡 (wáng) ->
    - edge of a knife
  - **interpretation:** The character 芒(máng, "edge of a knife") uses the 艹 (cǎo, "grass") component to highlight its relation to plant life or natural elements, while 亡 (wáng) provides the phonetic indication. Originally it may have depicted something like 方 but evolved to illustrate the thinness or sharpness of grass edges, metaphorically linking to the sharp edge of a knife.
- **examples:**
  - 刀的芒在阳(陽)光下闪(閃)闪(閃)发(發)光。
    - Dāo de máng zài yángguāng xià shǎnshǎn fāguāng.

  - 我们(們)要小心刀的芒，因为(為)它非常锋(鋒)利。

    - We must be careful of the knife's edge because it is very sharp.
  - 他用手指轻(輕)轻(輕)触(觸)摸刀的芒，感受到它的锋(鋒)利。
    - Tā yòng shǒuzhǐ qīngqīng chùmō dāo de máng, gǎnshòudào tā de fēnglì.
    - He gently touched the blade's edge with his finger and felt its sharpness.
- **historical forms:**

### 梦(夢) → 瞢 → 亡 → 芒 → 艹
- **definition:** grass
- **pinyin:** cǎo
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts blades of grass
  - **interpretation:** 艹 is a pictogram representing grass or plants, resembling blades of grass. It is commonly used as a radical in other characters related to grass or vegetation.
- **examples:**

    - When spring arrives, grass grows rapidly.

## 一生
---
## all one's life; a lifetime
### yìshēng
---
- **definition:** all one's life; a lifetime
- **pinyin:** yìshēng
- **components:**
  - 一
    - yī
    - one; single; whole
  - 生
    - shēng
    - life; birth; alive; grow
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** compound word
  - **description:** 一 (yī, "one") indicates a singularity or unity, while 生 (shēng, "life") signifies the concept of living or existence. Combined, they refer to everything from birth to death, encapsulating a complete span of life.
  - **interpretation:** The word 一生 (yìshēng) portrays the idea of a single, complete life journey. 一 (yī, "one") emphasizes the entirety or singularity of one's existence, while 生 (shēng, "life") denotes the period of living from birth to death. Together, they convey the notion of an individual's entire life span.
- **examples:**
  - 他一生都在追求梦(夢)想。
    - Tā yìshēng dōu zài zhuīqiú mèngxiǎng.
    - He spent all his life chasing dreams.
  - 她一生中最快乐(樂)的时(時)光是和家人在一起。
    - Tā yìshēng zhōng zuì kuàilè de shíguāng shì hé jiārén zài yīqǐ.
    - Her happiest times in life were spent with her family.
  - 老师(師)把他的一生都奉献(獻)给(給)了教育事业(業)。
    - Lǎoshī bǎ tā de yìshēng dōu fèngxiàn gěi le jiàoyù shìyè.
    - The teacher devoted his entire life to the cause of education.
### 一生 → 一
- **definition:** one; single; whole
- **pinyin:** yī
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogram
  - **description:** A horizontal stroke representing the concept of 'one'.
  - **interpretation:** The character 一(yī, "one") is a simple horizontal line signifying the singular and unified concept of 'one'. It directly represents being singular or the number one.
- **examples:**
  - 我有一个(個)苹(蘋)果。
    - Wǒ yǒu yī gè píngguǒ.
    - I have one apple.
  - 他只看到一只(隻)鸟(鳥)，飞(飛)进(進)了花园(園)。
    - Tā zhǐ kàn dào yī zhī niǎo, fēi jìn le huā yuán.
    - He only saw one bird, which flew into the garden.
  - 一条(條)直路通向远(遠)方。
    - Yī tiáo zhí lù tōng xiàng yuǎn fāng.
    - One straight road leads to the distance.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 一](@media/glyph4e00.png)
### 一生 → 生
- **definition:** life; birth; alive; grow
- **pinyin:** shēng
- **components:**
  - 屮
    - chè
    - sprout
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogrammic compound
  - **description:**
    - 屮 (chè, "sprout") on top of a horizontal line ->
    - signifies a plant sprouting from the ground ->
    - symbolizes life
  - **interpretation:** The character 生 (shēng, "life") represents the concept of life force or vitality, symbolized by a sprout emerging from the earth, embodying growth and renewal.
- **examples:**
  - 生命是一场(場)美丽(麗)的旅程。
    - Shēngmìng shì yī chǎng měilì de lǚchéng.
    - Life is a beautiful journey.
  - 他在战(戰)场(場)上奋(奮)力生存。
    - Tā zài zhànchǎng shàng fènlì shēngcún.
    - He fights to live on the battlefield.
  - 这(這)家餐厅(廳)的生鱼(魚)片非常新鲜(鮮)。
    - Zhè jiā cāntīng de shēngyúpiàn fēicháng xīnxiān.
    - The raw fish slices at this restaurant are very fresh.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 生](@media/glyph751f.png)
### 一生 → 生 → 屮
- **definition:** sprout
- **pinyin:** chè
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a sprout emerging from the ground
  - **interpretation:** 屮 (chè, 'sprout') is a pictogram that directly represents a young plant or sprout emerging from the ground. Its visual form captures the essence of new growth, and it historically served as an early representation of plant life or new vegetation.
- **examples:**
  - 春雨滋润(潤)后(後)，小屮冲(沖)破泥土而出。
    - chūn yǔ zī rùn hòu, xiǎo chè chōng pò ní tǔ ér chū.
    - After the spring rain nurtured the earth, the little sprout broke through the soil.
  - 草屮初生露尖端。
    - cǎo chè chū shēng lù jiān duān.
    - The grass sprout's tip has just emerged.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 屮](@media/glyph5c6e.png)

This visual imagery is straightforward and memorable, corresponding closely with its meaning of being at the center or middle of something.
- **examples:**

## 难(難)忘
---
## unforgettable; memorable
### nánwàng
---
- **traditional:** 難忘
- **definition:** unforgettable; memorable
- **pinyin:** nánwàng
- **components:**
  - 难(難)
    - nán
    - difficult
  - 忘
    - wàng
    - forget
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** compound word
  - **description:**
    - 難 (nán, "difficult") + 忘 (wàng, "forget") =
    - hard to forget ->
    - unforgettable
  - **interpretation:** The word 難忘 (nánwàng, "unforgettable") combines 難 (nán, "difficult") and 忘 (wàng, "forget") to describe something that leaves a strong impression, making it difficult to erase from memory.
- **examples:**
  - 这(這)次旅行非常难(難)忘。
    - Zhè cì lǚxíng fēicháng nánwàng.
    - This trip was unforgettable.
  - 他给(給)我留下了难(難)忘的印象。
    - Tā gěi wǒ liúxiàle nánwàng de yìnxiàng.
    - He left me with an unforgettable impression.
  - 毕(畢)业(業)典礼(禮)是一个(個)难(難)忘的时(時)刻。
    - Bìyè diǎnlǐ shì yīgè nánwàng de shíkè.
    - The graduation ceremony was a memorable moment.
### 难(難)忘 → 难(難)
- **traditional:** 難
- **definition:** difficult
- **pinyin:** nán
- **components:**
  - 隹
    - zhuī
    - bird
  - 暵
    - hàn
    - drought
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic 隹 (zhuī, 'bird') + phonetic 暵 (hàn) ->
    - originally depicted a type of bird ->
    - phonetically borrowed for 'difficult'
  - **interpretation:** The character 难(難) (nán, 'difficult') combines the semantic component 隹 (zhuī, 'bird') with the phonetic 暵 (hàn). It originally depicted a specific type of bird, but was phonetically borrowed to express 'difficult'. This phonetic borrowing extends the meaning beyond its literal components.
  - **simplification:** The traditional character 難 was simplified by eliminating the left component and retaining 又 (yòu, 'again').
- **examples:**
  - 这(這)道题(題)很难(難)。
    - Zhè dào tí hěn nán.
    - This question is very difficult.
  - 他觉(覺)得学(學)中文很难(難)，但是他会(會)努力。
    - Tā juéde xué Zhōngwén hěn nán, dànshì tā huì nǔlì.
    - He thinks learning Chinese is difficult, but he will try hard.
  - 解决(決)这(這)个(個)问(問)题(題)很难(難)，我们(們)需要更多时(時)间(間)。
    - Jiějué zhège wèntí hěn nán, wǒmen xūyào gèng duō shíjiān.
    - It's difficult to solve this problem, we need more time.
### 难(難)忘 → 难(難) → 隹
- **definition:** bird
- **pinyin:** zhuī
- **components:**
  - 鷕
    - yǎo
    - cry of a bird
  - 唯
    - wéi
    - only
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a short‐tailed bird (e.g., a sparrow) ->
    - also original form of 唯 (wéi, "only") before evolution into 鷕 (yǎo, "cry of a bird")
  - **interpretation:** 隹 (zhuī, "short-tailed bird") is a pictogram representing a bird with a short tail. Its depiction served as the foundation for other characters related to birds, such as 鷕 (yǎo, "cry of a bird").
- **examples:**
  - 这(這)只短尾的隹在树(樹)林中飞(飛)翔。
    - Zhè zhī duǎnwěi de zhuī zài shùlín zhōng fēixiáng.
    - This short-tailed bird flies in the forest.
  - 博物馆(館)里(裡)展出了一件以隹为(為)题(題)材的古代绘(繪)画(畫)。
    - Bówùguǎn lǐ zhǎnchūle yī jiàn yǐ zhuī wèi tícái de gǔdài huìhuà.
    - The museum displays an ancient painting themed on the short-tailed bird.
  - 远(遠)古诗(詩)篇中常用隹来(來)象征(徵)自由，寓意生动(動)。
    - Yuǎngǔ shīpiān zhōng cháng yòng zhuī lái xiàngzhēng zìyóu, yùyì shēngdòng.
    - In ancient poems, the short-tailed bird is often used to symbolize freedom, conveying vivid meaning.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 隹](@media/glyph96b9.png)
### 难(難)忘 → 难(難) → 隹 → 鷕
- **definition:** cry of a bird
- **pinyin:** yǎo
- **components:**
  - 唯
    - wéi
    - only
  - 鳥
    - niǎo
    - bird
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - 唯 (phonetic) + 鳥 (semantic, "bird") ->
    - cry of a bird
  - **interpretation:** The character combines 唯 (wéi, used phonetically for its sound) with 鳥 (niǎo, "bird") to denote the specific sound relating to a bird's cry.
### 难(難)忘 → 难(難) → 隹 → 鷕 → 唯
- **definition:** only
- **pinyin:** wéi
- **components:**
  - 口
    - kǒu
    - mouth
  - 隹
    - zhuī
    - short-tailed bird
  - 鷕
    - yǎo
    - cry of a bird
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic 口 (kǒu, "mouth") + phonetic 隹 (zhuī, "short-tailed bird") ->
    - original form of 鷕 ->
    - borrowed phonetically for 'only'
  - **interpretation:** The character 唯 originally represented the cry of a bird, with the mouth radical indicating the sound aspect. It was later phonetically borrowed for the abstract meaning 'only', without retaining its original context related to bird sounds.
- **examples:**
  - 唯有努力，才能成功。
    - Wéi yǒu nǔlì, cái néng chénggōng.
    - Only by working hard can one succeed.
  - 唯有在安静(靜)的夜晚，我才能听(聽)清自己的心声(聲)。
    - Wéi yǒu zài ānjìng de yèwǎn, wǒ cái néng tīng qīng zìjǐ de xīnshēng.
    - Only in the quiet of the night can I hear my own heart.
  - 我唯爱(愛)读(讀)书(書)，因为(為)书(書)籍能带(帶)给(給)我无(無)限的可能。
    - Wǒ wéi ài dúshū, yīnwèi shūjí néng dài gěi wǒ wúxiàn de kěnéng.

### 难(難)忘 → 难(難) → 隹 → 鷕 → 唯 → 口
- **definition:** mouth
- **pinyin:** kǒu
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts an open mouth.
  - **interpretation:** The character 口(kǒu, 'mouth') is a straightforward pictogram that visually represents an open mouth. It is a fundamental character in the Chinese language, often used both as an independent word and as a component in more complex characters, lending a semantic association to ideas relating to speech, openings, or enclosures.
- **examples:**
  - 他张(張)开(開)口，大声(聲)喊叫。
    - Tā zhāngkāi kǒu, dàshēng hǎnjiào.

    - Zhè kǒu fàn rùkǒu jíhuà.
    - This mouthful of food melts in your mouth.
  - 小女孩咬了一口苹(蘋)果，露出甜美的笑容。
    - Xiǎo nǚhái yǎole yī kǒu píngguǒ, lùchū tiánměi de xiàoróng.
    - The little girl took a bite of the apple and smiled sweetly.

  - **description:** Depicts a bird with a prominent beak and tail feathers
  - **interpretation:** The character 鳥 (niǎo, "bird") visually represents a bird, featuring distinct elements such as a beak and tail feathers, capturing its essence through its graphical form.

  - 花园(園)里(裡)有许(許)多鸟(鳥)，在空中翱翔。

    - Many birds soar in the garden.
  - 树(樹)林中有一只(隻)鸟(鳥)，在枝头(頭)跳跃(躍)。
    - Shùlín zhōng yǒu yī zhī niǎo, zài zhītóu tiàoyuè.
    - A bird hops on a branch in the forest.

### 难(難)忘 → 难(難) → 暵
- **definition:** drought
- **pinyin:** hàn
- **components:**
  - 日
    - rì
    - sun
  - 堇
    - jǐn
    - burnt earth
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:** 日 (rì, "sun") + 堇 (jǐn, phonetic element linked to heat and fire)
  - **interpretation:** The character 暵 (xiàn, "dry") combines the semantic component 日 (rì, "sun"), representing heat from the sun, with the phonetic component 堇 (jǐn), which suggests burning or heat. The combination evokes the sense of intense heat and dryness, as one might experience under a scorching sun.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 暵](@media/glyph66b5.png)
### 难(難)忘 → 难(難) → 暵 → 日
- **definition:** sun
- **pinyin:** rì
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts the sun; a dot or line added in the center to distinguish from similar characters e.g. 囗
  - **interpretation:** As a pictogram, 日(rì, 'sun') directly represents the sun. In ancient times, the added dot helped visually differentiate it from other characters. This is analogous to the astronomical symbol ☉ and Egyptian hieroglyph 𓇳, both depicting the sun.
- **examples:**
  - 晨曦来(來)临(臨)时(時)，日出东(東)方。
    - Chénxī láilín shí, rìchū dōngfāng.
    - At the break of dawn, the sun rises in the east.
  - 温(溫)暖的日光洒(灑)满(滿)大地。
    - Wēnnuǎn de rìguāng sǎ mǎn dàdì.
    - The warm sunlight spreads over the earth.
  - 中午时(時)分，日高挂(掛)天。
    - Zhōngwǔ shífēn, rì gāo guà tiān.
    - At noon, the sun hangs high in the sky.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 日](@media/glyph65e5.png)
### 难(難)忘 → 难(難) → 暵 → 堇
- **definition:** burnt earth
- **pinyin:** jǐn
- **components:**
  - 大
    - dà
    - big
  - 火
    - huǒ
    - fire
  - 廿
    - niàn
    - twenty
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogrammic compound
  - **description:**
    - 大 (person) + 火 (fire) + 廿 (open mouth screaming) =
    - a person being burned in a sacrificial ceremony ->
    - burnt earth
  - **interpretation:** The character 堇(jǐn, "burnt earth") combines the elements of a person 大(dà, "big") depicted as being part of a sacrifice, with 火(huǒ, "fire") representing a burning action. 廿(niàn, "twenty") is stylized here to depict an open mouth screaming, emphasizing the ritual aspect. The fire ritual thus conveys the idea of burnt earth used in sacrificial ceremonies, believed necessary for invoking rain or fertility in ancient practices.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 堇](@media/glyph5807.png)
### 难(難)忘 → 难(難) → 暵 → 堇 → 大
- **definition:** big
- **pinyin:** dà
- **components:**
  - 夫
    - fū
    - man
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a person facing forward ->
    - Borrowed phonetically for 'big'; original form of 夫 (fū, 'man')
  - **interpretation:** The character 大(dà) depicts a person facing forward, representing 'big' by suggesting the idea of someone standing prominently. Although often thought of as a person with outstretched arms, early scripts do not support this interpretation. It was originally the form of 夫 (fū, 'man') and was later phonetically borrowed for the meaning 'big.'
- **examples:**
  - 这(這)个(個)房子很大。
    - Zhè ge fángzi hěn dà.
    - This house is very big.
  - 大海波涛(濤)汹(洶)涌(湧)，展现(現)出大自然的力量。
    - Dàhǎi bōtāo xiōngyǒng, zhǎnxiàn chū dàzìrán de lìliàng.
    - The vast ocean waves surge, showcasing the power of nature.
  - 大人物登场(場)，留下传(傳)奇。
    - Dà rénwù dēngchǎng, liúxià chuánqí.
    - Great figures make an appearance, leaving behind legends.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 大](@media/glyph5927.png)
### 难(難)忘 → 难(難) → 暵 → 堇 → 大 → 夫
- **definition:** man
- **pinyin:** fū
- **components:**
  - 大
    - dà
    - big
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a variant form of 大 (dà, "big") representing an adult man with a hairpin ->
    - became associated with 夫 (fū, "man").
  - **interpretation:** 夫 (fū, "man") was visually similar to 大 (dà, "big") and was originally interchangeable. The addition of the horizontal stroke was interpreted as a hairpin, symbolizing adulthood for men.
- **examples:**
  - 此夫心怀(懷)大志。
    - Cǐ fū xīn huái dà zhì.
    - This man has lofty aspirations.
  - 他勤劳(勞)努力，堪称(稱)良夫。
    - Tā qín láo nǔ lì, kān chēng liáng fū.
    - He works diligently and is regarded as an exemplary man.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 夫](@media/glyph592b.png)
### 难(難)忘 → 难(難) → 暵 → 堇 → 火
- **definition:** fire
- **pinyin:** huǒ
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts flames rising from a fire
  - **interpretation:** The character 火 (huǒ, "fire") visually represents flames flickering upwards, which intuitively conveys the essence of fire. This simple depiction is an effective way to capture the dynamic and essential nature of fire.
- **examples:**
  - 火在壁炉(爐)中熊熊燃烧(燒)。
    - Huǒ zài bìlú zhōng xióngxióng ránshāo.
    - The fire burns fiercely in the fireplace.
  - 野外露营(營)时(時)，火能驱(驅)走寒冷。
    - Yěwài lùyíng shí, huǒ néng qūzǒu hánlěng.
    - When camping outdoors, the fire can drive away the cold.
  - 遇到火灾(災)时(時)，迅速疏散最为(為)重要。
    - Yù dào huǒzāi shí, xùnsù shū sàn zuìwéi zhòngyào.
    - In case of a fire, evacuating quickly is of utmost importance.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 火](@media/glyph706b.png)
### 难(難)忘 → 难(難) → 暵 → 堇 → 廿
- **definition:** twenty
- **pinyin:** niàn
- **components:**
  - 十
    - shí
    - ten
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts two 十 (shí, "ten") written side by side, with a horizontal stroke at the bottom that fuses them
  - **interpretation:** The character 廿 (niàn, "twenty") directly represents the number twenty by combining two tens ten (十) together and connecting them, illustrating the concept of two tens forming twenty.
- **examples:**
  - 我今年廿岁(歲)，准(準)备(備)考大学(學)。
    - Wǒ jīnnián niàn suì, zhǔnbèi kǎo dàxué.
    - I am twenty years old this year and I am preparing for college.
  - 放学(學)钟(鐘)响(響)时(時)，他收到廿个(個)红(紅)包。
    - Fàngxué zhōng xiǎng shí, tā shōudào niàn gè hóngbāo.
    - When the school bell rings, he receives twenty red envelopes.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 廿](@media/glyph5eff.png)
### 难(難)忘 → 难(難) → 暵 → 堇 → 廿 → 十
- **definition:** ten
- **pinyin:** shí
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Original vertical stroke ->
    - later horizontal stroke added ->
    - forms a cross ->
    - represents 'ten'
  - **interpretation:** The character 十(shí, 'ten') represents the number ten with a cross shape that could be seen as tally marks. It evolved from a simple vertical stroke to a cross by adding a horizontal stroke, symbolizing a complete set of ten.
- **examples:**
  - 我有十本书(書)。
    - Wǒ yǒu shí běn shū.
    - I have ten books.
  - 花园(園)里(裡)有十棵树(樹)，景色十分优(優)美。
    - Huāyuán lǐ yǒu shí kē shù, jǐngsè shífēn yōuměi.
    - There are ten trees in the garden, and the scenery is very beautiful.
  - 十年磨一剑(劍)。
    - Shí nián mó yī jiàn.
    - It takes ten years of practice to hone a sword.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 十](@media/glyph5341.png)
### 难(難)忘 → 忘
- **definition:** forget
- **pinyin:** wàng
- **components:**
  - 亡
    - wáng
    - lose
  - 心
    - xīn
    - heart
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - 亡 (wáng, "lose") as phonetic + 心 (xīn, "heart") as semantic =
    - to lose something in the heart ->
    - forget
  - **interpretation:** The character 忘(wàng, "forget") combines the phonetic element 亡 (wáng, "lose") with 心 (xīn, "heart"), indicating the concept of losing something from the heart, hence the idea of forgetting.
- **examples:**
  - 他总(總)是忘记(記)带(帶)钥(鑰)匙。
    - Tā zǒng shì wàngjì dài yàoshi.
    - He always forgets to bring the keys.
  - 请(請)不要忘记(記)你的承诺(諾)。
    - Qǐng bùyào wàngjì nǐ de chéngnuò.
    - Please don't forget your promise.
  - 有时(時)我会(會)忘记(記)时(時)间(間)，错(錯)过(過)重要的事情。
    - Yǒushí wǒ huì wàngjì shíjiān, cuòguò zhòngyào de shìqíng.
    - Sometimes I forget the time and miss important things.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 忘](@media/glyph5fd8.png)
### 难(難)忘 → 忘 → 亡
- **definition:** lose
- **pinyin:** wáng
- **components:**
  - 刀
    - dāo
    - knife
  - 芒
    - máng
    - edge of a knife
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogram
  - **description:**
    - A line on 刀 (dāo, 'knife') ->
    - cutting edge of a knife ->
    - original form of 芒 (máng, 'edge of a knife')
  - **interpretation:** The character depicts a line on a knife, representing the sharp edge. This connection to sharpness and cutting leads to the concept of 'perish,' as an edge can cut or end something, symbolically indicating destruction or the end of life.
- **examples:**
  - 战(戰)士们(們)在战(戰)场(場)上英勇战(戰)斗(鬥)，许(許)多人不幸亡。
    - Zhànshìmen zài zhànchǎng shàng yīngyǒng zhàndòu, xǔduō rén bùxìng wáng.
    - The soldiers fought bravely on the battlefield, and many unfortunately perished.
  - 如果不努力经(經)营(營)，这(這)家公司可能会(會)亡。
    - Rúguǒ bù nǔlì jīngyíng, zhè jiā gōngsī kěnéng huì wáng.
    - If the company does not operate diligently, it may perish.
  - 古代帝国(國)由于(於)内(內)外问(問)题(題)而一朝亡。
    - Gǔdài dìguó yóuyú nèiwài wèntí ér yī zhāo wáng.
    - The ancient empire perished overnight due to internal and external issues.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 亡](@media/glyph4ea1.png)
### 难(難)忘 → 忘 → 亡 → 刀
- **definition:** knife
- **pinyin:** dāo
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a knife
  - **interpretation:** 刀 (dāo, "knife") is a pictographic representation of a knife or blade, with a sharp edge and a handle, resembling the form of a basic cutting tool.
- **examples:**
  - 他用锋(鋒)利的刀，切开(開)蔬菜。
    - tā yòng fēnglì de dāo, qiē kāi shūcài.
    - He uses a sharp knife to cut vegetables.
  - 这(這)把刀非常锋(鋒)利。
    - zhè bǎ dāo fēicháng fēnglì.
    - This knife is very sharp.
  - 厨(廚)师(師)小心地持刀，为(為)客人切肉。
    - chúshī xiǎoxīn de chí dāo, wèi kèrén qiē ròu.
    - The chef holds the knife carefully and slices meat for the guest.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 刀](@media/glyph5200.png)
### 难(難)忘 → 忘 → 亡 → 芒
- **definition:** edge of a knife
- **pinyin:** máng
- **components:**
  - 艹
    - cǎo
    - grass
  - 亡
    - wáng
    - to flee
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic 艹 (cǎo, "grass") + phonetic 亡 (wáng) ->
    - edge of a knife
  - **interpretation:** The character 芒(máng, "edge of a knife") uses the 艹 (cǎo, "grass") component to highlight its relation to plant life or natural elements, while 亡 (wáng) provides the phonetic indication. Originally it may have depicted something like 方 but evolved to illustrate the thinness or sharpness of grass edges, metaphorically linking to the sharp edge of a knife.
- **examples:**
  - 刀的芒在阳(陽)光下闪(閃)闪(閃)发(發)光。
    - Dāo de máng zài yángguāng xià shǎnshǎn fāguāng.
    - The edge of the knife glistens in the sunlight.
  - 我们(們)要小心刀的芒，因为(為)它非常锋(鋒)利。
    - Wǒmen yào xiǎoxīn dāo de máng, yīnwèi tā fēicháng fēnglì.
    - We must be careful of the knife's edge because it is very sharp.
  - 他用手指轻(輕)轻(輕)触(觸)摸刀的芒，感受到它的锋(鋒)利。
    - Tā yòng shǒuzhǐ qīngqīng chùmō dāo de máng, gǎnshòudào tā de fēnglì.
    - He gently touched the blade's edge with his finger and felt its sharpness.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 芒](@media/glyph8292.png)
### 难(難)忘 → 忘 → 亡 → 芒 → 艹
- **definition:** grass
- **pinyin:** cǎo
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts blades of grass
  - **interpretation:** 艹 is a pictogram representing grass or plants, resembling blades of grass. It is commonly used as a radical in other characters related to grass or vegetation.
- **examples:**
  - 他写(寫)字时(時)用艹作草字的偏旁。
    - Tā xiězì shí yòng cǎo zuò cǎozì de piānpáng.
    - He uses '艹' as the radical for grass in his characters.
  - 春天到来(來)时(時)，艹生长(長)得很快。
    - Chūntiān dàolái shí, cǎo shēngzhǎng de hěn kuài.
    - When spring arrives, grass grows rapidly.
### 难(難)忘 → 忘 → 心
- **definition:** heart
- **pinyin:** xīn
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a heart
  - **interpretation:** The character 心(xīn, "heart") originally depicted the shape of an actual heart, representing thoughts, emotions, and the core of a person. Over time, it has become highly stylized, but it continues to convey the notion of the heart as the center of emotions and consciousness.
- **examples:**
  - 她的心一直都在帮(幫)助别(別)人。
    - Tā de xīn yīzhí dōu zài bāngzhù biérén.
    - Her heart is always in helping others.
  - 在城市的中心，有一个(個)美丽(麗)的公园(園)。
    - Zài chéngshì de zhōngxīn, yǒu yí gè měilì de gōngyuán.
    - At the center of the city, there is a beautiful park.
  - 对(對)于(於)许(許)多人来(來)说(說)，家庭是生活的核心。
    - Duìyú xǔduō rén lái shuō, jiātíng shì shēnghuó de héxīn.
    - For many people, family is the core of life.
- **historical forms:**

## 老年
---
## old age
### lǎonián
---
- **definition:** old age
- **pinyin:** lǎonián
- **components:**
  - 老
    - lǎo
    - old; venerable; experienced
  - 年
    - nián
    - year; age
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** compound word
  - **description:** 老 (lǎo, "old") refers to age or elderliness, and 年 (nián, "year") refers to the concept of time or age in years. Together, 老年 specifically denotes the period of life known as old age.
  - **interpretation:** 老 (lǎo, "old") indicates a stage in life characterized by experience and wisdom accumulated over time. 年 (nián, "year") brings in the temporal aspect, emphasizing the cumulative passage of years. Thus, 老年 represents the accumulation of years in life, focusing on the advanced age stage, often associated with retirement and reflection.
- **examples:**
  - 在老年，保持健康是非常重要的。
    - Zài lǎonián, bǎochí jiànkāng shì fēicháng zhòngyào de.
    - In old age, maintaining health is very important.
  - 他的老年生活很幸福。
    - Tā de lǎonián shēnghuó hěn xìngfú.
    - His old age is very happy.
  - 人们(們)常常在老年时(時)回忆(憶)过(過)去。
    - Rénmen chángcháng zài lǎonián shí huíyì guòqù.
    - People often recall the past in old age.
### 老年 → 老
- **definition:** old; venerable; experienced
- **pinyin:** lǎo
- **components:**
  - 人
    - rén
    - man
  - 毛
    - máo
    - hair
  - 匕
    - bǐ
    - cane
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogrammic compound
  - **description:**
    - 人 (rén, "man") + 毛 (máo, "hair") + 匕 (bǐ, "cane") =
    - a man with long hair leaning on a cane ->
    - old man
  - **interpretation:** The character 老(lǎo) visually depicts aspects associated with age: a man with long hair and a cane. This combination intuitively suggests the concept of being elderly.
- **examples:**
  - 他虽(雖)然年老，但经(經)验(驗)丰(豐)富。
    - tā suīrán niánlǎo, dàn jīngyàn fēngfù.
    - He may be old, but he is experienced.
  - 他是我们(們)班的老老师(師)。
    - tā shì wǒmen bān de lǎo lǎoshī.
    - He is our class's venerable teacher.
  - 老故事传(傳)递(遞)智慧。
    - lǎo gùshi chuándì zhìhuì.
    - Old stories convey wisdom.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 老](@media/glyph8001.png)
### 老年 → 老 → 人
- **definition:** man
- **pinyin:** rén
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts side view of a standing man, highlighting an arm and a leg ->
    - visual representation of a person
  - **interpretation:** The character 人 (rén, 'person') effectively uses simple lines to depict the essential form of a human, making it immediately recognizable and intuitive as meaning 'person.'
- **examples:**
  - 他是个(個)好人。
    - Tā shì gè hǎo rén.
    - He is a good person.
  - 每个(個)人都有责(責)任，为(為)社会(會)作出贡(貢)献(獻)。
    - Měi gè rén dōu yǒu zérèn, wèi shèhuì zuòchū gòngxiàn.
    - Every person has a responsibility to contribute to society.
  - 人在旅途中，心灵(靈)获(獲)得了成长(長)。
    - Rén zài lǚtú zhōng, xīnlíng huòdé le chéngzhǎng.
    - People gain growth along their journey.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 人](@media/glyph4eba.png)
### 老年 → 老 → 毛
- **definition:** hair
- **pinyin:** máo
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a feather or hair
  - **interpretation:** The character 毛(máo, "hair") visually represents either a feather or the strands of hair, capturing the texture and common features of these natural elements.
- **examples:**
  - 他的头(頭)上有许(許)多白色的毛。
    - Tā de tóu shàng yǒu xǔduō báisè de máo.
    - There are many white hairs on his head.
  - 猫(貓)的毛很柔软(軟)。
    - Māo de máo hěn róuruǎn.
    - The cat's hair is very soft.
  - 这(這)条(條)围(圍)巾是用羊毛制(製)成的。
    - Zhè tiáo wéijīn shì yòng yángmáo zhìchéng de.
    - This scarf is made of wool.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 毛](@media/glyph6bdb.png)
### 老年 → 老 → 匕
- **definition:** cane
- **pinyin:** bǐ
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a spoon
  - **interpretation:** The character 匕(bǐ, 'cane') originally depicts a spoon, which has a similar shape to the character itself. It is unrelated to the meanings of 'walking cane', 'knife', or 'person', which appear in other characters with similar forms.
- **examples:**
  - 古时(時)候的老人常用匕支撑(撐)。
    - Gǔ shíhòu de lǎorén cháng yòng bǐ zhīchēng.
    - In ancient times, elders often used a cane for support.
  - 他拄着(著)匕，在公园(園)里(裏)散步。
    - Tā zhǔ zhe bǐ, zài gōngyuán lǐ sànbù.
    - He walked in the park with a cane.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 匕](@media/glyph5315.png)
### 老年 → 年
- **definition:** year; age
- **pinyin:** nián
- **components:**
  - 禾
    - hé
    - grain
  - 人
    - rén
    - person
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - 禾(“wheat; grain”) + 人(“person”) as phonetic ->
    - originally “harvest” ->
    - later “year”
  - **interpretation:** The character 年 (nián, "year") originally depicted a harvest of grains, linking the concept of agricultural cycles with the passing of a year. Over time, the form evolved, retaining the semantic component 禾 (hé, "grain") and using 人 (rén, "person") for its phonetic sound in early stages, which later transformed into the current form through script evolution.
- **examples:**
  - 今年是兔年。
    - Jīnnián shì tùnián.
    - This year is the Year of the Rabbit.
  - 他今年二十岁(歲)。
    - Tā jīnnián èrshí suì.
    - He is twenty years old this year.
  - 五年后(後)我希望能去旅行。
    - Wǔ nián hòu wǒ xīwàng néng qù lǚxíng.
    - I hope to travel in five years.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 年](@media/glyph5e74.png)
### 老年 → 年 → 禾
- **definition:** grain
- **pinyin:** hé
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a stalk of grain or cereal plant
  - **interpretation:** The character 禾 (hé, 'grain') visually represents a plant with roots and leaves, focusing on the appearance of staple crops like rice or millet. This clearly conveys its meaning as it resembles the actual shape of a plant grown for its grain.
- **examples:**
  - 收获(穫)的禾香弥(彌)漫在田野中。
    - Shōuhuò de hé xiāng mímàn zài tiányě zhōng.
    - The fragrance of grain filled the fields.
  - 农(農)民辛勤耕作，收割禾穗。
    - Nóngmín xīnqín gēngzuò, shōugē hé suì.
    - The hardworking farmers harvested the ears of grain.
  - 春雨滋润(潤)了禾苗，预(預)示着(著)丰(豐)收。
    - Chūnyǔ zīrùn le hé miáo, yùshì zhe fēngshōu.
    - The spring rain nourished the grain seedlings, foreshadowing a bountiful harvest.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 禾](@media/glyph79be.png)
### 老年 → 年 → 人
- **definition:** person
- **pinyin:** rén
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts side view of a standing man, highlighting an arm and a leg ->
    - visual representation of a person
  - **interpretation:** The character 人 (rén, 'person') effectively uses simple lines to depict the essential form of a human, making it immediately recognizable and intuitive as meaning 'person.'
- **examples:**
  - 他是个(個)好人。
    - Tā shì gè hǎo rén.
    - He is a good person.
  - 每个(個)人都有责(責)任，为(為)社会(會)作出贡(貢)献(獻)。
    - Měi gè rén dōu yǒu zérèn, wèi shèhuì zuòchū gòngxiàn.
    - Every person has a responsibility to contribute to society.
  - 人在旅途中，心灵(靈)获(獲)得了成长(長)。
    - Rén zài lǚtú zhōng, xīnlíng huòdé le chéngzhǎng.
    - People gain growth along their journey.
- **historical forms:**

## old age
